। atha tṛtīyaḥ pādaḥ ।
।
tatra cānyatra ca prasiddhānāṃ śabdānāṃ viṣṇau samanvayaṃ prāyeṇāsmin pāde darśayati । viṣṇoḥ paravidyāviṣayatvamuktam ।
etatpādapratipādyaṃ darśayati tatreti । anyonyasamuccaye caśabdau । devatādhikaraṇāpaśūdrādhikaraṇayoḥ samanvayākaraṇāttadvyāvṛttyarthaṃ aprāyeṇa'; prācuryeṇeti । tathā ca prāyeṇāsmin tṛtīye pāde atatra'; harau tasmāt aanyatra'; rudraprakṛtyādau ca śrutiliṅgādibhiḥ prasiddhānāṃ nāmaliṅgātmakaśabdānāṃ viṣṇau asamanvayaṃ'; paramamukhyayā vṛttyā tātparyaprabalahetubhiḥ adarśayati'; pratipādayati sūtrakṛdityarthaḥ । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyamudāhṛtya viṣayasaṃśayasayuktikapūrvapakṣān darśayati viṣṇoriti ।

tatra ayasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī cāntarikṣamotaṃ manaḥ saha prāṇaiśca sarvaiḥ tamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānam'; ityatra ।
aprāṇānāṃ granthirasi rudro mā'viśāntakaḥ'; 
aprāṇeśvaraḥ kṛttivāsāḥ pinākī'; ityādinā rudrasya
prāṇādhāratvapratīteḥ ।
asa eṣo antaraścarate bahudhā jāyamānaḥ'; 
iti jīvaliṅgācca tayoḥ prāptiriti ।
uktamityāvartate । tatretyavyayaṃ tadityarthe api । atretyapyāvartate । ādiśabda ubhayānvayī । rudrasyeti śeṣe ṣaṣṭī । tayorityetat pradhānavāyvorapyupalakṣakam । tathā ca adṛśyatvādiguṇakākṣarasya viṣṇoḥ paravidyāviṣayatvaṃ yatroktaṃ tatraivātharvaṇe tatparavidyāviṣayatvaṃ
yasmin dyauḥ pṛthivī cāntarikṣamotaṃ manaḥ saha prāṇaiśca sarvaiḥ ।
tamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānamanyā vāco vimuñcatha । 
aamṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ'; ityatra iti vākye tatra dyubhvādyāśraye uktamityekā yojanā । tatra dyubhvādyāyatanatve atayoḥ'; rudrajīvayoḥ prāptiḥ । kutaḥ? atravākye dyubhvādyāyatane prāṇādhāratvapratīteḥ śravaṇāt । tathā sa eṣa iti jīvaliṅgaśravaṇācca । na ca prāṇādhāratvaśravaṇe api kuto atra rudrasya prāptiriti vācyam । aprāṇānāṃ granthirasi rudromāviśāntakastenānnenāpyāyasva'; iti taittirīyavākyena, tathā 
yo brahmā brahmaṇa ujjabhāra prāṇeśvaraḥ kṛttivāsāḥ pinākīr ।
iśāno devassa na āyurdadhātu 
ityādikhilasaṃhitāvākyena ca rudrasya prāṇādhāratvapratīteḥ ityaparā yojanā । yadvā asminneva pakṣe tayorityetatsaptamyantamāśritya liṅgaliṅgirūpadharmadvayaparatayā vyākhyeyam । tathātve ādiśabdo arudro vāva lokādhāraḥ'; iti vākyagrāhī । evaṃ tatra tayoḥ prāptiriti dūrānvayena atatra'; paravidyāviṣayatve tayo rudrajīvayoḥ prāptirityanyā yojanā । tatra ādyayojanāyāṃ dyubhvādyāyatanatvasya viṣṇvanyatvākṣepamukhena atamevam'; ityādinā aamṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ'; iti vākyaśeṣabalātpratītasya mokṣajanakajñānajanakavidyāviṣayatvarūpasya tattvapradīparītyānanyayogena prādhānyena jñeyatvarūpasya vā paravidyāviṣayatvasya pūrvoktasya viṣṇoritaratvākṣepāt adṛśyatvādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tathā dyubhvādyāyatanatvarūpo viṣayaḥ darśitaḥ । dvividhadvitīyayojanāyāṃ sayuktikapūrvapakṣo darśitaḥ । tṛtīyāyāṃ tu pūrvapakṣaphalaṃ darśitamiti draṣṭavyam । ayasmin'; paramātmani dvyādilokāḥ amanaḥ'; tadabhimānī asarvaiḥ prāṇaiḥ'; indriyaistadabhimānibhiśca saha ataṃ'; praviṣṭaṃ paramātmānam aekaṃ'; pradhānaṃ ajānatha'; jānīdhvam iti śrutyarthaḥ ।
rudra u mā āviśa iti padacchedaḥ । u ityavyayaṃ sambuddhidyotako nipātaḥ । mā ityavyayaṃ, nāsmadādeśaḥ māśabdaḥ । yadvā metyanenāsmadādeśo māśabdaścetyubhau tantreṇopāttau । sa ca niṣedhārthaḥ । tathā ca he rudra tvaṃ aprāṇānām'; indriyāṇāṃ grathyate asminniti agranthiḥ'; āśrayaḥ aantakaḥ'; saṃhartā cāsi । sa tvaṃ amā'; mām aāviśa'; praviśa mayi sannidhiṃ kurvityarthaḥ । yadvā he rudra antakastvaṃ māṃ mā praviśetyarthaḥ । atena'; āhutirūpeṇa dattena aannena'; mām aāpyāyasva'; sukhaya ।
yo abrahmaṇe'; caturmukhāya abrahma'; vedān aujjabhāra'; ujjahāra, sa aprāṇeśvaraḥ'; indriyeśaḥ akṛttivāsāḥ'; kṛttiścarma vasanaṃ yasyāsau, apinākīr'; iśāno na āyuḥ adadhātu'; puṣṇātviti śrutyantarārthaḥ । siddhānte tu rudrādiśabdāḥ viṣṇuparāḥ । ya eṣa jīvo abahudhā'; bahuśarīreṇotpadyamānaḥ śarīrāntaḥsañcārītyātharvaṇaśrutyarthaḥ ।

ata ucyate 
sū oṃ
dyubhvādyāyatanaṃ svaśabdāt ।
oṃ ।
atamevaikaṃ jānatha ātmānam'; ityātmaśabdāt
dyubhvādyāśrayo viṣṇureva ।
ātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāstamṛte viṣṇumavyayam ।
na sambhavanti yasmātternaivāptā guṇapūrṇatā ।
iti brahmavaivarte ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe ata iti । sautrasvaśabdasya svaśabdaparyāyātmaśabdāditi viṣṇutattvanirṇayokteḥ, svetiśabdaḥ svaśabda iti vyutpattyā svaśabdaparyāyātmaśabdagrāhitvaṃ viṣṇoḥ svarūpasyaiva sākṣādvācako hyayamātmaśabda iti tattvapradīpokteḥ, svasya viṣṇoreva vācakaḥ śabdaḥ svaśabda iti vigrahāśrayeṇa ca ātmaśabdaparāmarśitvamāśritya svaśabdādityetadātmaśabdāditi vyākhyātam । tathā ca aityātmaśabdāt'; ityatrātmaśabdaśravaṇādityarthaḥ । dyubhvādyāśraya ityanenāyatanaśabdo vyākhyātaḥ । kvacidāyatanaśabdasyaiva pāṭhaḥ । viṣṇurevetyanena samanvayasūtrānuvṛttaṃ tattvityetat śrutyanusārālliṅgavipariṇāmena vyākhyātam । anena asvaśabdāt'; viṣṇuvācisvaśabdaparyāyātmaśabdāt svaśabdāt adyubhvādyāyatanaṃ'; svargabhūmyādisarvāśrayaḥ atattu'; viṣṇureveti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।
ātmāśabdādapi kuto ayaṃ viṣṇurityata āha ātmeti । yasmāt ataiḥ'; viṣṇoritaraiścaturmukhādijīvaiḥ guṇapūrṇatā anaivāptā'; na sarvathā prāptā । tasmādātmabrahmādayaḥ śabdāḥ aavyayaṃ'; nityaniratiśayapravṛttinimittavantaṃ viṣṇum aṛte'; vinā tadanyaṃ ana sambhavanti'; na mukhyato vācakatvena prāpnuvantītyarthaḥ । anenātmaśabdasyāpi guṇapūrtirartha ityuktaṃ bhavati । brahmavaivarta ityanantaramanyatra niravakāśatayoktāditi śeṣaḥ । tasyātmaśabdādityanenānvayaḥ।

sū oṃ ।
muktopasṛpyavyapadeśāt ।
oṃ ।
aamṛtasyaiṣa setuḥ'; iti ।
nanu viṣṇau mukhyo apyātmaśabdo jāyamānatvarūpajīvaliṅgabalādamukhyārthaḥ kiṃ na syāt । tathā ca na tato viṣṇordyubhvādyāyatanatvanirṇaya ityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya tadupāttaśrutimevādāharati mukteti ।। iti muktāprāpyatvavyapadeśādityanvayaḥ । sūtre dyubhvādyāyatanasyeti vipariṇāmena anuvartanīyam । muktopasṛpyeti bhāvanirdeśaḥ। upasṛpyatvaṃ ceha śrautasetuśabdabalātprāpyāntararahitatve sati prāpyatvaṃ vivakṣitam । nanvarcirādivatprāpyatvamātram । tathā ca dyubhvādyāyatanasya aamṛtasya'; iti muktopasṛpyatvokterviṣṇutvaniścayānnātmaśabdasyāmukhyārthatvamāśritya viṣṇoranyat dyubhvādyāyatanaṃ kalpyamiti । amuktānām'; iti smaraṇādamṛtasyeti jātāvekavacanam । tathā ca aamṛtasya'; muktajātasya aeṣaḥ'; paramātmā asetuḥ'; seturiva seturmukhyāśraya ityarthaḥ ।

brahmavidāpnoti param । anārāyaṇaṃ mahājñeyaṃ viśvātmānaṃ
parāyaṇam'; amuktānāṃ paramā gatiḥ';
aetamānandamayamātmānamupasaṅkrāmati'; ityādinā
tasyaiva muktāprāpyatvavyapadeśāt ।
bahunātra kimuktena yāvacchvetaṃ na gacchati ।
yogī tāvanna muktassyādeṣa śāstravinirṇayaḥ ।
ityādityapurāṇe ।
nanu dyubhvādyāyatanasya muktaprāpyatvaṃ kutaḥ viṣṇutvaniścāyakamityāśaṅkāparihārakatayāpi sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe brahmaviditi । aityādinā'; vākyena atasya'; viṣṇoḥ evetyanena prāpyatvaṃ prāpyāntararahitatve sati prāptatvam । anena dyubhvādyāyatanasya muktopasṛpyatvavyapadeśāttasya viṣṇoreva muktopasṛtapyatvavyapadeśādityāvṛttyā sūtraṃ vyākhyātam। pradhānasūtre anuvṛttaṃ tattvityetadiha vipariṇāmena anuvartanīyamiti sūcitam । upasṛpyapadaṃ bhāvapradhānaṃ kṛtvā vyākhyātam। evakāro liṅgasyānyaniṣṭhatvavyavacchedakaḥ । abrahmavit'; viṣṇujñānī muktassan aparaṃ'; viṣṇumāpnotīti taittirīyaśrutyarthaḥ । anārāyaṇam'; iti taittirīyopaniṣadi mahopaniṣadi ca śrutam । atra atadviśvamupajīvati'; ityanuvartate । tathā ca atadviśvaṃ'; jagat mahanīyaṃ jñeyaṃ, pūjyajñeyaṃ vā । viśvasvāminaṃ aparāyaṇaṃ'; muktānāmāśrayamupajīvatīti śrutyarthaḥ। amuktānāṃ paramā gatiḥ'; iti sahasranāmagatamekaṃ nāma । paramā mukhyā gamyata iti gatirāśrayaḥ । aetam'; iti taittirīyavākyamānandamayanaye vyākṛtam । ādipadena aetamānandamayamātmānamupasaṅkramya'; aparamaṃ yaḥ parāyaṇam'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate ।
nanūdāhṛtavākyairastu viṣṇoḥ muktaprāpyatvaṃ, tathāpyatrānyavyavacchedābhāvādviṣṇuvadanyasya muktaprāpyatvaṃ kiṃ na syāditi liṅgasya sāvakāśatvamāśaṅkya anyatra prāpyatvamātrasambhave api niruktopasṛpyatvaṃ sautramuktaśabditavivakṣitamuktyupetajīvaprāpyatvaṃ vānyatra niravakāśamiti pramāṇenāha bahuneti । aatra'; prāpyamokṣatatsādhanaviṣaye abahunoktena'; idamidaṃ ceti pratyekaṃ bahunā vacanena akiṃ prayojanaṃ'; na kimapi, pratyutoktigauravameveti bhāvaḥ । tarhi kathaṃ nirṇaya ityata āha yāvacchvetamiti । aśvetaṃ'; śvetadvīpākhyaṃ viṣṇusthānaṃ ayāvanna gacchati'; na prāpnoti, tatratyaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca na paśyati atāvadyogī'; aparokṣajñānākhyopāyavān mukto na syāt । bhagavadicchārūpāvaraṇānmuktaḥ samyagāvirbhūtajñānānandādimān na bhavediti aeṣaḥ'; upadeśaḥ aśāstravinirṇayaḥ'; śāstratattvaviṣayakanirṇayasādhanamityarthaḥ । eṣor'thaḥ aśāstravinirṇayaḥ'; tajjanyanirṇayaviṣaya iti vā । bhāvabodhe tu sūtre purāṇe ca muktapadena liṅgabhaṅgavān vivakṣita ityuktam । atra śvetadvīpāganturamuktatvoktyā śvetadvīpaṃ prāptasyaiva muktatvaṃ jñāyate । tathā ca tatsthitasya viṣṇorevetaravyavacchedena muktaprāpyatvaṃ siddhamiti bhāvaḥ । ityādityapurāṇe ityasya tasyaiva muktaprāpyatvavyapadeśādityanenānvayaḥ । anena tasyaivetyevakārasyopayogo jñāpito bhavati । asya hetorna liṅgasya sāvakāśatvaṃ śaṅkyamityadhyāhṛtasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

sū oṃ
। nānumānamatacchabdāt ।
nānumānam atacchabdāt ।
oṃ ।
nānumānātmakāgamaparikalpitarudro atra vācyaḥ ।
nanu prāguktarītyā rudraprakṛtyordyubhvāyatanatvaṃ kiṃ na syādityatastatsādhakābhāvānna tayostadityāha sūtrakṛt nānumānamiti । atra nānumānamiti sādhyāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe nānumānātmaketi । aanumānaprāptaprāmāṇyāsadāgamo anumātmakaḥ'; iti tattvapradīpokteḥ anumānātmake anumānasiddhaprāmāṇyake pāśupatādyāgame sarvāśrayatvena kalpito bodhita ityarthaḥ । kecittu pramāṇatvena anumīyata ityanumānamiti vyācikhyuḥ । etatpakṣe ātmakaśabdavaiyarthyaṃ, tattvapradīpaṭīke viruddhe । rudrapadaṃ pradhānāderupalakṣakam । pradhānasūtrādanuvṛttena dyubhvādyāyatanapadenopasthāpitaṃ nañarthapratiyoginaṃ darśayati atreti । dyubhvādyāyatanaprakaraṇa ityarthaḥ । avācyaḥ'; pratipādyaḥ । sarvāśrayatveneti śeṣaḥ ।

bhasmadharogratvāditacchabdābhāvāt ।
evaṃ sūtre pratijñāṃśaṃ vyākhyāya hetvaṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe bhasmadhareti । tasya rudrasya śabdastacchabdaḥ । tacchrutiliṅgātmakaḥ । tathā ca bhasmadharogratvādidharmaviśiṣṭadharmibodhakabhasmadharogrādiśabdābhāvādityarthaḥ । atha vā akimucyate bhasmadharogratvādīnāṃ tacchabdatvam'; ityuttaraṭīkābalādbhāvabhavitrorabhedavivakṣayā svārthe tvapratyayaḥ । tatprayogastu liṅgātmakaśabdasyāpi saṅgrahāya । bhāvabodhe tu bhasmadharetyanena rudravācakanāmātmakaśabdo gṛhyate । ugratvapadena ugratvarūpaliṅgātmakaśabdo gṛhyate । ādipadena nāmaliṅgātmakaśabdāntarāṇi gṛhyante । samākhyāderupalakṣakametat । tathā ca bhasmadharādirudraśrutīnām ugratvādirūpatalliṅgānāṃ rudraprāpakasamākhyādīnāṃ cābhāvādityartha ityuktam । atra rudraśivāditacchabdābhāvādityanuktvā bhasmadharogratvādīti vacanaṃ arudro bhasmadharo nagnaḥ'; iti vacanādviśeṣanāmābhiprāyeṇa । ata evaitadvacanoktāḥ nagnādiśabdā evādipadena grāhyā iti dhyeyam । bhasmadharetyetatpradhānatriguṇatvādirūpaprakṛtiprāpakaśrutiliṅgādyabhāvādityarthāntaropalakṣakatayāpi vyākhyeyam । yadyapi atacchabdādityasya tacchabdābhāvāditi vyākhyāne nañaḥ kriyāsāpekṣatvenāsamarthatvātsamāsānupapattiḥ । tathāpi nirmakṣikamityādāviva aarthābhāve yadavyayam'; ityavyayībhāvasamāsāśrayaṇānnānupapattiḥ । pañcamītvāt nātrām bhavati । anena sūtre jagatkartṛtvenānumīyate ityanumānaśabdena vā aānumānamanumānasambandhi'; iti sattarkadīpāvalyukterānumānamiti padacchedenānumānaśabdena vā anumānasiddhaprāmāṇyakapāśupatādyāgamasiddhaṃ rudrapradhānādhikaṃ gṛhyate । yadvā pramāṇatvenānumīyata ityanumānaṃ pāśupatādyāgamaḥ । tato matvarthe arśa ādibhyo ac, tena tatpratipādyamucyate । evamānumānamiti padacchede apyaṇantātpunaraṇ kāryaḥ । tatra prathamāṇantarapadenāgama ucyate । dvitīyena pratipādyatvam । tathā ca anumānātmakapāśupatādyāgamapratipādyaṃ rudrādikaṃ na dyubhvādyāyatanaṃ na ayasmin'; ityādiprakaraṇe sarvāśrayatvena pratipādyaṃ, kutaḥ? aatacchabdāt'; rudrapradhānādisādhakaśrutiliṅgādyabhāvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

aso antakaḥ sa rudraḥ sa prāṇabhṛtsa prāṇanāyakaḥ sar iśo yo hariryo ananto yo viṣṇuryaḥ parovarīyān'; ityādinā prāṇagranthirudratvāderviṣṇorevoktatvāt ।
nanvātharvaṇe rudrādijñāpakābhāve api atroktaprāṇādhāratvapratipādikāyāṃ aprāṇānāṃ granthirasi rudra'; ityādisamākhyāśrutau rudrādiśabdānām antakatvādiliṅgānāṃ coktatvāttadbalāttatroktaṃ dyubhvādyātanatvaṃ rudrādeḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha sa iti । yo antakassaṃhartā sa eva tacchabdavācyaḥ śrutaḥ sa viṣṇureva । yo rudraḥ śrutaḥ so api viṣṇureva । yaḥ aprāṇabhṛt'; prāṇādhāratvabodhakaprāṇagranthiśabdavācyaḥ, so api viṣṇureva । yaḥ aprāṇanāyakaḥ'; tatsvāmī tata eva prāṇeśa śabditaḥ so api viṣṇureva । yar iśaḥ śrutaḥ so api viṣṇureva । yo anantastacchabdavācyaḥ so api trividhaparicchedaśūnyatvādviṣṇureva, na śeṣaḥ । yaḥ parovarīyān so api rudrādeḥ parato vāṇyādeḥ parādviriñcāt parataḥ prakṛteḥ paratvāddharireva nānya iti śrutyarthaḥ ।
atrāntarādhikaraṇodāhṛtacaturvedaśikhāvākye ca aparasmāduttamaṃ proktam'; iti vacanānusāreṇa paraparataravaravaratamānāṃ caturṇāṃ pratyāyanāya vṛttivākye subādeśasya sorutvotvaguṇasamānaśabdalopā jñātavyāḥ । pratyuddeśyaṃ vidheyānvayajñāpanāya bahūnāṃ yattadāṃ prayogaḥ । aityādinā'; śrutyantaravākyena aprāṇagranthirudratvādeḥ'; prāṇagranthitvaliṅgasya rudraśabdavācyatvasya ca tasyaiva viṣṇorevoktatvādityarthaḥ । prāṇeśvarādiśabdavācyatvamantakatvādiliṅgaṃ cādiśabdārthaḥ । prakṛtiśrutiliṅgāderapyupalakṣakametat । na tu rudrāderityevakārārthaḥ । evakāreṇānyatrāmukhyatassattvamanumanyate । uktatvādityasya ana rudrādiśrutiliṅgavirodhaḥ'; ityadhyāhṛtasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

brahmāṇḍe ca 
rujaṃ drāvayate yasmādrudrastasmājjanārdanarḥ ।
iśānādeva ceśāno mahādevo mahattvataḥ ।
pibanti ye narā nākaṃ muktāssaṃsārasāgarāt ।
tadādhāro yato viṣṇuḥ pinākīti tataḥ smṛtaḥ ।
śivaḥ sukhātmakatvena śarvaḥ śaṃrodhanāddhariḥ ।
kṛtyātmakamimaṃ dehaṃ yato vaste pravartayan ।
kṛttivāsāstato devo viriñcaśca virecanāt ।
bṛṃhaṇādbrahmanāmāsāvaiśvaryādindra ucyate ।
nanu tathāpi na prāṇādhāratvadyubhvādyāyatanatvabodhakasamākhyāśrutau viṣṇoḥ pratipādyatvaniścayaḥ । tatratyānāṃ rudrādiśabdānāṃ paśupatyādāveva rūḍhatvena viṣṇau tadabhāvāt, bhāve vā punaraniścayāt । viṣṇau yogavṛttisambhave api tasyā rūḍhito durbalatvenāniścāyakatvāt । na hi śrutyantare viṣṇuliṅgādyastītyata āha brahmāṇḍe ceti । co apyarthaḥ samuccaye । uktatvādityanuvartate । tenāsyānvayaḥ । kimuktamityato rudrādiśabdānāṃ mahāyogavidvadrūḍhipratipādakaṃ vākyaṃ paṭhati rujamiti । arujaṃ'; rogam utpattyādikaṃ adrāvayate'; nirvāpayati nivartayati yasmāttasmādrudra ityucyate । ka ityata stadrūpaviśeṣamāha janārdana iti । jananamardayatīti vyutpattirḥ । aiśanārt iśānāṃ'; brahmādīnāṃ ceṣṭakatvādīśāno api sa evetyarthaḥ । mahattvata ityupalakṣaṇam । dyotanādeścetyapi draṣṭavyam । ye anarāḥ'; janāḥ saṃsārasāgarānmuktāḥ santo anākaṃ'; paramasukhaṃ apibanti'; bhuñjate te pinākāḥ । viṣṇuryataḥ atadādhāraḥ'; teṣāmādhārastataḥ pinākīti asmṛtaḥ'; abhihitaḥ śrutāviti śeṣaḥ । śruta iti pāṭhaḥ svarasaḥ । aśaṃrodhanāt'; muktiparyantaṃ svarūpabhūtamapi sukhaṃ rudhvā vartanāt āsurasakhaṃ nirudhya vartanādvā śarva ityarthaḥ । yataḥ akṛtyātmakaṃ'; carmamayamimaṃ dehaṃ apravartayan'; sṛjan niyamayan vā tena svātmānaṃ jīvaṃ vā avaste'; ācchādayati tadantarvartate । yadvā dehaṃ vaste adhivasatītyataḥ kṛttivāsā ityucyata ityarthaḥ । avirecanāt'; jagatsarjanādasau viṣṇuḥ bṛṃhaṇādvardhanādvā brahmanāmā । asau paramaiśvaryādindra ityucyate ।

evaṃ nānāvidhaiśśabdaiḥ eka eva trivikramaḥ ।
vedeṣu sapurāṇeṣu gīyate puruṣottamaḥ ।
evaṃ viṣṇau rudrādiśabdānāṃ mahāyogamuktvā vidvadrūḍhiṃ cāha evamiti ।
nimittairityadhyāhāryam । tathā ca aevam'; uktarītyā nānāvidhairnimitaiḥ sapurāṇeṣu vedeṣu gataiḥ etairnānāvidhaiḥ śabdairviṣṇureka eva agīyate'; mukhyato abhidhīyata ityarthaḥ । kathamanyatrādṛṣṭaṃ sarvaśabdamukhyavācyatvamasyetyataḥ apuruṣottamastrivikramaḥ'; ityābhyāṃ tatropapādakamuktam । tribhuvanārthaśabdavyāpī hi trivikramaḥ । sarvapuruṣaśabdanimittakasvāmī hi puruṣottamaḥ । tathā cānena viṣṇau rudrādiśabdānāṃ mahāyogavidvadrūḍhikathanāt tayośta rūḍhimātrātprābalyādyuktaḥ samākhyāśrutyantare api viṣṇoḥ pratipādyatvaniścaya iti bhāvaḥ । apuruṣottama iti'; ityantasya abrahmāṇḍe'; iti pūrveṇānvayaḥ ।

vāmane ca 
na tu nārāyaṇādīnāṃ nāmnāmanyatra sambhavaḥ।
anyanāmnāṃ gatirviṣṇuḥ eka eva prakīrtitaḥ ।
nanu yadi rudrādiśabdānāṃ viṣṇuparatvamuktvā arudro mā'viśāntakaḥ'; ityādiśrutīnāmanirṇāyakatvamucyate, tarhi nārāyaṇādināmnāṃ rudrādiparatvena anārāyaṇaṃ mahājñeyam'; ityādiśrutīnāmanirṇāyakatvaṃ ca syādityata āha vāmane ceti । asyāpyuktatvādavirodhaiti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । kimuktamityatastadvākyaṃ paṭhati na tviti । turavadhāraṇe । anārāyaṇādīnāṃ'; nārāyaṇa ityādīnamanyatra rudrādau sambhavo mukhyavṛttiḥ astīti śeṣaḥ । aanyanāmnāṃ'; rudrādiśabdānāṃ aviṣṇureka eva gatiḥ'; mukhyavācyaḥ prakīrtita ityarthaḥ । itiśabdasya vāmana ityanenānvayaḥ । tasya nārāyaṇādināmnāṃ anyatra niravakāśatvokteḥ na tacchrutīnāmanirṇāyakatvamiti vivakṣitasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

skānde ca 
ṛte nārāyaṇādīni nāmāni puruṣottamaḥ ।
prādādanyatra bhagavān rājevarte svakaṃ puram ।
bhagavannāmatvāviśeṣādrudrādināmavannārāyaṇādināmnāmapi rudrādau vṛttiḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha skānde ceti । co apyarthaḥ samuccaye । asyāpyuktatvāditi pūrveṇānvayaḥ । kimuktamityatastadvākyaṃ paṭhati ṛta iti ।
vinetyarthaḥ । aanyatra'; anyebhyo rudrādibhyaḥ anyāni rudrādināmānītiśeṣaḥ । ādiśabdena viṣṇurityādikaṃ gṛhyate। atra dṛṣṭāntamāha rājeti ।। yathā rājā svakaṃ puramṛte anyadamātyādibhyo dadāti tadvadityarthaḥ । itītyantasya skānde ityanenānvayaḥ । tasya ca nārāyaṇādināmnāmanyatra vṛttyabhāvasyoktatvānna sāmyamityupaskṛtenānvayaḥ । anena skānde nārāyaṇādināmnāṃ viṣṇorevoktatvānna sāmyamityanvayena pūrvaprayuktaivakārasya kṛtyāntaraṃ sūcitaṃ bhavati ।

caturmukhaśśatānando brahmaṇaḥ padmabhūriti ।
ugro bhasmadharo nagnaḥ kapālīti śivasya ca ।
viśeṣanāmāni dadau svakīyānyapi keśavaḥ ।
iti ca brāhme ।
yadyevaṃ rudrādiśabdāḥ viṣṇvaikaparāḥ tarhi kimucyate bhasmadharogratvādīnāṃ tacchabdatvam । viṣṇudattatvābhiprāyeṇa cet tarhi rudrādiśabdā api tādṛśā iti kathaṃ tairnirṇayābhāva ityata āha caturmukha iti ।। yadyapi svakīyāni, tathāpi akeśavaḥ'; brahmarudrapravartako viṣṇuḥ asvakīyāni'; mukhyataḥ svavācakānyeva caturmukhaḥ śatānandaḥ padmabhūriti aviśeṣanāmāni'; nāmaviśeṣāneva abrahmaṇo'; brahmaṇe dadāvityarthaḥ । anagnaḥ'; digambaraḥ । castvarthaḥ । brāhma ityasyāpyuktatvāditi pūrveṇānvayaḥ । rudrādau bhasmadharogratvādereva viṣṇossakāśātprāptatveneti tadarthaḥ । tasya ca pūrvoktaṃ yuktamiti sādhyenānvayaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
prāṇabhṛc ca ।
oṃ ।
etaireva hetubhirna jīvo vāyuśca ।
nanu asa eṣo antaścarate bahudhā jāyamānaḥ'; iti jīvaliṅgaśravaṇātprāṇitvaprasiddheśca jīvasāmānyasya vā, viṣayabhūtalokādhāratvasya avāyunā vai gautama sūtreṇāyaṃ lokaḥ paraśca lokaḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni saṃdṛbdhāni bhavanti'; iti śrutyantare vāyuniṣṭhatvena prasiddhatvādvāyorvātra prakaraṇe dyubhvādyāśrayatvena pratipādyatā kiṃ na syādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe prāṇabhṛcceti । ātmaśabdaḥ muktopasṛpyatvamatacchabdo rudrādiprāpakaśrutīnāṃ viṣṇuparatvamityevaṃrūpaiḥ pūrvoktahetubhirityarthaḥ । nātra hetvantaraṃ vācyamityevaśabdārthaḥ । jīvo vāyurityanena prāṇabhṛcchabdo vyākhyātaḥ । atra vācya ityanuṣajyate । caḥ samuccaye । anena sūtre caśabdaḥ prāguktahetūnāṃ nānumānamityato nañaśca samākarṣakaḥ । na kevalaṃ rudro atra na vācyaḥ, kintu jīvo vāyuśceti samuccayārthaścetyuktaṃ bhavati ।

aajāyamāno bahudhā vijāyate'; 
iti tasyaiva bahudhā janmokteḥ ।
nanu avāyunā vai gautama'; ityādiśruterviṣṇuparatvena vāyusādhakatvābhāve api bahudhā janmākhyaliṅgena jīvo atra vācyaḥ kiṃ na syādityata āha ajāyamāna iti । dehataḥ aajāyamānaḥ'; avikurvāṇo abahudhā'; rāmakṛṣṇādirūpeṇa avijāyate'; tatra tatra prādurbhavatītyarthaḥ । iti puruṣasūktagatavākyenetyarthaḥ । yasya janmāsambhavo abhihitaḥ pūrvavādinā tasyaiva viṣmorna jīvasyetyevaśabdārthaḥ । tathā ca liṅgaṃ sāvakāśamiti na tadvirodha iti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
bhedavyapadeśāt ।
।
na caikyaṃ vācyam । ajuṣṭaṃ yadā paśyatyanyamīśamasya mahimānam'; iti bhedavyapadeśāt ।।
nanu kiṃ jīvaliṅgasya viṣṇugatatvapratipādanāyāsena, liṅgabalājjīvasyaiva dyubhvādyāyatanatvaṃ syāt । na coktātmaśabdādihetuvirodhaḥ । jīveśābhedābhiprāyeṇa jīve apyātmaśabdādyuktisambhavādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe bhedeti । jīveśvarayoratrābhipretamiti ca śeṣaḥ । anena sūtre nānumānamityato nañanuvartanīyaḥ । sa ca hetugatabhedapratiyoginā saṃyojya ityuktaṃ bhavati । caśabdo jīveśaikyaprayuktātmaśabdavācyataitatprakaraṇabodhyatāpi netisamuccayārthaḥ । kau'sau vyapadeśa ityata āha juṣṭamiti । iti bhedavyapadeśāditi । iti bhedaśruterityarthaḥ । anena ajuṣṭam'; iti vākye apaśyati'; iti darśanakartṛtvena prakṛtajīvasyar iśapadokteścar iśvarādbhedokteḥ na tayoraikyamatrābhipretamiti vācyamiti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । śrutistavānandamayanaye vyākṛtā ।

sū oṃ ।
prakaraṇāt ।
।
adve vidye veditavye'; 
iti tasya hyetatprakaraṇam ।
nanvatra jīvasya kasmāccidīśādanyatvamucyate, na paramātmanaḥ, ato na tayorbheda ityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe prakaraṇāditi । itītyanantaram aityupakramyādhītam'; iti śeṣaḥ । ahi'; yataḥ aetat'; juṣṭamityādivākyajātaṃ yataḥ atasyaiva'; paravidyāviṣayasya paramātmana eva aprakaraṇaṃ'; nānyasyetyevaśabdārthaḥ । anena svaprakaraṇāt adve vidye veditavye'; iti paravidyāviṣayavastuno atrādhītatvena viṣṇuprakaraṇatvātparamātmana eva bhedavyapadeśāvagateḥ na jīvaparamātnorabhedo atrābhipreta iti vācyamiti sūtrayojanā darśitā bhavati ।

sū oṃ ।
sthityadanābhyāṃ ca ।
।
dvāsuparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānaṃ bṛkṣaṃ pariṣasvajāte ।
tayoranyaḥ pippalaṃ svādvattyanaśnannanyo abhicākaśīti । 
itir iśajīvayoḥ sthityadanokteḥ ।
। iti dyubhvādhiprakaṇam । ।
na kevalaṃ ajuṣṭam'; iti bhedaśruterna jīveśabhedo atra prakaraṇe vivakṣita iti jñāyate, kintu liṅgādapītyāha sūtrakṛt sthitīti । tadasiddhivāraṇāya śrutyudāharaṇena vyācaṣṭe dvā suparṇeti । anena advā suparṇā'; ityatra śrutābhyāḥ karmaphalānupajīvanāvasthititadupajīvanābhyāṃ hetubhyāṃ ca naivātra jīveśayoraikyaṃ vācyamiti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । caśabdastu hetusamuccāyaka iti spaṣṭatvānna vyākhyātaḥ । śrutāvadanasya prāthamye api sthiterīśasambandhitvenābhyarhitatvādalpākṣaratvācca sūtre tadanusāreṇa bhāṣye ca śrautakramamullaṅghya sthiteḥ prathamamuktiḥ । asayujā'; sayujau saṃyuktau upakāryopakārakabhāvavattayā parasparāparihāreṇa vartamānau asakhāyā'; sakhāyau prītyā ekadeśasthau advā'; dvau asuparṇā'; suparṇau । suparṇasarūpau । asuparṇā sakhāyā'; iti viśeṣaṇasvārasyādasya samajīvamātraviṣayatve suṣṭhuparamānandarūpau jīveśvarau asamānam'; ekaṃ avṛkṣaṃ'; dehākhyam aśvatthaṃ apariṣasvajāteḥ'; āliliṅgatuḥ । atayoḥ'; suparṇayormadhyer iśvarāt aanyo'; jīvaḥ apippalam'; aśvatthaphalarūpaṃ dehajanitakarmaphalam aatti'; asvādveva svādutvenaiva aśnāti । jīvāt aanyarḥ'; iśvarastu aanaśnan'; jīvādyamevābhuñjānaḥ aabhi'; abhitaḥ acākaśīti'; prakāśate । na tu svasthityai jīvavatkarmaphalamapekṣata iti muṇḍakaśrutyarthaḥ ।।
। iti dyubhvādhikaraṇam । ।

।
aprāṇo vā āśayā bhūyān'; ityuktvā ayo vai bhūmā tatsukham';
ityuktestasyaiva bhūmatvaprāptiḥ ।
atrādhikaraṇe bhūmanāmno viṣṇau samanvayaḥ pratipādyate । bhūmaśabdaśca abhūmnaḥ kratuvat'; ityādau kvaciddharmavācako apyatra pūrṇarūpadharmivacanaḥ । pūrṇatvaṃ ca guṇata uttamatvamiti dhyeyam । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayan sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ darśayati prāṇa iti ।। achāndogye'; ityādau upaskāryam । aityuktvā'; ityupakrametyupalakṣaṇam । taduttamamanuktvetyapi draṣṭavyam । ata eva tasyaiva prāṇasyaivetyevakāro anyavyavacchedakaḥ prāyoji । śrutau pūrvapakṣe prāṇaśabdo vāyumātraparaḥ । siddhānte tu bhāṣyarītyā vāyuviṣṇūbhayaparaḥ । nyāyavivaraṇachāndogyabhāṣyarītyā tu vāyumātraparaḥ । na ca vāyuviṣṇūbhayavācitvaṃ vāyumātravācitvamityarthadvayaṃ viruddham । antaryāmivivakṣayā bhāṣyasya tadavivakṣayā vivaraṇādeḥ pravṛttatvāt । yathā aātmanaḥ ākāśaḥ'; ityatra sambhūtaśabdasyānekārthatve antaryāmiviṣṇurapyākāśapadenocyate । tasya janimātrārthatve tu na tena sa ucyate । tathā tattvapradīpe tu aabhyupagamavādatvāt'; ityādinā ayaṃ prāṇo viṣṇurityabhyupetya vādena bhāṣyaṃ pravṛttam, ityuktam । tathā cādyapakṣe prāṇaḥ aāśāyāḥ'; bhāratyāḥ abhūyān'; guṇato jyeṣṭhaḥ । evaṃ aprāṇaḥ'; tadantaryāmī viṣṇurantaryāmitvādeva tata āśāyāśca bhūyānityarthaḥ । anena pūrvamānandamayaśabdoktasajātīyotkṛṣṭatvarūpapūrṇatvasyeha vāyāvākṣepādānandamayādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ sūcitā । chāndogaśrutyukto bhūmākhyo viṣayaḥ, kiṃ vāyuruta viṣṇuriti sandehaśca sūcitaḥ । tathā tasyaiva bhūmatvaprāptiriti pūrvapakṣaḥ । tatra prāṇopakramataduttamānuktirūpayuktiśca darśitā bhavati । ayo vai bhūmā tatsukhaṃ nālpe sukhamasti bhūmaiva sukham'; iti vākye sukhaśabdaḥ pūrṇasukhārthaḥ । ayatsukhaṃ sa bhūmā'; iti vyāsatīrthīyokteḥ, sarvanāmāni paryāyeṇa tattalliṅgabhāñjītyukteśca nirupapadasukhaśabdamātrasyāpi pūrṇasukhārthatvāt । yadananyādhīnapūrṇānandasukhaṃ sa bhūmā guṇataḥ pūrṇo nārāyaṇa ityuddeśyavidheyayorvyatyayaḥ । ata eva svātantryeṇa sukhasya viśeṣaṇāt na muktajīveṣvanaikāntyamityāśayena tadupapādayati nālpa iti । aalpe'; apūrṇe muktajīve tatprasādaṃ vinā yataḥ sukhaṃ nāstītyarthaḥ । nigamayati bhūmaiva sukhamiti ।

autkrāntaprāṇān'; ityāditalliṅgatprāṇaśabdaśca vāyuvācīti ।
nanu aprāṇo vā āśāyā bhūyān'; ityuktaprāṇaśabdasya aata eva prāṇaḥ'; ityuktarītyā viṣṇuparatvādviṣṇoreva bhūmatvaprāpteḥ kathaṃ prāṇaśabdabalādvāyorbhūmatvaprāptirityata āha utkrānteti । luptavibhaktiko nirdeśaḥ । ādiśabdena autkrāntaprāṇān śūlena samāsaṃ vyatiṣaṃ dahet nainaṃ brūyuḥ pitṛhāsīti'; samagravākyaṃ gṛhyate । tacca tat liṅgaṃ ca, tasya liṅgamiti ca vigrahaḥ । caśabdo avadhāraṇe । vāyuvācī ceti bhinnakramaḥ । tathā ca aayaṃ'; prāṇaśabdo avāyuvācyeva'; na viṣṇuvācī । kutaḥ? autkrāntaprāṇān'; ityādau atalliṅgāt'; tasya prāṇasyotkramaṇādirūpaliṅgaśravaṇāditi yojanā । utkrāntaḥ prāṇo yebhyaste tathoktāḥ । tānmātṛpitrācāryādīn asamāsaṃ'; sākalyena avyatiṣam'; ekadeśena ca śūlena viluṇṭhya yadi dahetputraḥ śiṣyo vā tathā nainaṃ brūyuḥ janāḥ । kimiti? pitṛhāsīti mātṛhāsīti । mukhyaprāṇasannidhānābhāvāditi bhāvaḥ । iti śrutyarthaḥ ।

ato vakti 
sū oṃ ।
bhūmā saṃprasādādadhyupadeśāt ।
।
asamprasādāt'; pūrṇasukharūpatvāt aadhyupadeśāt';
sarveṣāmuparyupadeśācca viṣṇureva bhūmā ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati ata iti । sūtre prasīdatyanena jana iti prasādaḥ sukham, samyakprasādaḥ samprasādaḥ, tasmāditi vigraharḥ । iśvare sukhamiva duḥkhamapi syāditi nāśaṅkyaṃ, pūrṇasukhakāryeṇa samyakprasādena duḥkhābhāvaniścayādityāśayena prayuktaṃ samprasādāditi hetumanūdya vyācaṣṭe samprasādāditi । uttarasūtrasthacaśabdo atrākarṣaṇīya ityāśayena aadhyupadeśāt'; ityetaddhetvantaraparatayānūdya vyākhyāti adhyupadeśāditi । nāmādīnāṃ sarveṣām aupari'; taduttamatvena aupadeśāt'; ukterityarthaḥ । atrādhītyeva hetuḥ, na tu samagra eko hetuḥ । sa ceśvaravacano bhāvapradhānaḥ, viśeṣānukteḥ akhileśvaratvāditi hetvarthaḥ akhileśatvādityanuvyākhyānasudhokto jñātavyaḥ । asiddhiparihārāyopadeśaparyantaṃ dhāvanam । prāyapāṭhādbhūmno akhilādhipaprāṇādhipatye akhilādhipatyaṃ siddhyatīti bhāvaḥ । samanvayasūtrādanuvṛttasya tattvitividheyasamarpakasyārthamāha viṣṇureveti bhūmā viṣṇurevetyanvayaḥ।

asahasraśīrṣaṃ devaṃ viśvākṣaṃ viśvaśambhuvam ।
viśvaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ devamakṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam ।
viśvataḥ paramāṃ nityam'; iti hi śrutiḥ ।
pūrṇasukhatvādikaṃ kuto viṣṇutvaniścāyakamityata āha sahasreti । ahi'; yasmāt aiti'; nārāyaṇānuvākagatā śrutirasti, tasmātsamprasādāt viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatyevetyarthaḥ । asahasraśīrṣaṃ'; sahasrapadopalakṣitāmitamūrdhānaṃ adevaṃ'; prakāśarūpaṃ viśvato darśanādakṣyasyeti viśvākṣaṃ aviśvaśambhuvaṃ'; pūrṇasukhāśrayaṃ aviśvaṃ'; jagatpraviṣṭatvena vartamānaṃ anārāyaṇaṃ'; muktasaṅghe vyaktam aakṣaraṃ'; svarūpato nāśarahitam akṣeṣu ramamāṇaṃ vā । parebhyo brahmādibhyo adhikatvena mīyata iti parā mā yasyeti vā paramastaṃ paramaṃ apadaṃ'; prāpyaṃ viśvataḥ paramaścāsāvaśceti vigrahaḥ, savarṇadīrghaḥ । somapāśabdavadayaṃ śabdaḥ । sudhārītyā ābantatvāśrayeṇa liṅgavyatyayo vā । tathā ca aviśvataḥparamāṃ'; sarvasmāduttamam akāravācyaṃ sarvottamaṃ vā anityaṃ'; dehato nāśarahitaṃ aviśvaṃ'; guṇaiḥ pūrṇaṃ yajñeṣu haviḥsvīkaraṇāt harivarṇatvācca ahariṃ'; adevaṃ'; krīḍādiguṇakaṃ anārāyaṇaṃ'; tadākhyaṃ devaṃ tadviśvamupajīvatīti śrutyarthaḥ । yadyapi viśvataḥ paramam iti drāviḍapāṭhaḥ । tathāpyāndhrapāṭhamanusṛtya paramāmityuktam ।

atamutkrāmantaṃ prāṇo anūtkrāmati'; 
ityādinā notkramaṇādiliṅgavirodho api ।
atra prāṇaśabdena viṣṇorvācyatvāṅgīkāre prāguktatkramaṇādiliṅgavirodha ityato netyāha tamiti । prathamādiśabdena taduttaravākyāni dvitīyena talliṅgāntarāṇi ca gṛhyante । apiśabdaḥ samuccaye, yadyapi tathāpītyarthe ca । tathā ca na kevalaṃ prāṇaśabdopakramavirodhaḥ, tasya viṣṇuparatvāt, kintu aapi'; atra prāṇaśabdena viṣṇorvācyatvāṅgīkāre utkramaṇādiliṅgavirodho nāsti । kutaḥ? aapi'; tathāpi sarvagate api viṣṇāvutkramaṇādiliṅgasya atamutkrāmantam'; ityādinā vājasaneyavākyena siddhatvāditi yojanā । śrutisiddher'the lokadṛṣṭivirodho akiñcitkara iti bhāvaḥ । atasya haitasya hṛdayasyāgraṃ pradyotate । tena pradyotenaiṣa ātmā niṣkrāmati'; iti pūrvavākye prakṛtaḥ paramātmā tacchabdena parāmṛśyate । tathā ca pradyotitahṛdayāgreṇāparokṣajñānidehāt autkrāmantaṃ'; nirgacchantaṃ paramātmānamanusṛtya aprāṇo'; mukhyavāyuḥ autkrāmati'; dehānnirgacchatīti śrutyarthaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
dharmopapatteś ca ।
।
sarvagatatvādidharmopapatteśca ।
। iti bhūmādhikaraṇam । ।
yuktyantareṇa viṣṇorbhūmatvapratipādakaṃ sūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe dharmeti । ādipadena svātantryasvapratiṣṭhitvādikaṃ gṛhyate । asya hetorviṣṇureva bhūmeti pradhānasādhyenānvayaḥ । yadyapi chāndogye ayatra nānyat'; iti svātantryabodhakavākyānantaraṃ asa evādhastāt'; iti sarvagatatvābhidhāyakavākyaśravaṇāt prathamaśrutasvātantryadharmaṃ svaśabdena gṛhītvā sarvagatatvāmādiśabdena grāhyam । tathāpi tadvākye bhūmatvaniyatasarvagatatvasya spaṣṭaṃ pratītestadeva vācakaśabdena gṛhītamiti draṣṭavyam । anena sūtre co yuktisamuccaye dharmaśabdātparamanveti । liṅgasya niravakāśatvajñāpanāyopapattiparyantaṃ dhāvanam । tathā ca na kevalaṃ samprasādādeḥ, kintu asa evādhastātsa upariṣṭātsa paścātsa purastātsa dakṣiṇataḥ sa uttarataḥ sa evedaṃ sarvam'; iti vākye, tathā ayatra nānyatpaśyati nānyacchṛṇoti nānyadvijānāti sa bhūmā'; iti vākye, tathā asa bhagavaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti sve mahimni'; ityādi vākye ca sarvagatatvādidharmaśravaṇācca bhūmā viṣṇureva, teṣāṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ viṣṇāvevopapatteriti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । asaḥ'; bhūmaśabdito nārāyaṇaḥ adhaḥ upari paścātpurastāddakṣiṇata uttarataḥ sarvatrāsti । tatprayojanamāha sa evedaṃ sarvamiti । tenaivedaṃ jagadvyāptaṃ sa eva sarvasattāpradastadarthameva sarvatra tiṣṭhatītyarthaḥ । ayatra'; yadvinā yadadhīnaṃ vinā anyannapaśyatyadhikārī sarvameva tadadhīnaṃ paśyati, tathaiva śṛṇoti, vijānāti ca sa bhūmetyarthaḥ । ayatra'; yasmin dṛṣṭe anyatsvatantraṃ na paśyatīti vā । he abhagavo'; bhagavān sa bhūmā kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti nāradapraśne mahimaguṇātmake asve'; svasmin svakīye mahimni vā svayaṃ apratiṣṭhitaḥ'; āśrita iti sanatkumāraḥ pratyāheti śrutyarthaḥ । ।
। iti bhūmādhikaraṇam । ।

।
adṛśyatvādiguṇā viṣṇoruktāḥ । aadṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭraśrutaṃ
śrotṛ'; ityādinā । aahaṃ somamāhanasaṃ
bibharmi'; ityādestasyāpi
sambhavānmadhyamākṣarasyoktā iti ।
atrādhikaraṇe akṣaranāmasamanvayaḥ kriyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyamudāhṛtya viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayan sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ ca darśayati adṛśyatvādīti ।। te iti śeṣaḥ । ādyādiśabdenāgrāhyatvādi gṛhyate । guṇā ityanena candrādityādyādhāratvaguṇo api gṛhyate । dvitīyādiśabdena aaśrutaṃ śrotramataṃ mantravijñātaṃ vijñātṛnānyadato asti draṣṭṛ nānyadato asti śrotṛ nānyadato asti mantṛ nānyadato asti vijñātṛ etasmin khalvakṣare gārgyākāśa otaśca protaśca'; iti śiṣṭavākyam, tathā aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ'; iti vākyaṃ ca gṛhyate । tṛtīyādiśabdena aahaṃ tvaṣṭāramuta pūṣaṇaṃ bhagam'; iti vākyam, tathā ye tvakṣaramanirdeśyamavyaktaṃ paryupāsate ।
sarvatragamacintyaṃ ca kūṭasthamacalaṃ dhruvam । 
iti gītāvākyam ।
āsīdidaṃ tamobhūtamaprajñātamalakṣaṇam ।
apratarkyamavijñeyaṃ prasuptamiva sarvataḥ ।
iti tadbhāṣyodāhṛtavākyaṃ ca gṛhyate । caśabdenākṣaraśabdasya śrītattve prasiddheśceti akṣarapadasūcito hetuḥ samuccīyate । tasyetipadamāvartate, vipariṇamyate ca । na kevalaṃ viṣṇoreva, kintu atasya'; akṣarasyāpītyaperarthaḥ । viṣṇujaḍavyāvṛttyarthaṃ madhyameti । abhūmatvaprāptiḥ'; iti pūrvapākyādbuddhyā vivekena prāptiritipadamatrānuvartate । tathā ca pūrvamadṛśyatvādhikaraṇe ye adṛśyatvādiguṇā akṣarasya viṣṇoruktāḥ । te vājasaneyake atadvā etadakṣaraṃ gārgi adṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭṛ'; ityādinā vākyena amadhyamākṣarasya'; śrītattvasya auktāḥ'; ucyante ityekā yojanā । aparā tu atasya'; teṣāmadṛśyatvādiguṇānāṃ atasya'; tasmin madhyamākṣare api sambhavādyuktatvāt atasya'; candrādyādhāratvaliṅgasyāpi aahaṃ somamāhanasam'; ityādivākyāttasminnakṣare upapatteḥ atasya'; akṣaraśabdasya tasmin madhyamākṣare prasiddheśca atasya'; madhyamākṣarasyāpi atasya'; akṣaranāmavācyatvasya prāptiriti । tatrādyayojanāyām adṛśyatvādhikaraṇoktādṛśyatvādiguṇakākṣarasya viṣṇvanyatvākṣepāttenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tathākṣarākhyo viṣayaḥ, draṣṭṛtvābhidhāyakottaravākyaparyālocanayā jaḍavyāvṛtteḥ । kiṃ cetanaprakṛtirutaviṣṇuriti saṃśayaśca sūcitaḥ । dvitīyayojanāyāṃ sayuktikaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ pradarśita iti jñātavyam । atadvā'; ityādeḥ siddhāntarītyāyamarthaḥ atat'; ākāśāśrayatvena vakṣyamāṇam aakṣaraṃ'; na kṣaratītyakṣaraśabdavācyaṃ brahma aetat'; etallakṣaṇakaṃ ca prasiddham । tadevāha adṛṣṭamityādinā । anyaiḥ sākalyena adṛṣṭatvātsvayaṃ draṣṭṛtvādadṛṣṭaṃ draṣṭrityucyate । evamuttaravākyamapi vyākhyeyam । draṣṭṛtvādau viśeṣamāha neti । aataḥ'; akṣarādanyat svātantryeṇa draṣṭṛ śrotṛ mantṛ jñātṛ ca nāstītyarthaḥ । aetasmin'; evaṃbhūte akṣaraśabdite brahmaṇi dīptinimittākāśapadoktaṃ śrītattvam aotaśca protaśca'; atrotaṃ ca protaṃ ca । tathā ca sarvakāreṇa tadāśritaṃ khalvityarthaḥ ।
gārgīti yājñavalkyakartṛkapatnīsambodhanam । aetasya vā akṣarasya'; viṣṇoḥ apraśāsane'; ājñāyāmiti nimittasaptamī । tathā ca ājñāmātrāt asūryācandramasau'; akeśau sūryavidhū matau'; iti bṛhadbhāṣyokterbrahmarudrau bhāṣyaṭīkārītyā prasiddharavicandrau ca avidhṛtau'; viśeṣeṇa dhṛtau bhavata iti । pūrvapakṣī tu akṣaraśabdaṃ śrītattvaparaṃ manyate । tatpakṣe ākāśaśabdaḥ prakṛtyanyatatpoṣyaparaḥ ।
aham aāhanasaṃ'; svābhimanyamānalatādvārā yajñeṣvabhiṣūyamāṇaṃ asomaṃ'; somalatābhimāninaṃ candraṃ tvaṣṭāraṃ ca auta pūṣaṇaṃ'; pūṣaṇaṃ ca bhagaṃ ca abibharmi'; dadhāmītyaṃbhraṇīvākyasyārthaḥ । tvaṣṭrādayastu sūryaprabhedāḥ । tattvapradīpasattarkadīpāvalyostu bṛhadbhāṣyānusāreṇa asomam'; umayā sahitam aāhanasam'; āsamantāt hantāraṃ saṃhartāraṃ rudraṃ bibharmīti vyākhyātam ।
aakṣaraṃ'; dehato apyavināśi, aanirdeśyaṃ'; śabdāgocaraṃ, asarvatragaṃ'; deśato vyāptam, aacintyaṃ'; manasāgrāhyaṃ, guṇabāhulyāt, kūṭe ākāśe abhimānitvena tiṣṭhatīti akūṭastham', aacalaṃ'; kadāpi svapadādabhraṣṭaṃ adhruvam'; utpattivināśaśūnyam, aavyaktaṃ'; śrītattvaṃ ye paryupāsate iti gītārthaḥ ।
pralaye aabhūtam'; ajātam aaprajñātaṃ'; pratyakṣāvedyam avedyalakṣaṇatvādalakṣaṇam ata eva aatarkyam'; anumānāvedyam aavijñeyam'; āgamāvedyam anādyavidyābhimānitvāt, tamaḥśabdavācyamidaṃ lakṣmyākhyaṃ tattvaṃ aprasuptamiva'; nirvyāpāraṃ asarvataḥ'; sarvatrāsīditi smṛtyarthaḥ ।

ato brūte 
sū oṃ ।
akṣaramambarāntadhṛteḥ ।
।
aetasmin khalvakṣare gārgyākāśa otaśca protaśca';
ityambarāntasya sarvasya dhṛterbrahmaivākṣaram ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārayati ata iti । sūtre gahanārthatvātprathamaṃ hetubhāgaṃ vyākariṣyamāṇo asiddhiparihārāya śrutimudāharati etasminniti । itītyanantaraṃ avākye'; iti śeṣaḥ । anyapadārthaṃ darśayanvigrahaṃ darśayati ambareti । ambaramākāśaḥ anto yasya sarvasya pṛthivyāderdhārakatvokterityarthaḥ । yadyapi aetasmin'; iti vākye ambaradhṛtirevocyate । na tu tadantarasarvadhṛtiḥ । tathāpi ayadūrdhvaṃ gārgi divo yadarvākpṛthivyā yadantarā dyāvāpṛthivī ākāśa eva tadotaṃ ca protaṃ ca'; ityanenākāśasya citprakṛteḥ sarvādhāratvamuktvānantaram aetasmin'; iti vākye akṣarasya tādṛśaprakṛtyādhāratvokteḥ prakṛtidvārākṣarasyāmbarāntasarvādhāratvamatroktameveti na doṣaḥ । etacca sūtre ambarāntetyantapadaprayogātsūcitam । sūtre tattvityanuvṛttapadadvayopetapratijñābhāgaṃ vyākhyāti brahmaiveti । akṣaraṃ brahmaivetyanvayaḥ । anena akṣarasya aetasmin'; iti prakṛtidvārā'kāśāntasarvādhāratvaśruterakṣaraṃ brahmaiveti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

ya u tridhātu pṛthivīmuta dyā meko dādhāra bhavanāni viśvā । 
sarvādhāratvaṃ kuto viṣṇutvaniścāyakamityataḥ tasya viṣṇuliṅgatvena śrutisiddhatvādityāha ya iti । vyākhyāteyaṃ śrutirjanmanaye ।

bhartā sanbhriyamāṇo bibharti ।
eko devo bahudhā niviṣṭaḥ ।
yadā bhāraṃ tandrayate sa bhartum ।
parāsya bhāraṃ punarastameti । 
abhartā san'; iti taittirīyāṇāṃ śrutiḥ । adevaḥ'; prāṇākhyo bhagavān svayaṃ jagatā jīvena vā hṛdi bhriyamāṇaḥ tat abibharti'; dhatte puṣṇāti ca । tarhi jagadīśayoḥ sāmyāpattirityata āha bhartā sanniti । jagato mūlabhartā sanneva bhriyamāṇaḥ, na svakīyasthityetyarthaḥ । nanvekasyaiva bhagavataḥ bhartā bhriyamāṇo bibhartītyanekavidhavyavahāraviṣayatvaṃ kathamityata āha eko bahudheti । eko api bhartṛtvādinā abahudhā'; bahurūpeṇa ca aniviṣṭo'; vyāpta ityarthaḥ । tatra praviṣṭa iti vā । ayadā bhāraṃ tandrayate sa bhartuṃ parāsya bhāraṃ punarastameti'; iti vākyaśeṣaḥ । asa'; viṣṇuryadā taṃ jagadbhāraṃ aparāsya'; adho nidhāya punarbhartuṃ atandrayate'; necchati tadā asau bhāraḥ aastameti'; naśyatītyarthaḥ ।

yasminnidaṃ saṃcavicaidhi sarvaṃ
yasmin devā adhi viśve niṣeduḥ । 
ityādiśruteḥ ।
ayasmin'; ityapi taittirīye anyadvākyam । atra yacchabdasya atadeva brahma paramam'; ityuttaravākyasthatacchabdenānvayaḥ । cau prakārasamuccaye । tathā ca ayasminnidaṃ'; sarvaṃ jagat asaṃ'; samyak avi'; vividhaṃ acaidhi'; avardhata । edhaterliṅi chāndasaṃ rūpametat । yadvā edhivardhate । astīti vārthaḥ । asmin pakṣe asterlaṭi madhyamapuruṣaikavacane chāndasaṃ rūpam । vastuto loṭi madhyamapuruṣaikavacane rūpametat । yasmiṃśca aviśve'; sarve devāḥ aadhiniṣeduḥ'; yamadhyagustadeva brahmetyarthaḥ । ityādiśruterityasya ambarāntadhṛterityanenānvayaḥ । brahmaṇyavagatāyā iti śeṣaḥ । tṛtīyārthe pañcamī । ādiśabdena ayenāvṛtaṃ khaṃ ca divaṃ mahīṃ ca yenādityastapati tejasā bhrājasā ca'; ityādikam, atameva mṛtyumamṛtaṃ tamāhustaṃ bhartāraṃ tamu goptāramāhuḥ'; ityādi ca gṛhyate । tathā ca viṣṇuliṅgatvena śrutisiddhāt sarvādhāraṇāt viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatyeveti bhāvaḥ ।

pṛthivyādi prakṛtyantaṃ bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhavacca yat ।
viṣṇureko bibhartīdaṃ nānyastasmātkṣamo dhṛtau ।
iti ca skānde ।
viṣṇuvadanyasyāpi sarvādhāratvaṃ kiṃ na syādityata āha pṛthivyādīti । prakṛtyantapadena sautrāntapadaṃ vyākhyātam । abhūtam'; atītaṃ abhavyaṃ'; bhaviṣyat abhavat'; vartamānaṃ ayat'; idaṃ viśvaṃ tadviṣṇuḥ aeka eva'; asahāyo bibharti । tasya dhṛtau tasmādviṣṇoranyaḥ akṣamaḥ'; samartho netyarthaḥ । iti skānda ityasya auktatvāt'; ityadhyāhāreṇa na sāvakāśatvaṃ liṅgasyeti vākyaśeṣeṇānvayaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
sā ca praśāsanāt ।
।
sā ca dhṛtiḥ prasāsanāducyate । aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane
gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ'; ityādinā ।
yuktyantareṇa viṣṇorevākṣaratvaṃ pratipādayatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe sā ceti । asā ca'; sarvadhṛtirapi ityādinā praśāsanāducyate yato ato api brahmākṣaramityanvayaḥ । ādiśabdenaivaṃrūpāṇyekaprakaraṇagatānekavākyāni gṛhyante । anena yadā asā'; pūrvoktā sarvadhṛtireva akṣarasya viṣṇutvasādhikā, tadā sutarāṃ, yā tu aetasya'; iti śrutivākye akṣarasya praśāsanādeva asaṅkucitaviṣayānanyāyattaprakṛṣṭājñāmātrādeva sarvadhṛtirucyate seti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

tacca praśāsanaṃ viṣṇoreva ।
nanu sarvadhṛtihetupraśāsanena kuto akṣarasya viṣṇutvaniścaya ityatastasya viṣṇukartṛkatvādityāha tacceti। sarvadhṛtikāraṇaṃ praśāsanaṃ tvityarthaḥ । na kevalaṃ sarvadhṛtiḥ, kintu taddhetupraśāsanaṃ ceti samuccaye vā caśabdaḥ । aviṣṇoreva'; viṣṇukartṛkameva । na tvanyakartṛkamiti evārthaḥ । evakārasyottaratropayogaḥ ।

saptārdhagarbhā bhuvanasya reto viṣṇostiṣṭhanti pradiśā vidharmaṇi । 
kuta etajjñāyata ityatastaccetyanena pratijñātārthe śrutiṃ pramāṇayati sapteti । ā ṛddhagarbhāḥ ārdhagarbhāḥ । brahmāṇḍākhyātisamṛddhagarbhāḥ । nigaraṇena bhriyanta iti garbhāstadāvaraṇabhūtā iti yāvat । reta iti liṅgavyatyayenaikavacanaṃ prathamābahuvacanārthe । tathā ca abhuvanasya'; lokasya aretaso'; ratipradāḥ sārabhūtā vā । yadvā bhūmatvātpūrṇatvādvananīyatvādbhajanīyatvādbhuvanasya viṣṇo retorūpāḥ asapta'; mahadahaṅkārapañcamahābhūtākhyāḥ brahmādayo devāḥ । bhavanasya areto'; retaso jagadratipradasya viṣṇoḥ apradiśā'; ādeśenājñayā avidharmaṇi'; vividhaviśvadhāraṇe tiṣṭhantīti ṛṅmantrārthaḥ । viśveśvaratīrthīye tu aardhasya'; viṣṇoḥ agarbhāḥ'; sapta devāḥ bhuvanasya aretaḥ'; kāraṇam । ete ca viṣṇoḥ pradiśā vidharmaṇi tiṣṭhantītyartha uktaḥ ।

caturbhissākaṃ navatiṃ ca nāmabhiścakraṃ na vṛttaṃ vyatīravīvipat ।
acaturbhiḥ'; iti vākyaṃ tu janmanaye vyākhyātam । evaṃjātīyakaśrutirādiśabdārthaḥ । śruterityasya jñāyata ityadhyāhāreṇa tacceti pūrvavākyenānvayaḥ ।

ekaśśāstā na dvitīyo asti śāstā ।
yo hṛcchayastamahamiha bravīmi ।
sarvadhṛtihetupraśāsanaṃ viṣṇorivānyasyāpi kiṃ na syādityata āha eka iti । idaṃ ca bhāratavākyaṃ sabhāparvagam । aśāstā'; sarvadhṛtihetvājñākartā । aekaḥ'; na tu dvitīyo asti, sa ca viṣṇurevetyarthaḥ । agarbhe śayānaṃ puruṣaṃ ko asti śāstā'; iti śiṣṭavākyam । ayo hṛcchayaḥ'; ityanyadvākyamuttaravākyaparyālocanayā prakṛtasaṅgatam । ayaḥ'; sarvadhṛtihetupraśāsanāya ahṛcchayaḥ'; sarvahṛdayanivāsī tamahamiha sthāne bravīmītyarthaḥ ।

na kevalaṃ me bhavataśca rājan ।
sa vai balaṃ balināṃ cāpareṣām ।
ityādeśca ।
ana kevalam'; ityādi hiraṇyakaśipuṃ prati prahlādavākyam । he rājan na kevalaṃ me bhavataśca asaḥ'; bhagavān abalaṃ'; balaprado dhṛtihetuḥ, kintvanyeṣāṃ balināṃ ca balamityarthaḥ । ityādeścetyasya atacca praśāsanaṃ viṣṇoreveti jñāyate'; ityanenānvayaḥ । anena viṣṇorevetyevakārasya kṛtyaṃ sūcitam ।

sū oṃ ।
anyabhāvavyāvṛtteśca ।
।
aasthūlamanaṇu'; ityādinā sthūlāṇvādīnāmanyavastusvabhāvānāṃ vyāvṛtteśca ।
hetvantareṇa viṣṇorevākṣaratvaṃ pratipādayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe anyeti । ādiśabdena aetadvai tadakṣaraṃ gārgi brāhmaṇā abhivadanti asthūlamanaṇvahrasvamadīrghamalohitamasnehamacchāyamatamo avāyvanākāśamasaṅgamarasamagandhamacakṣuṣkamaśrotramavāgamano atejaskamapramāṇamamukhamamātramanantaramabrāhmaṃ na tadaśnāti kiñcana na tadaśnāti kaścana'; iti samagravākyaṃ gṛhyate । asthūlāṇvādīnām'; iti bhāvapradhāno nirdeśaḥ । vyāvṛtterityanantaraṃ akathanāt'; iti śeṣaḥ । co hetusamuccaye । asyāpi brahmaivākṣaramiti pūrveṇānvayaḥ ।
anena na kevalaṃ pūrvoktahetubhyāṃ, kintvanyeṣāṃ sakalavastūnāṃ bhāvānāṃ svarūpāṇāṃ sthaulyādidharmāṇāṃ vyāvṛtteḥ ananyāpekṣārāhityasya aasthūlam'; ityādinākṣare kathanādapyakṣaraṃ brahmaiveti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।
śrutyarthastu atat'; ākāśāśrayatvena vakṣyamāṇam aakṣaraṃ'; na kṣaratītyakṣaraśabdavācyaṃ brahma etallakṣaṇakaṃ abrāhmaṇāḥ'; jñānino abhivadanti vai prasiddham । tatkiṃ lakṣaṇamityata āha asthūlamiti । sthūlaṃ mahat । svaprabuddhārthāntaraṃ tu aetat'; akṣaraṃ brāhmaṇāḥ atat'; citprakṛtyākhyamiti vadanti pūrvapakṣayanti tadbrahmetyabhivadanti siddhāntayanti । siddhāntasādhakaṃ hetumevāha asthūlamityādineti । anena aprasiddhasthūlasūkṣmādivailakṣaṇyājjanārdanaḥ'; iti bṛhadbhāṣyoktarītyā prasiddhasthūlādivailakṣaṇyamucyate । sthūlāṇvādipadasya bhāvapradhānatve tu lokikasthaulyādirāhityamanenoktaṃ bhavati । aalohitaṃ'; lohitaśabditaraktādyupalakṣitaprākṛtarūpasāmānyarahitam । aasnehaṃ'; prākṛtasneharahitam । aacchāyaṃ'; achāyātvavidyā samproktā'; iti vacanādajñānarahitam । jīvadehasyeva chāyārahitaṃ ca । aatamaḥ'; āvaraṇarahitam । aavāyu'; pīḍārūpaśvāsocchvāsarahitam । yadvā vyāsatīrthīyoktarītyā avāyvanākāśamatejaskamityetaistadārabdhaśarīrarahitamityucyate । ata eva aacchāyamatamo avāyvanākāśam'; ityatra sarvātmanā niṣedha ityuktaṃ sudhāṭīkayoḥ। aasaṅgaṃ'; sarvagatamapi tatkṛtaleparahitam । arasamagandhamityābhyāmupalakṣaṇayā prākṛtarasagandhādirāhityamucyate । acakṣuṣkamityādinā prākṛtasvabhinnacakṣurādirāhityam । aatejaskaṃ'; prākṛtavarcorahitam । aaprāṇam'; uktacakṣurādivyatiriktaprākṛtajñānendriyakarmendriyarahitam । vyāsatīrthīyoktarītyā prāṇavāyurahitamiti vā । aamukhaṃ'; prākṛtavigraharahitaṃ vā । aamātraṃ'; parimitiśūnyam । mīyante ebhiriti mātrā indriyāṇīti ṭīkokteḥ amātraṃ cakṣurādīndriyarahitamiti vyāsatīrthīyoktiḥ । sarvātmanā śarīrārambhakapañcamātraśūnyaṃ vā । na vidyate antaraṃ bāhyaṃ ca yasmāttadanantaramabāhyam, idameva sarvasmādantaraṃ bāhyaṃ cetyarthaḥ । atat'; brahma akiṃ ca na'; annādikaṃ śubhamaśubhaṃ vā sāśanānaśanatvena naradevau yathoditau ।
attiṃ vināpyadaurbalyāttathānattirharerbhujiḥ ।
iti smṛterupajīvanārthaṃ anāśnāti'; nātti । akaścana'; ko api samarthaḥ atat'; brahma anāśnāti'; na saṃharatīti ।

aasthūlo anaṇuramadhyamo madhyamo avyāpako vyāpako yo asau harirādiranādiraviśvo viśvaḥ saguṇo nirguṇaḥ'; ityāderviṣṇoreva
te dharmāḥ ।
laukikasthaulyādirāhityaṃ kathaṃ viṣṇutvaniścāyakaṃ, taddharmatvenāniścitatvādityata āha asthūla iti। aasthūlaḥ'; laukikamahattvarahitaḥ, aanaṇuḥ'; laukikāṇutvarahitaḥ, aamadhyamaḥ'; laukikamadhyamaparimāṇarahitaḥ । na ca parimāṇādirāhitye viṣṇorasvabhāvatvāpattiriti vācyam । laukikasthaulyādirāhitye apyalaukikaparimāṇādisadbhāvādityāha madhyama ityādinā ।। na cānena sthūlatvāderanukternacoktaparihāra iti vācyam । amadhyamo vyāpakaḥ'; ityādyukteḥ sthūlo aṇuścetyupalakṣakatvāt । na camadhyamaparimāṇavattve viṣṇoranityatvāpattiriti vācyam । anityatvānāpādakamadhyamaparimāṇābhyupagamāt । tattvapradīpe tu aamadhyamo'; madhyamaparimāṇaniyativarjitaḥ avyāpto aṇurmadhyamastathā'; ityukteḥ madhye mīyamānatvānmadhyama iti vyākhyātam । asmin pakṣe niyatamadhyamaparimāṇa śūnyatvānnānityatvamiti parihāro abhipretaḥ । na vidyate anyo vyāpako yasyāsāvavyāpakaḥ । lokavilakṣaṇavyāpaka iti vā । avyāpakaḥ'; sarvadeśakālavyāpī । ādiḥ kāraṇamanādistacchūnya utpattiśūnya iti vā । na vidyate viśvaḥ pūrṇo yasmādaviśvaḥ । pūrṇatvādviśvaḥ । yadvā aaviśvo'; laukikeṣvapraviṣṭaḥ । aviśvaḥ'; jagaddhṛdayaṃ vā praviṣṭaḥ । asaguṇo'; jñānānandādiguṇavān । anirguṇaḥ'; sattvādiguṇahīna ityarthaḥ । aityādeḥ'; itivākyāt । ādiśabdena aaṇoraṇīyānmahatomahīyān'; iti kaṭhaśrutirgṛhyate । ate'; asthūlatvādayaḥ । yata iti niścitā iti śeṣaḥ । asya ataste akṣarasya viṣṇutvaniścāyakā bhavantītyupaskṛtavākyenānvayaḥ । nanu tathāpi te viṣṇoreveti kathaṃ, yasmātte aprākṛtavigrahe madhyamākṣare api santi । naiṣa doṣaḥ yataste yatra bhagavadapekṣayaiva santi । anyānapekṣā eva dharmāhyatra hetutvena vivakṣitāḥ ।

asthūlo anaṇurūpo asāvaviśvo viśva eva ca ।
viruddhadharmarūpo asāvaiśvaryātpuruṣottamaḥ ।
iti ca brāhme ।
। iti akṣarādhikaraṇam । ।
nanu laukikaparimāṇādirāhityaṃ kathaṃ viṣṇoryuktaṃ, loke sarvapadārthānāṃ prākṛtaparimāṇasyaiva darśanādityata āha asthūleti । aasau puruṣottamaḥ'; bhagavān aasthūlo anaṇurūpo bhavati'; prākṛtalaukikasthūlāṇutvarūpadharmarahitavapurbhavati । evaṃ aaviśvo viśvaśca'; lokabahirbhūto lokāntargataśca bhavati । tathā viruddhadharmarūpaśca bhavati । loke parasparaṃ viruddhāḥ sthūlatvāṇutvādayo dharmāḥ svarūpabhūtā yasya saḥ tathoktaḥ । kathamityato ghaṭakamāha aiśvaryāditi । acintyaiśvaryasāmarthyādityarthaḥ । aiśvaryādevetyanena nātropapādakāntaramanveṣaṇīyamutyuktaṃ bhavati । iti brahmāṇḍe ityasya uktatvāt yuktā ityadhyāhāreṇa te dharmāḥ viṣṇoryuktā eveti pūrvavākyenānvayaḥ ।
। iti akṣarādhikaraṇam । ।

।
asadeva somyedamagra āsīt'; ityādinā sataḥ sraṣṭṛtvamucyate ।
atrādhikaraṇe anekaprakaraṇātmakaṃ asadeva'; ityādisthānaṃ samanvīyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyamudāhṛsya viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayati saditi ।। aityādinā'; chāndogyavākyena । ādiśabdena aekamevādvitīyaṃ, tattejo asṛjata, sanmūlāḥ somyemāḥ, satā somya tadā sampanno bhavati'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । taccetyataḥ tadityākṛṣyate । tathā ca ityādinā sataḥ atat'; janmanayoktaṃ asraṣṭṛtvam'; ananyādhīnakāraṇatvam । sarvottamatvasarvādhāratvasuptigamyatvādikaṃ ca aucyate'; pratipādyate iti yojanā । anena janmādhikaraṇoktakāraṇatvasya viṣṇvanyasmin pradhāne ākṣepāttenāsya ākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tathā viṣayavākyam, sadākhyo viṣayaścoktaḥ । asadeva'; ityuddālakavākyam । he asomya'; bhaktijñānalakṣaṇasomārha śvetaketho aidam'; asya jagataḥ aagre'; tatsṛṣṭeḥ pūrvaṃ pralaye sacchabdoktaṃ brahmaivāsīt svātantryeṇeti śeṣaḥ। tatsat aekamevādvitīyaṃ'; svagatasvāvayavabhedābhedaśūnyaṃ sarvottamam । prajāḥ asanmūlāḥ'; sadbrahmaiva mūlaṃ yāsāṃ tāstathoktāḥ । atadā'; suptau satā sampanno bhavati supta iti siddhānte śrutyarthaḥ । brahmalakṣaṇābhidhāyakānekavākyasaṅgrahakādiśabdaprayogena siddhānte apyatra pradhānasya pratipādyatvābhyupagamenāniṣṭābhāvādadhikaraṇavaiyarthyamiti śaṅkā nirastā bhavati । atra prakaraṇe śrutānāṃ brahmalakṣaṇānāṃ pradhāne asambhavena brahmaṇo api pratipādyatvena pradhānamātrasya pratipādyatvānabhyupagamāt ।

tacca sat abahu syāṃ prajāyeya'; iti pariṇāmapratīterna viṣṇuḥ ।
sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣayati tacceti । ca śabdaḥ pradhānamiti padākarṣako avadhāraṇe ca । tadityāvṛttaṃ vipariṇamyate । tathā ca atat'; chāndogye śrutaṃ satpradhānameva bhavet, na tu viṣṇuḥ । kutaḥ ? atasya'; sato abahu syām'; ityuttaravākyena bahubhāvākhyapariṇāmasya vikārasya pratīteriti yojanā । aprajāyeya'; prajanayeyaṃ jagatsṛjāni। tadarthaṃ abahu syām'; niyāmakabahurūpī bhaveyamiti । abahu syām'; tadarthaṃ prajāyeyeti vā śrutyarthaḥ ।

sa hi aavikārassadā śuddho nitya ātmā sadā hariḥ';
ityādināvikāra prasiddha iti ।
vikāritvapratītāvapi kuto ayaṃ na viṣṇurityata āha sa hīti । ahi'; yasmāt asaḥ'; viṣṇuḥ aavikāraḥ sadā'; ityādipramāṇairavikāraḥ aprasiddhaḥ'; tattvena niścitastasmāt tadasambhavāt pradhāne ca tatsambhavāt atra ca vikārapratīteḥ tatsat na viṣṇuḥ, kintu pradhānameveti yojanā । śrutau dvitīyasya sadāśabdasya sadāvikāra ityanvayaḥ । ādyasya tu sadā aśuddho'; nirmala iti ।

ato bravīti 
sū oṃ ।
īkṣatikarmavyapadeśāt saḥ ।
।
atadaikṣata'; itīkṣatikarmavyapadeśātsa eva viṣṇuratrocyate ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe ata iti । sūtroktaṃ vyapadeśaṃ darśayati taditir । ikṣatīti dhātunirdeśena tadarthekṣaṇakriyā lakṣyater । ikṣatikarmeti sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ tatkartṛtvaparam । tathā ca atadaikṣata'; iti śrutāvīkṣaṇākhyavyāpāre kartṛtvokterityarthaḥ। yadvā karmaśabdena sṛṣṭyādikriyocyate । tathātve vaiyadhikaraṇyarm । ikṣatipūrvakasṛṣṭyādivyapadeśādityarthaḥ । samanvayasūtrāttadityasya anuṣaṅgasambhave api aeko nārāyaṇa āsītsamunirbhūtvā'; ityādisamākhyāmapi pramāṇīkartuṃ sa ityuktam । tadanūdya viṣṇuriti vyākhyātam । viṣṇurevetyanvayaḥ । eveti tu śabdārthaḥ । anena samanvayasūtrāttuśabdamātramanuvartanīyamiti sūcitam । sūtre samanvetavyānukterāha atreti । asadeva'; ityādisthāna ityarthaḥ । sacchabdeneti pradhānamiti sādhyavākyārthaḥ । anena atra sadevetyādisthāne sacchabdenocyamānaḥ sa viṣṇureva, na pradhānam । kutarḥ ? aikṣatikarmavyapadeśāt saḥ'; tataḥ atadaikṣata'; itīkṣaṇākhyakriyākartṛtvaśravaṇādīkṣitṛtvasṛṣṭyādikriyayorvā śravaṇājjaḍaprakṛtau ca tadasambhavāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । sūtre sacchabdeneti śeṣaṃ vinā sa ityasyāvṛttiḥ, tatraikasya pratīkagrahaṇārthatvamiti pakṣer ikṣatikarmavyapadeśāt asaḥ'; aso akāmayata'; ityādiprakaraṇapratipādyaḥ sa viṣṇureva bhavet, na pradhānamitayartho avaseyaḥ ।

anānyo ato asti draṣṭā'; anānyadato asti
draṣṭṛ'; ityādinā tasyaiva hi tallakṣaṇam ।
nanvīkṣaṇakartṛtvaṃ viṣṇuvatpradhānasya kiṃ na syādityataścetanasyāpi iha hetutvenābhimataṃ mukhyekṣaṇaṃ na sambhavati, kimu jaḍasyetyāśayena tatra pramāṇamāha neti । aato'; brahmaṇaḥ sakāśāt aanyaḥ'; svātantryeṇa draṣṭā draṣṭṛ ca nāstīti vājasaneyaprakaraṇadvayagatavākyadvayasyārthaḥ । ādiśabdenaivaṃjātīyakaṃ vākyaṃ gṛhyate । atasya'; viṣṇoreva । hi śabdaḥ prasiddhau । svātantryeṇekṣaṇakartṛtvalakṣaṇaṃ liṅgaṃ uktamiti śeṣaḥ । asya tasmānna liṅgasya anyagāmitvaṃ mantavyamityupaskṛtavākyenānvayaḥ ।

bahutvaṃ cāvikāreṇaivoktam aajāyamāno bahudhā vijāyate'; iti ।
। iti sadadhikaraṇam । ।
nanu viṣṇoravikāritayā siddhatvena tatra bahubhāvākhyavikārānvayāyogānniravakāśavikāritvaliṅgenātrekṣatirgauṇo vyākhyeyaḥ । asattvātsañjāyate jñānam'; iti smaraṇāt jñānopādānatayā siddhe pradhāne tatkartṛtvāsambhavena tatra tasyāmukhyatvādityata āha bahutvaṃ ceti ।। aavikāreṇa'; vikāritvaṃ vinaiva svarūpabahutvenaivetyarthaḥ। ityādinoktamityanvayaḥ। tathā ca bahutvasya sāvakāśatvāt na tadbalenar ikṣatergauṇatvaṃ kalpanīyamiti bhāvaḥ। yadvā abahutvaṃ'; abahu syām'; iti bahubhāvavacanaṃ ca auktaṃ'; vyākhyātam । tathā ca ityevamādipramāṇavākyena abahu syām'; iti bahubhāvavacanam aavikāreṇa'; vikāraṃ vinaiva niyāmakasvarūpabahutvenaiva mukhyapratipādyenaiva yuktamityuktam iti yojanā । tathā ca siddhānte abahu syām'; ityasya tattanniyāmakasvarūpabahubhāvasaṅkalpor'tha ityuktaṃ bhavati । na caivaṃ niyāmakasvarūpabahubhāvasaṅkalpānantaraṃ niyamyasṛṣṭirayukteti vācyam । gurutvarājatvādeḥ śiṣyabhṛtyasāpekṣatvena tatsaṅkalpānantaraṃ śiṣyādisampādanavat niyāmakatāyā niyamyasāpekṣatvena niyāmakabahubhāvasaṅkalpānantaraṃ tatsāpekṣaniyamyasṛṣṭeryuktatvāt aajāyamānaḥ'; avikurvāṇaḥ iti śrutyarthastu dyubhvādinaye abhihitaḥ ।।
। iti sadadhikaraṇam । ।

।
candrādityādyādhāratvaṃ viṣṇoruktam । tacca aatha yadidamasmin
brahmapure daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma daharo asminnantara ākāśaḥ kiṃ
tadatra vidyate a; 
aubhe asmin dyāvāpṛthivī antareva samāhite ubhāvagniśca vāyuśca
sūryācandramasāvubhau vidyunnakṣatrāṇi'; 
ityādinā'kāśasya pratīyate ।
atrādhikaraṇe sarvādhāratayānveṣṭavyatayā ca sākṣādvā vyavadhānena vā sāmānyato hṛtpadmasthatvaliṅgasya brahmaṇi samanvayaḥ kriyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayavākyamudāhṛtya viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayan sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣayati candreti ।। aetasya vā akṣarasya'; ityādineti vartate । ādipadena dyāvāpṛthivyādikaṃ gṛhyate । tataḥ kimityata āha tacceti ।। caḥ samuccaye avadhāraṇe ca । tathā ca atatra'; chandogaśrutau yadakṣaranayodāhṛtavākyoktaṃ candrādityādhāratvaṃ tadeva tathā tatsamānādhikaraṇaṃ hṛtpadmasthatvaṃ ca ākāśasya aatha'; ityādinā vākyena pratīyata iti yojanā ।
yadyapi bṛhadbhāṣye akṣaranayodāhṛtabṛhadāraṇyakaśrutigatasūryacandrapadayorbrahmarudraparatayā vyākṛtatvādevamanuvādo anupapannaḥ । tathāpi tayoḥ prasiddhacandrasūryaparatvasyāpyanumatatvādevamuktiḥ । yadvā atra bhāṣye api candrādityapade rudrabrahmapare । ata eva tattvapradīpe akṣaranaye aahaṃ somam'; iti vacane somaśabdo rudraparatayā vyākṛtaḥ । tathā ca na ko api virodhaḥ । anenākṣaranayoktacandrādityādyādhāratvasya sākṣāt hṛtpadmasthākāśaniṣṭhatākṣepāttena asyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । evaṃ sarvādhāratvānveṣṭavyatvasamānādhikaraṇaḥ sākṣādvyavadhānena vā sāmānyato hṛtpadmasthatvarūpo viṣayaśca darśitaḥ । na caivaṃ acandrāditya'; iti bhāṣyeṇa sa candrādityādyādhāraḥ kiṃ daharākāśaḥ syāt? āhosvittatsthaḥ kaścit? iti tattvapradīpena ca virodha iti vācyam । tayorakṣarādhikaraṇākṣepeṇa atra pūrvapakṣa iti darśayituṃ pravṛttatvena viṣayapradarśanāyāpravṛttatvāt । aākāśasya'; ityanena prasiddhabhūtākāśasyaiva sarvādhāratayā sākṣāt hṛtpadmasthatvamiti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ pradarśitaḥ । tathā praśnaprativacanapūrvakaṃ sākṣādākāśasyaivātra sarvādhāratayā hṛtpadmasthatvakathanāditi pūrvapakṣayuktiśca pradarśitā bhavati । atra yadyapi aatha yadidamasmin brahmapure daharaṃ puṇḍarīkaṃ veśma daharo asminnantarākāśaḥ tasmin yadantastadanveṣṭavyaṃ tadvāva vijijñāsitavyamiti । taṃ cadbrūyuḥ kiṃ tadatra vidyate yadanveṣṭavyaṃ yadvā va vijijñāsitavyamiti । sa brūyādyāvānvāyamākāśastāvāneṣo antarhṛdaya ākāśaḥ । ubhe asmin dyāvāpṛthivī antareva samāhite । ubhāvagniśca vāyuśca sūryācandramasāvubhau । vidyunnakṣatrāṇi'; ityādisamagravākyamudāhartavyam, na tu vicchidya । tathāpi samānajātīyaśrutyantaropasaṅgrahāyaivamudāhṛtamiti dhyeyam । śrutāvathaśabdaḥ prameyāntarārambhārthaḥ । abrahmapuram'; ityetat brahmaṇaḥ puraṃ nivāsasthānamiti brahmaiva pūrṇatvātpuramiti ca dvedhā vyākhyeyam । aantarhṛdaye'; iti saptamyantam । aākāśaḥ'; iti prathamāntam । tathā ca etasmin brahmapure śarīre yatpuraṃ brahmāsti aasmin'; tasminbrahmaṇi adaharaṃ'; dabhramalpaṃ apuṇḍarīkam'; abjaṃ aveśma'; tasya sadmarūpamasti asmin aantardaharaḥ'; alpo bhūtākāśo asti । kiṃ cātaḥ? atasmin'; ākāśe antaryadvartate atadanveṣṭavyaṃ'; jñātavyaṃ mārgitavyaṃ vā । nanu na ghaṭādivadanveṣaṇaṃ yuktam, apratyakṣatvādityatastadeva vivṛṇoti tadvāveti । tathā ca tadeva avijijñāsitavyaṃ'; vicāritavyam । iti guruṇokte ataṃ'; guruṃ prati acet'; yadi śiṣyāḥ abrūyuḥ'; pṛccheyuḥ । kimiti? aatra'; bhūtākāśe yadanveṣṭavyaṃ yadvāva vijījñāsitavyamityuktaṃ atat'; ādheyasvarūpaṃ akiṃ'; kiṃmahimaṃ ceti । na ca brahmapure brahmaṇo veśmetyuktyaivākāśasya brahmatvaniścayātpraśnāyoga iti vācyam । anyapure apyanyasya veśmasambhavādanyaveśmanyapyanyasyāvasthānasambhavāttadukteraniścāyakatvāt । evaṃ śiṣyaiḥ pṛṣṭe asaḥ'; gururbrūyāt ।
kimiti? hṛdo antaḥ antarhṛt tasminnayate astīti vyutpattyā aantarhṛdaye'; tacchabdabodhye hṛtpadmagatabhūtākāśe dyāvāpṛthivyādyāśrayaḥ aākāśaḥ'; tadākhyaḥ paramātmāstīti । nanvaṇau tasmin kathaṃ dyāvāpṛthivyādyavasthitirityatastasya vyāptatvamāha yāvāniti ।। aayaṃ'; bahiḥsthitaḥ aākāśaḥ'; tadākhyo bhagavān guṇataḥ parimāṇataśca yāvān eṣa āntaro api tāvāneva । tathā cāṇāvapi rūper iśaśaktyā mahattvasyāpi sattvādvyāptasya tasyānekādhāratvaṃ yujyata eveti bhāvaḥ ।
anyaparityāgenāsyaiva jijñāsyatve ko heturityato asya sarvādhāratvākhyaṃ mahimānamāha ubha ityādinā । asminnantare ye ubhe muktāmukte dyāvāpṛthivyau devyau asamāhite'; samavasthite । evamubhayavidhau agniśca vāyuścetyetau devau samāśritau । tathā ubhau muktāmuktau sūryācandramasau vidyut nakṣatrāṇi ca samāśritānīti chāndogyabhāṣyarītyā śrutyarthaḥ । nyāyavivaraṇe tadvivaraṇarūpaṭīkāyāṃ atasmin yadantaḥ'; ityatra hṛtpadmasthākāśagataṃ brahmānveṣṭavyamityuktam । na ca padmasthasya brahmatvāsiddhiḥ । śarīrapuṇḍarīkayorbrahma prati puratvaveśmatvoktyaiva anveṣṭavyasya brahmatvasiddheḥ । tathā ca padme brahmāstītyukte api tadbrahma kiṃ prakāramiti bhāvena punaḥ akiṃ tadatra vidyate'; iti pṛṣṭe tatprakārajñāpanāya ayāvān'; ityādyāha guruḥ । anena ca yadbrahmānveṣṭavyatayoktaṃ tadbrahmāntarhṛdaye yāvāneṣa prasiddhākāśastāvān sarvo apyākāśo vartate । tasmiṃścākāśe pṛthivyādikaṃ sarvaṃ samāśritam । apahatapāpmatvādiguṇakaṃ ca tadityevamākāśādisarvāśriyatvādapahatapāpmatvādiprakāra ukto bhavatīti prakārāntareṇa vyākhyātam । pūrvapakṣī tu ahṛdaya ākāśe'; iti padaṃ saptamyantaṃ kṛtvā daharākāśastho vyāptākāśo anveṣṭavya iti vā ākāśaḥ iti prathamāntaṃ kṛtvā prāguktadaharabhūtākāśamanūdya yāvānityanena bāhyākāśatulyatayā taṃ viśiṣya jijñāsyatvena tatra dyāvāpṛthivyādikamucyata ityāha ।

sa cākāśo na viṣṇuḥ । atasyānte suṣiraṃ sūkṣmaṃ tasmin
sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam'; iti śruteriti ।
nanvastvākāśasya sarvādhāratayā hṛtpadmasthatvaṃ tasya cākāśasya aākāśastalliṅgāt'; iti nyāyena viṣṇutvena viṣṇoreva hṛtpadmasthvaṃ sidhyatītyata āha sa ceti । castvarthaḥ, pratijñāsamuccaye vā । tathā ca yassarvādāratayā hṛtpadmasthatvena ca śrutyuktaḥ asa cākāśo na viṣṇuḥ'; bhūtameva na tu viṣṇurityarthaḥ । kuto vā na viṣṇurityata āha tasyānta iti । sa cetyanuṣaktaścaśabdo atra buddhyā viviktasuṣirapadenānvīyate avadhāraṇe ca ayam । śrutisamānoktyupalakṣakaṃ caitat । tathā ca atasyānte'; iti vākye asuṣirapadaśruteḥ'; suṣiraśabdaśravaṇāt suṣirasya chidrātmakaprasiddhākāśasyaiva śruteḥ sarvādhāratayā hṛtpadmasthatvokteḥ tatsamākhyānādityarthaḥ । atasya'; apadmakośapratīkāśaṃ hṛdayaṃ cāpyadhomukham'; iti pūrvavākye prakṛtasya hṛtpadmakośasya aante'; antare tanmadhye sūkṣmaṃ asuṣiraṃ'; chidramasti, tasmin asarvaṃ'; jagatpratiṣṭhitamiti taittirīyaśrutyarthaḥ ।

ata āha 
sū oṃ ।
dahara uttarebhyaḥ ।
।
aya ātmāpahatapāpmā vijaro vimṛtyurviśoko avijighatso apipāsaḥ satyakāmassatyasaṅkalpaḥ so anveṣṭavyaḥ
sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ'; ityādibhya uttarebhyo guṇebhyo dahare viṣṇureva ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe ata iti । aityādibhyaḥ'; ityādirūpebhyaḥ auttarebhyaḥ'; viṣayavākyānantarabhāvibhyaḥ aśabdebhyaḥ uktebhyaḥ'; iti śeṣaḥ । ityādyuttaravākyebhya iti paryavasitārthaḥ । yadvā aguṇebhyo'; guṇavacanebhya ityarthaḥ । hetvasiddhiparihārāya śrutyudāharaṇam । ādipadena aviśoko avijighatso apipāsaḥ satyakāmaḥ satyasaṅkalpaḥ so anveṣṭavyaḥ sa vijijñāsitavyaḥ'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । guṇebhyaḥ ityanenottarapadamuttaratraśrutānekaśabdavācyaguṇopalakṣakamityuktaṃ bhavati । adahare'; hṛtpadmagatālpākāśe ityanena sūtre adahare'; iti saptapyantaṃ padaṃ, na paramata iva prathamāntamityuktaṃ bhavati । sthito anveṣṭavyatayokta iti śeṣaḥ । samanvayasūtrādanuvṛttasya vidheyaparasya tattvityasyārtho viṣṇoreveti । anena ayaḥ'; iti daharavākyāduttaravākye śrutebhyo guṇebhyo adahare'; vijijñāsyatayoktaḥ atattu'; viṣṇureva na bhūtākāśādiriti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । yo hṛtpadmākāśagataḥ paramātmā ana vadhenāsya hanyate'; iti prāk śarīrasya nāśenāvadhyatvenoktaḥ saḥ aapahatapāpmā'; nityameva svato apahatapāpmā pāpātyantābhāvavāniti yāvat । ata eva na tatkāryaṃ jarādikamasyetyucyate vijara ityādinā । aavijighatsaḥ'; bubhukṣārahitaḥ । aapipāsaḥ'; pānecchārahita iti । abubhukṣādinā pīḍābhāva ucyate'; iti jñānapādīyaṭīkokternādanapānecchābhāvobhi'dhīyate, pramāṇabādhitatvāt । kintu tatpīḍābhāvaḥ । atra hetuḥ satyakāma iti । tasya yadiṣṭaṃ tatsvataḥ eva bhavediti satyakāmaḥ । tatrāpi hetuḥ asatyasaṅkalpaḥ'; apratihatasaṅkalpa iti। ya evaṃ bhūtaḥ so anveṣṭavya iti śrutyarthaḥ ।

ayo aśanāyāpipāse śokaṃ mohaṃ jarāṃ mṛtyumatyeti'; 
asa eṣa sarvebhyaḥ pāpmabhya uditaḥ'; ityādinā viṣṇoreva hi te guṇāḥ ।
apahatapāpmatvādikaṃ kathaṃ viṣṇutvaniścāyakaṃ, tadgatatvenāsiddhatvādityata āha ya iti । bṛhadāraṇyakaśrutiriyam । aaśanāyā'; aśanecchā । apipāsā'; pānecchā । te aatyeti'; atikramya vartate । yaśca aśokaṃ'; duḥkhaṃ amohaṃ'; mūrchāṃ ajarāṃ'; maraṇaṃ cāpyetītyarthaḥ । atratyasya yacchabdasya atamātmānaṃ viditvā'; iti tacchrutisthatacchabdenānvayaḥ । asa eṣaḥ'; iti chandogaśrutiḥ । asa eṣaḥ'; paramātmā apāpmabhyaḥ'; pāpebhyaḥ auditaḥ'; nityaṃ svata evodgataḥ pāparahita ityarthaḥ । aityādinā'; vākyena ādiśabdena satyakāmatvādiguṇāntarabodhakavākyāni gṛhyante । hi śabdo yata ityarthe । te apahatapāpmatvādirūpottaravākyoktāḥ siddhā iti śeṣaḥ । tasmānna teṣāṃ viṣṇuliṅgatvaniścayaḥ iti vākyaśeṣeṇāsyānvayaḥ । anyatra pāpādyabhāvasya kathañcidyoge api sarvathā satyakāmatvādikaṃ na yujyata iti jñāpanāyādiśabdabahuvacanayoḥ prayogaḥ ।

nityatīrṇāśanāyādireka eva harissvataḥ ।
aśanāyādikānanye tatprasādāttaranti hi ।
tathāpi naite guṇā viṣṇoreva, ramādiṣvapi sambhavādityata āha nityeti । asvataḥ'; anyānapekṣayā nityaṃ tīrṇā aśanāyādayo yena sa harireka eva, nānyo asti । hareranye ramābrahmādayastu aaśanāyādikān'; aśanapānecchāśokādidoṣān atatprasādāt'; tasya hareranugrahādeva ataranti'; atiyanti, na svata ityarthaḥ । hi śabdaḥ prasiddhau । apādme'; uktamiti śeṣaḥ । ato nirapekṣaguṇānāmanyatrābhāvāt viṣṇorevetyuktamiti bhāvaḥ ।

sāpekṣanirapekṣayośca nirapekṣaṃ svīkartavyam ।
nanu ramādiṣvapahatapāpmatvādīnāmanyānadhīnānāmabhāve api yathā kathañcitsattvādanyagataistaiḥ kathaṃ viṣṇutvaniścaya ityata āha sāpekṣeti । asāpekṣam'; anyādhīnaṃ anirapekṣam'; anyānadhīnaṃ tayormadhye ityarthaḥ । co avadhāraṇe, nirapekṣameveti sambadhyate । apahatapāpmatvādikamiti viśeṣyaṃ prakṛtatvāllabhyate । asvīkartavyaṃ'; liṅgatveneti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca vivakṣitaliṅgasyānyatrābhāvāttena viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatyeveti bhāvaḥ ।

satyakāmaḥ paro nāsti tamṛte viṣṇumavyayam ।
satyakāmatvamanyeṣāṃ bhavettatkāmyakāmitā । ।
kiṃ ca sāpekṣatvanirapekṣatvādiviśeṣitānāmapahatapāpmatvādīnāmabhāvarūpāṇāmanyatrākāśādau sākṣādvābhimānidvārā vā yathākathañcidvṛttāvapi na kathañcidanyatra satyakāmatvādyastīti yuktastena viṣṇutvaniścaya ityāha satyakāma iti । aavyayam'; akṣīṇakāmamamoghakāmaṃ satyakāmaṃ viṣṇum aṛte'; vinā aparo anyaḥ'; viṣṇoranyaḥ satyakāmaḥ satyasaṅkalpaśca nāsti । viṣṇau tadbhāvasya tadanyasmin tadabhāvasya ca pratipādanāya vakroktiḥ । viṣṇoranyeṣāṃ ramādīnāṃ kvacidāgame pratīyamānamapi satyakāmatvaṃ atatkāmyakāmitā'; viṣṇukāmanāviṣayaviṣayakakāmanāvattvarūpameva bhavenna mukhyamityarthaḥ । tathā cāpahatapāpmatvaṃ svataḥ parādhīnaṃ ceti yathā dvividhaṃ, na tathā satyakāmatvaṃ kiṃ tvekavidhaṃ, tacca mukhyaṃ viṣṇāveva, anyatra tu pāribhāṣikamiti bhāvaḥ । askānde'; uktamiti śeṣaḥ। ataḥ satyakāmatvādivivakṣayā viṣṇoreva hi te guṇā ityuktaṃ yuktamiti bhāvaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
gatiśabdābhyāṃ tathā hi dṛṣṭaṃ liṅgaṃ ca ।
।
aaharahargacchantya etaṃ brahmalokaṃ na vindanti'; 
iti suptasya tadgatirbrahmaśabdaścocyate ।
yuktyantareṇa viṣṇorhṛtpadmasthatvaṃ pratipādayatsūtramupanyasyāsiddhiparihārāya śrutyudāharaṇapūrvakaṃ vyācaṣṭe gatīti । aimāḥ'; suptāḥ prajāḥ aaharahaḥ'; pratidinametaṃ agacchantyaḥ'; prāpyamāṇāḥ aetaṃ'; brahmalokaṃ brahmaṇo viṣṇorāvāsasthānabhūtaṃ hṛtpadmaṃ taddvārā tatratyaṃ brahma sākṣāllokapadoktaṃ brahmākhyamāśrayaṃ vā ana vindanti'; na vijānanti, sa eṣa ātmā hṛdīti śrutyarathaḥ । iti chandogavākye asuptasya'; cetanasya atadgatiḥ'; aharaho hṛdgataṃ brahmalokaṃ prati gatiḥ prāptiḥ aucyate'; vyapadiśyata ityarthaḥ । abrahmaśabdaḥ'; ityatrāpi taditi padaṃ buddhyā vivicya vipariṇāmena sambadhyate । tathā ca tasmin prāpyamāṇe hṛdgate brahmaloke abrahmaśabdaḥ'; aucyate'; śrūyate ityarthaḥ । ucyate ca ityapi sambandhaḥ । caḥ samuccaye । asyāto api dahare viṣṇureveti pradhānasādhyenānvayaḥ ।

asatā somya tadā sampanno bhavati'; 
iti śrutestaṃ hi supto gacchati ।
suptaprāpyatvaṃ kuto viṣṇutvaniścāyakamityata āha sateti । he asomya'; bhaktijñānārha śvetaketo atadā'; suptikāle asatā'; brahmaṇā asampannaḥ'; saṅgato bhavatītyarthaḥ । uddālakavākyametat । ataṃ'; viṣṇum । hi śabdaḥ prasiddhau । agacchati'; prāpnoti । iti jñāyate iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca suptaprāpyatvasya viṣṇuliṅgatvena śrutiprasiddhatvāt tena viṣṇutvaniścayo bhavatīti bhāvaḥ ।

aaraśca ha vai ṇyaścārṇavau brahmaloke'; iti liṅgaṃ ca tathā dṛṣṭam ।
aliṅgaṃ ca tathā hi dṛṣṭam'; iti sūtraśeṣaṃ hetvantaraparatayā vyācaṣṭe araśceti । ca śabdo hetusamuccaye । yathā suptagamyatvam aaharahaḥ'; iti śrutau hṛtpadmasthe dṛṣṭam, tathā araṇyanāmāmṛtasamudradvayāśrayalokavattvarūpaṃ liṅgamapi aaraśca'; iti śrutau hṛtpadmasthe dṛṣṭaṃ śrutamiti । upamāyāṃ tathāśabdaḥ । anenāsiddhiḥ parihṛtā । na ca gatiśabdayorivāsya sannidhau hṛtpadmasthasyānukterasiddhyanivṛttiriti vācyam । hṛtpadmasthasya brahmaṇa āvāsatvena nimittena tallokabhūte hṛtpadme aetaṃ brahmalokam'; iti prayuktasya brahmalokaśabdasyāṇyāśrayaloke api prayogāttanmukhena tādṛśalokavattvarūpaliṅgasya hṛtpadmasthabrahmaniṣṭhatāyā prāptatvāt । dṛṣṭamityanantaraṃ yata iti śeṣaḥ। asyāto api dahare viṣṇureveti pratijñāvākyenānvayaḥ । śrutau havā iti nipātau prasiddhidyotakau । samudrayoranyonyasamuccaye ca śabdau । tathā ca brahmaṇo viṣṇorloke śvetadvīpe araṇyākhyārṇavau sudhāsamudrau arṇavopame sudhāsarasī vā sta iti śrutyarthaḥ ।

araśca vaiṇyaśca sudhāsamudrau tatraiva sarvābhimatapradau dvau ।
ityādinā tasyaiva hi tallakṣaṇatvenocyate ।
nanu hṛtpadmasthasyāraṇyāśrayalokavattvaliṅgaśravaṇe api kuto ayaṃ viṣṇurityato araṇyāśrayatvasya viṣṇulokaikaliṅgatvena smṛtisiddhatvādityāśayena sautrahiśabdābhipretāṃ smṛtiṃ darśayati araśceti । vaiśabdaḥ prasiddhau । caśabdau parasparasamuccaye । atatraiva'; kṣīrābdhimadhyasthitaviṣṇuloka eva asarvābhimatapradau'; sarveṣṭakarau sta ityarthaḥ । evakāro anyatra sattvavyāvartakaḥ । tenāraṇyāśrayalokavattvaliṅgasya viṣṇutvenāvyabhicāraḥ siddhyati । ata eva bhāṣye tasyaivetyevakāraḥ । aityādinā'; puruṣottamadhyānacakravākyena atasyaiva'; viṣṇoreva atat'; sudhārṇavadvayāśrayalokavattvaṃ alakṣaṇatvena'; liṅgatvena aucyate'; pratipādyate ityarthaḥ । ahi'; yasmādityarthe । tasmādetalliṅgabalāt viṣṇutvaniśrayo yukta iti vākyaśeṣaḥ । yadvā brahmalokamiti hṛtpadmasya viṣṇulokatvokteḥ tadantargato viṣṇurityuktaṃ, brahmalokapadaṃ kuto viṣṇulokavācītyata āha araśceti । brahmalokapadasya viṣṇuloke aaraśca'; iti vākye prayogādatra hṛtpadme prayuktam aetaṃ brahmalokam'; iti padamapi viṣṇulokaparameva । na ca aaraśca'; iti śrutāvapi brahmalokapadaṃ kuto viṣṇulokaparamiti vācyam । yatastatrāraṇyāśrayatvaliṅgaṃ śrutamityarthaḥ । athāpyaraṇyāśrayatvasya bhagavallokaliṅgatvaṃ kuta ityata āha araśceti ।। asmin pakṣe sautraṃ liṅgapadaṃ hṛtpadmasthasya brahmatvarūpapradānasādhye hetutvābhāvātsūtre liṅgaśabdena pṛthaguktiḥ । pūrvavyākhyāne api gatiśabdayorivāsya liṅgasya viṣṇuniṣṭhatāyā upapādanasāpekṣatvena spaṣṭatvābhāvādgatiśabdaliṅgairityanuktvā liṅgaṃ ceti pṛthaguktiryuktā । anena na kevalamuttarebhyo guṇebhyaḥ, kintu gatiśabdābhyāṃ ca aaharahaḥ'; iti vākye hṛtpadmasthaniṣṭhatayā śrutābhyāṃ suptaprāpyabrahmaśabdābhyāṃ ca dahare viṣṇureveti jñāyate । na kevalametābhyāmeva, kintu yataḥ aaraśca'; iti śrutau atathā'; gatiśabdayoriva ahi'; viṣṇuliṅgatvena smṛtisiddhamaraṇyāśrayalokavattvarūpaṃ liṅgaṃ hṛtpadmasthe viṣṇuloke prayuktabrahmalokapadasya hṛtpadme prayogāt adṛṣṭaṃ'; śrutamato api dahare viṣṇureva । yadvā kuto atra prayuktasya brahmalokapadasya viṣṇulokaparatvam? aaraśca'; iti vākye viṣṇuloke brahmalokapadaprayogāt । atrāpi aetaṃ brahmalokam'; iti tasyaiva prayogāt । na ca tatrāpi viṣṇulokaparatvaṃ kutaḥ? yato araṇyāśrayatvaṃ liṅgaṃ adṛṣṭaṃ'; śrutamata iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū oṃ ।
dhṛteśca mahimno asyāsminnupalabdheḥ ।
।
aeṣa seturvidhṛtiḥ'; iti dhṛteḥ,
hetvantareṇa viṣṇorhṛtpadmasthatvaṃ pratipādayatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe dhṛteriti । aiti dhṛteḥ'; ityasya aasminnasya'; iti padānuvartanenetyasminvākye asya hṛtpadmasthasya dhṛtipadoktasarvādhāratvaśruterityarthaḥ । asya dahare viṣṇureveti pratijñāvākyenānvayaḥ । śrutau vidhṛtiḥ seturityanvayaḥ । tatra vidhṛtirityetatsetutve hetuḥ । tathā ca ya ātmā hṛtpadmasthatvenoktaḥ sa eṣa aeṣāṃ'; bhūrādilokānām aasambhedāya'; asāṅkaryāya avidāraṇāyeti, vyāsatīrthīyoktarītyā varṇāśramasāṅkaryābhāvāyeti vā avidhṛtiḥ'; dhāraṇapoṣaṇasamartho ata eva seturiva asetuḥ'; āśraya ityarthaḥ । dhārakatvaṃ ca na dhāryādbahiṣṭhatayā, kintvantaḥkṛtajagattvena, aśritamasmin jagatsarvamiti seturitīritaḥ'; ityukteḥ mukhyārtha eva vā setuśabdaḥ । yadyapi asa seturvidhṛtiḥ'; iti chandogaśrutipāṭhaḥ । tathāpi śākhāntarāṇāmapyatropasaṅgrahāyaivamuktiḥ । evamanyatrāpīti sampradāyavidaḥ ।

aeṣa bhūtādhipatireṣa bhūtapālaḥ'; ityādyasya mahimno asminnupalabdheḥ ।
evaṃ setusamuccāyakasautracaśabdasya yathāśrutānvayena liṅgoktiparatayā dhṛteścetyaṃśaṃ vyākhyāyedānīṃ samagraṃ sūtraṃ samānoktirūpasamākhyāparatayā vyācaṣṭe eṣa iti । dhṛteritipadamatrānuṣajyate । asmin pakṣe sautracaśbada upalabdheścetyanveti । tathā ca na kevalaṃ dhṛterliṅgāt, kintu adhṛteḥ'; dhṛtiyuktāyāstadbodhikāyā upalabdheḥ vāsaneyake aya eṣo antarhṛdaya ākāśastasmin śete sarvasya vaśī'; ityādyuktvā āmnātāyāḥ aeṣa sarveśvara eṣa bhūtādhipatireṣa bhūtapāla eṣa seturvidharaṇa eṣāṃ lokānāmasambhedāya'; ityukteḥ samānokteśca dahare viṣṇureveti yojanā । samākhyāyāḥ kuto viṣṇuparatvamityata āha eṣa iti । ityādīti luptatṛtīyāvibhaktiko nirdeśaḥ । ādiśabdena aeṣa sarvasya vaśī eṣa sarvasyādhipatireṣa sarveśvaraḥ'; iti pūrvavākyam aeṣa seturvidharaṇa eṣāṃ lokānāmasambhedāya'; ityuttaravākyaṃ ca gṛhyate । ata eva madhyasthavākyagrahaṇaṃ kṛtam । asya mahimna iti vyadhikaraṇaṣaṣṭhyau । upalabdherityāvṛttamatrānveti । tathā ca aasmin'; vājasaneyake aeṣa bhūtādhipatiḥ'; ityādinā vākyena aasya'; viṣṇorbhūtādhipatitvādimahimnaḥ aasmin'; daharākāśagate vastuni aupalabdheḥ'; uktatvāditi yojanā । ya eṣa sarvasyādhipatiḥ, yaścaiṣa sarveśvaro, yaścaiṣa prasiddho abhūtādhipatiḥ'; bhūta evādhipatirnāsyādhipatyamādimat, yaścaiṣa bhūta eva pālako, yaśca aeṣāṃ'; bhūrādilokānām aasambhedāya'; amelanāya eṣāṃ avidharaṇaḥ'; vidhāraṇasamarthaḥ, na kevalaṃ sāmarthyamātraṃ, kintu ya eṣāṃ lokānāṃ asetuḥ'; āśrayaśca, tametaṃ bhagavantaṃ brāhmaṇā vividiṣantīti śrutyarthaḥ । anena na kevalaṃ pūrvoktahetubhyaḥ, kintu vidhṛteścāsmin prakaraṇe asa seturvidhṛtiḥ'; iti sarvādhāratvaliṅgaśravaṇādapi daharapadmastho viṣṇureva । na cāsya hṛtpadmasthatvaṃ kuta iti vācyam । aasya'; hṛtpadmasthasya amahimnaḥ'; apahatapāpmatvāderlakṣaṇasya aasmin'; sarvādhāre asarve pāpmāno ato nivartante'; ityanena aupalabdheḥ'; uktatvāt । na kevalaṃ dhṛterliṅgāt, kintu dhṛterdhṛtiyuktāyā upalabdherukteḥ । aya eṣo antarhṛdaya ākāśastasmin śete eṣa seturvidharaṇaḥ'; iti vājasaneyasamākhyāyāśca dahare viṣṇureva । samākhyāyā api kuto viṣṇuviṣayatvam? aasmin'; vājasaneyake aasya'; viṣṇoḥ amahimno'; bhūtādhipatitvāderuktatvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । yadyapi aasya mahimnaḥ'; ityādyaṃśo bhāṣye dhṛteścetyasya liṅgaparatayā yojanāyāṃ nānvitaḥ । tathāpi ṭīkāyāṃ asarve pāpmāno ataḥ'; iti tallakṣaṇokteścetyuktatvāt liṅgasya hṛtpadmasthatvarūpapakṣadharmopapādakatayāpi yojanīyaḥ ।

aetasmin khalvakṣare gārgyākāśa otaśca'; 
aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi'; 
yaduktaṃ sarvādhāratvaliṅgaśravaṇāt hṛtpadmastho viṣṇuriti, tatra sarvādhāratvaṃ kuto viṣṇutvaniścāyakaṃ, tatsamānādhikaraṇatvenāsiddhatvādityata āha etasminniti । aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane'; iti pratīkagrahaṇena aetasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi sūryācandramasau vidhṛtau tiṣṭhataḥ, etasya vā akṣarasya praśāsane gārgi dyāvāpṛthivyau'; ityādibahuvākyāni sūcayati । imānyakṣaranaye vyākṛtāni ।

asa hi sarvādhipatiḥ sa hi sarvapālaḥ sar iśaḥ sa
viṣṇuḥ'; apatiṃ viśvasyātmeśvaram'; ityādiśrutibhyastasya hyeṣa mahimā ।
nanu samākhyāśrutyuktaḥ sarveśvaratvādimahimā kuto viṣṇoravagata ityata āha sa hīti । asa hi'; ityārabhya asa viṣṇuḥ'; ityantamekaṃ vākyaṃ śrutyantaragatam । asaḥ'; prakṛtaḥ । apatiṃ viśvasya'; iti nārāyaṇānuvākasthaṃ vākyam । aviśvasya'; acetanaprapañcasya patiṃ aātmeśvaraṃ'; cetaneśvaraṃ nārāyaṇaṃ tadviśvamupajīvatītyarthaḥ। evamādiśrutivākyebhya ityarthaḥ । ādiśabdenaitajjātīyaṃ gṛhyate । tṛtīyārthe pañcamī। atasya'; viṣṇoḥ ahiḥ'; prasiddhau hetau vā । aeṣa sarveśvaraḥ'; ityādimahimā । tasmānnaiteṣāṃ viṣṇutvarūpasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyāsiddhiriti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

sarveśo viṣṇurevaiko nānyo asti jagataḥ patiḥ ।
iti ca skānde ।
nanu sarveśvaratvādikaṃ viṣṇuvadanyasyāpi kiṃ na syādityata āha sarveśa iti । atra sarvajagacchabdau cetanācetanaprapañcaparau । yadvā jagataḥ patiriti pratiyogitvenaivoktasyānuvādaḥ । athavā apatiḥ'; pālakaḥ । tathā ca sarveśvaraḥ sarvapālakaśca viṣṇureka eva nānyo astītyarthaḥ । iti skānda ityasya evakāroktapadādhyāhāreṇa tasyahyeṣa mahimeti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । tasmānnaitalliṅgānāmanyatra sāvakāśatvaṃ śaṅkyamiti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
prasiddheś ca ।
।
atatrāpi daharaṃ gaganaṃ viśokastasmin yadantastadupāsitavyam'; iti prasiddheśca ।
samākhyāntararūpayuktyantareṇa viṣṇorhṛtpadmagatākāśasthatvaṃ sādhayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe prasiddheśceti । itītyanantaraṃ śrutāviti śeṣaḥ । tasyetyanuvartate । atasya'; viṣṇoḥ atasya'; hṛtpadmasthasyeti tadarthaḥ । anena sūtre asyāsminnitipadadvayaṃ pūrvasūtrādanuvartanīyam । tathā ca na kevalaṃ vājasaneyasamākhyānāt, kintu aasmin'; tatrāpīti taittirīyaśrutivākye aasya'; hṛtpadmasthasya viṣṇutvaprasiddheśca tatsamākhyānādapi daharapadmastho viṣṇureveti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । adivye brahmapure hyeṣa vyomnyātmā sampratiṣṭhitaḥ'; ityātharvaṇe prasiddheśca । aya eṣo antarhṛdaya ākāśastasminnayaṃ puruṣaḥ'; iti taittirīyavākyāntare prasiddheśceti sūtrasya yadvṛttyantaraṃ ṭīkāyāṃ sūcitaṃ, tadbhāṣyasthetiśabdasyādyarthatvamāśrityeti draṣṭavyam । śrutau adaharaṃ vipāpmaṃ paraveśmabhūtaṃ yatpuṇḍarīkaṃ puramadhyasaṃstham'; iti vākye yat adaharam'; alpaṃ parasya brahmaṇaḥ sadmabhūtam, ata eva vigatapāpaṃ dehākhyabrahmapuramadhye saṃsthaṃ hṛdayakamalaṃ prakṛtaṃ tattatreti parāmṛśyate । tathā ca atatrāpi'; puṇḍarīke api yat adaharam'; alpaṃ gaganamasti tasmin aantaḥ'; antare aviśoko'; viśokaṃ viśokapadopalakṣitaṃ jarādiśūnyaṃ yadbrahma tadupāsitavyamityarthaḥ । viśokaḥ iti liṅgavyatyayaḥ chāndasaḥ । tattvapradīpe tu liṅgavyatyāsastasya puruṣatvajñāpanārthaḥ । aya ātmāpahatapāpmā vijaro vimṛtyurviśokaḥ'; ityādāvuditaguṇānāmadhikaraṇaikyabalena sannidhīyamānānāmanukarṣaṇārthaśceti prayojanamuktam ।

tadantassthatvāpekṣatvānna suṣiraśrutivirodhaḥ ।
nanu sākṣāt padmagatasya viṣṇutvābhyupagame suṣiraśrutivirodhaḥ । evaṃ padmagatākāśasyaiva viṣṇutvābhyupagame api suṣiraśrutivirodhaḥ, suṣiraśabdasyākāśavācitvāt । etadvihāya daharapadmasyākāśatvaṃ, viṣṇostvākāśagatatvaṃ, tasyaiva sarvādhāratvamityupagame api suṣiraśrutivirodhaḥ । tatra sākṣātsuṣirasya sarvādhāratvokterityata āha tadantasstheti ।। buddhyā viviktasuṣiraśrutipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhyantamatrānvīyate । tathā ca asuṣiraśruteḥ'; iti suṣirapadaghaṭitaśruteḥ atadantassthāpekṣatvāt'; padmagatasuṣirāntassthaparamātmānamapekṣya pravṛttatvāttasya ca sarvādhāratvānna suṣiraśrutivirodho asmadabhyupagamasyetyarthaḥ । yathā mandirasthamañjūṣāntargatamapi vastu mandirasthamiti saṅgīyate, evamihāpīti bhāvaḥ । tadantassthatveti pāṭhe paramātmanaḥ suṣirāntassthatvamapekṣya śruteḥ pravṛttatvādityarthaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
itaraparāmarśātsa iti cennāsaṃbhavāt ।
।
aparaṃ jyotirupasampadya svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate,'; aeṣa ātmeti hovāca'; 
iti jīvaparāmarśātsa iti cet 
bhagavato hṛtpadmasthatvamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasyākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe itareti । aniṣpadyate'; ityanantaramityuktasyeti śeṣaḥ । asya ca samāsapraviṣṭajīvapadenānvayaḥ । anena sūtre asminnasyetyasyānuvṛttiḥ । itarapadaṃ siddhāntyabhimatabrahmapratiyogijīvaparam । ata eva śrutāveṣa iti jīvaparāmarśaḥ । siddhānte śrutyarthastu vakṣyate ।

na, tasya svato apahatapāpmatvādyasambhavāt ।
dhṛtisūtrāt aasyāsmin upalabdheḥ'; ityasyānuvṛttimabhipretyaparihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe neti । hṛtpadmastho na jīva ityarthaḥ । kuto netyatastatrānuvṛttavākyena aasmin'; prakaraṇe aasya'; apahatapāpmatvāderupalabdherityasya hetorlābhāttamanupanyasyoktahetorjīve niravakāśatvoktiparatayāsambhavādityaṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe tasyeti ।। jīvasyetyarthaḥ । muktabhāvamādāya jīve sambhavāt asiddhivārāṇāya svata iti । svātantryeṇetyarthaḥ । satyakāmatvādikamādiśabdārthaḥ । anena aasmin'; aparaṃ jyotiḥ'; itivākye abhivyaktikartṛtvenoktasya prakṛtasyopasampattikarmībhūtādbrahmaṇa itarasyāsya jīvasyātmeti aya ātmā'; ityuktahṛtpadmasthātmatvavidhānāya aeṣaḥ'; ityetacchabdena aparāmarśāt'; upasthāpanāt । jīvaparāmarśakaitacchabdaśravaṇāditi yāvat । dahare sa jīva eva, na viṣṇuriti cet na hṛtpadmastho jīvaḥ। kutaḥ? asminprakaraṇe asyāpahatapāpmatvāderupalabdheḥ śravaṇāt । asya cāsmin jīve svato asambhavāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū oṃ ।
uttarāccedāvirbhūtasvarūpastu ।
।
asa tatra paryeti jakṣan krīḍan ramamāṇaḥ'; 
ityādyuttaravacanājjīva eveti cet 
jīvasyāpahatapāpmatvādyasambhavamākṣipya samādadhatsūtramupanyasyākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe uttarāditi । aityādyuttaravacanāt'; evaṃrūpāddaharavākyāpekṣayā parāmarśavākyāpekṣayā vānantarādvacanādityarthaḥ । vacanādityanantaram asyāsminnupalabdherityanuṣajyate । sambhavāditi śeṣaḥ । aasya'; satyakāmatvasya aasmin'; jīve pratītestata eva viśokatvādeḥ aupalabdheḥ'; siddheruktaguṇānāṃ sambhavāditi tadarthaḥ । jīva ityanena pūrvasūtrātsa ityasyānuvṛttiḥ sūcitā। neśvarā iti evaśabdārthaḥ । hṛtpadmastha iti vartate ।

na, tatra hi parameśvaraprasādādāvirbhūtasvarūpo mukta ucyate ।
nañanuvṛttyā parihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe neti । naitadvākyabalena jīvasya satyakāmatvādiguṇān sambhāvya hṛtpadmasthatvaṃ vācyamityarthaḥ । kuto netyato abhihitam aāvirbhūtasvarūpastu'; ityaṃśaṃ tatreti padādhyāhāreṇa vyācaṣṭe tatreti ।। asa tatra'; ityuttaravākya ityarthaḥ । tatra aāvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ'; ucyate iti sambandhaḥ । āvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ ityasya vyākhyānaṃ mukta iti । hiśabdo yata ityarthe । uttaravacanādityatrāpi sambadhyate । tathā ca auttaravacanāt'; asvena rūpeṇa'; iti jaḍadehatyāgottarakālīnasvarūpābhivyaktiśruteḥ । atra muktasyokteḥ hṛtpadmasya ca dehāntaravṛttitayā muktatvāyogāt nāyaṃ jīva iti bhāvaḥ । nanvasya muktaviṣayatve api muktasyāpi jīvatve nāstyeva jīve apahatapāpmatvādisambhavaḥ । na ca tasya hṛtpadmasthatvāyogaḥ, yato jīvo bhāvibhāvenāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇaḥ idānīṃ hṛtpadmagatatayocyata ityata āha parameśvaraprasādāditi । anena tu śabdo vyākhyātaḥ । parameśvaraprasādādityanena uttarādityetaduttamādityapi vyākhyātam । atra mukta iti na sautrapadavyākhyānamātram । kintūddeśyasamarpakaṃ ca । anena āvṛttistuśabdasya yathāśrutānvayaśca sūcitaḥ । tathā ca yo atra mukta ucyate sa tu parameśvaraprasādādeva aāvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ'; āvirbhūto vyaktaḥ svarūpaḥ apahatapāpmatvādiḥ svadharmo yasya sa tathoktaḥ । ato na svato apahatapāpmatvādiguṇakaḥ, ato na daharasthaḥ jīva iti yojanā ।

yatprasādātsa mukto bhavati sa bhagavān pūrvoktaḥ।
nanu aparaṃjyotirupasampadya svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate'; ityatra muktasyābhivyaktāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇakatvamevocyate, na tu tadguṇānāṃ parameśvarādhīnatvam । atastatsvata evetyata āha yaditi ।। asya yacchabdasya dvitīyatacchabdenānvayaḥ । prasādo nāma icchāviśeṣaḥ । punaḥ sa ityuktyā sūtre anuvṛttasya sa ityasyāvṛttiḥ sūcitā । pūrvokta ityanena sūtre uttaratretyasya pratiyogitayā pūrvatretyupaskāryamityuktaṃ bhavati । tatheti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca ayatprasādāt'; yasyānugrahāt asaḥ'; jīvo amuktaḥ'; apahatapāpmatvādiguṇo bhavati । asaḥ'; guṇapradātā bhagavān, apūrvoktaḥ'; aparaṃjyotirupasampadya'; iti pūrvavākye atathā'; guṇapradātṛtayā ukta iti yojanā। anyathā lyabantapadaṃ vyarthaṃ syāditi bhāvaḥ । ukta ityanantaraṃ yata iti śeṣaḥ । asyātonātra muktaguṇaprāpteḥ parameśvarādhīnatvoktyabhāva ityupaskṛtavākyenānvayaḥ । athavā nanu jīve anyādhīnasya tadguṇajātasya sattvātsa evāpahatapāpmatvādinokto hṛtpadmasthaścāstvityata āha yaditi । yojanā tu yatprasādātsa jīvo jaḍadehānmukto bhavati, mukto bhūtvā ca sopahatapāpmatvādiguṇo bhavati, sa bhagavāneva apūrvoktaḥ'; aeṣa ātmāpahatapāpmā'; ityādipūrvavākye tathāpahatapāpmatvādinokto na jīvaḥ । dātṛpratigṛhītrormadhye dātureva mukhyatvānmukhyāmukhyayośca mukhyasyaiva grāhyatvāditi ।
