anena asya aeṣa samprasādo asmāccharīrātsamutthāya'; ityaktasya jīvasya auttarāt'; daharavākyāpekṣayā parāmarśavākyāpekṣayā vānantarāt asa tatra paryeti'; ityādivacanāt aasmin'; pūrvaprakṛte jīve aasya'; satyakāmatvasya aupalabdheḥ'; pratīteḥ, tata evāsya viśokatvādeḥ siddheśca । ata evāsyoktaguṇāsambhavābhāvātsa hṛtpadmastho jīva eva neśvara iti cet na, yatastatra asvena'; ityuttaravākyabalādāvirbhūtasvarūpo mukta ucyate । sa ca dehānantargatatayā na hṛtpadmastho bhavatīti bhāvaḥ । na ca muktasyāpi jīvatvena tatrāpahatapāpmatvahṛtpadmasthatvayorbhinnakālīnatve api sāmānādhikaraṇyopapatterasti punastasya prāptiriti vācyam । yato atra vākye yo mukta ucyate sa uttarāduttamātparameśvaraprasādādevāvirbhūtasvarūpo na svataḥ । na cātra muktasya tadguṇatvamevocyate, na parameśvarādhīnatvaṃ tadguṇajātasyeti vācyam । yataḥ pūrvatra aparaṃ jyotiḥ'; iti pūrvavākye yatprasādātsa mukto bhavati sa paramātmā tathā guṇapradātṛtayocyate । na ca yathākathaṃ cit jīvasyāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇakatvātpunastatprāptiriti vācyam । yato yasmāduttarāduttamādbhagavatastatprasādātsa muktaḥ aāvirbhūtasvarūpaḥ'; abhivyaktāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇakaḥ sa tu bhagavāneva pūrvatra aeṣa ātmāpahatapāpmā'; iti pūrvavākye ukto, na muktajīva iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । śrutyarthastu aeṣaḥ'; jīvo yataḥ asamprasādaḥ'; samyagviṣṇuprasādavān ato aasmāt caramaśarīrāt'; asamutthāya'; muktaḥ ayatparaṃ'; ajyotiḥ'; brahma aupasampadya'; prāpya svena rūpeṇa aabhiniṣpadyate'; abhivyajyate asa uttamaḥ puruṣaḥ'; paraṃ jyotirakhyaḥ । muktasya viṣayaiścaraṇaprakāramāha sa iti । asaḥ'; prāptinijānandāvirbhāvo muktaḥ atatra'; muktisthāne paramātmānugraheṇaiva ajakṣan'; svāpekṣitaṃ bhakṣayan hasanvā jñātibhissaha muktaiḥ ajñātibhiḥ pūrvakalpamuktaiḥ akrīḍan'; strībhiḥ aramamāṇaḥ'; ratiṃ prāpnuvan prākṛtastryādiviṣayasaukhyamanubhavan aparyeti'; paritaḥ sañcaratīti ।

sū oṃ ।
anyārthaśca parāmarśaḥ ।
।
yaṃ prāpya svena rūpeṇa jīvo abhiniṣpadyate sa eṣa ātmeti
paramātmārthaśca parāmarśaḥ ।
nanu aeṣaḥ'; iti jīvaṃ parāmṛśya aātmā'; iti tasya hṛtpadmasthātmatvābhidhānādamukhyāpahatapāpmatvādiguṇo api jīvaḥ etacchabdaparāmarśabalena hṛtpadmasthātmā kiṃ na syādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya aitaraparāmarśātsa iti cenna'; ityanuvṛttapūrvavākyenāpekṣitasya siddhāntapratijñāyāśca lābhānnetyuktasādhye hetutayā sūtraṃ vyācaṣṭe anyeti । śrutau aparaṃjyotiḥ'; iti napuṃsakapadanirdiṣṭasya yamiti pulliṅgena nirdeśo liṅgasyāvivakṣitatvādvā viśeṣyaśabdavivakṣayā vā yuktaḥ । anena śrutau paraṃjyotiriti ekaṃ padam । yadvakṣyati aparaṃjyotiḥśabdena paramātmaivocyate'; iti, tacca aparaṃjyotiḥ paraṃbrahma'; iti paurāṇikarūḍhyā viṣṇuvācītyuktaṃ bhavati । jyotiḥ prakāśarūpaṃ paraṃ brahmeti bhinne pade ityapi kecit । asmin pakṣe uktabhāṣyavirodhaḥ । kiṃ ca yaṃ aparaṃjyotirākhyaṃ bhagavantam'; iti yacchabdavyākhyānaparaṭīkāvirodhaḥ । aparaṃjyotiḥ paramātmānam'; iti viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāvirodhaśca । śrutāvupasampadyetyasyārthaḥ prāpyeti । sautrānyapadaṃ pūrvapakṣyabhimatajīvapratiyogitayā vyākhyāti paramātmeti । paramātmaivārtho abhidheyo yasya sa tathoktaḥ । aparāmarśaḥ'; etacchabdaḥ । yadvā paramātmana evātmatvavidhānamarthaḥ prayojanaṃ yasya sa, tathoktaḥ । tathātve aparāmarśaḥ'; etacchabdena parigrahaṇamityarthaḥ । sūtrabhāṣyayoścaśabdastu na kevalaṃ jīvapakṣe apahatapāpmatvāsambhavākhyabādhakasadbhāvaḥ, kintu parāmarśākhyasādhakābhāvaśceti samuccayārthastuśabdārtho vā । candrikāyāṃ tu na kevalaṃ parāmarśasyar iśvarapakṣe bādhakatvābhāvaḥ, kintu jīvapakṣasādhakatvābhāvaścetyuktatvātparāmarśo jīvānyeśvarārtha eva ityavadhāraṇārthatayā vyākhyātaḥ । anena aitaraparāmarśāt'; itaraṃ jīvaṃ aeṣaḥ'; iti parāmṛśya tasya hṛtpadmasthatvavidhānātsa hṛtpadmastha ātmā jīva eva neśvara iti cet na, kutaḥ? yataḥ aeṣaḥ'; iti parāmarśaḥ aanyārthaḥ'; jīvānyeśvarārtha eva, na jīvārthaḥ, ataḥ । athavā na kevalamasambhavāt, kintu yataḥ parāmarśo anyārtho api । yadvā asambhavānna hṛtpadmastho jīvaḥ, kintvīśvara eva । na caivaṃ parāmarśāyogaḥ । yataḥ aparāmarśaḥ'; etacchabdastu anyārtha iti tredhāsūtrārtha ukto bhavati । ayaṃ prāpya'; yatsamīpaṃ prāpyeti । anena jīvaḥ paraṃ jyotirākhyaṃ paramātmānamupasampadyāparokṣato jñātvā atha samīpaṃ prāpyavidyāvidhūnanenānandādinā svena rūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate āvirbhūtasvaguṇo bhavatīti yāvat । yaṃ prāpya svarūpeṇābhiniṣpadyate jīvaḥ, sa eṣa ātmā ya ātmeti prāguktaḥ paramātmeti hovāca brahmādīn prati rameti siddhānte śrutyarthaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
alpaśruteriti cettaduktam ।
।
adaharaḥ'; ityalpaśruterneti cet 
uktamākṣipya samādadhātsūtramupanyasya śrutyudāharaṇenākṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe alpeti । adaharaḥ'; iti pratīkagrahaṇena adaharo asminnantara ākāśastasminyadantaḥ'; iti vākyaṃ gṛhyate । alpapadaṃ cālpasthānasthitiparam । śruterityanantaramasambhavādityanuvartate । asminniti cāsti । tathā ca adaharaḥ'; iti vākye aasmin'; daharagate vastunyalpasthānasthitirūpaliṅgaśrutestasyāścāsminparamātmani aasambhavāt'; anupapatterityanvayaḥ । asmāddhetorna dahare viṣṇuḥ, kintu sa jīva evetītarasūtrānuvṛttapratijñayānvayaḥ ।।

na, anicāyyatvādevaṃ vyomavacca'; ityuktatvāt ।
sūtre anuvṛttanaña āvṛttimabhipretya parihārāṃśaṃ vyākhyāti neti । nālpasthānasthitiśravaṇaṃ viṣṇāvanupapannamityarthaḥ । kuto netyataḥ pravṛttaṃ taduktamityaṃśaṃ yata ityadhyāhārābhiprāyeṇa hetutayā vyākhyāti nicāyyatvāditi । tathā ca anicāyyatvāt'; ityatra sarvagatasyāpi viṣṇorvyomavadalpasthānasthiteruktatvādityarthaḥ ।

aeṣa ma ātmāntarhṛdaye jyāyān'; iti śrutyuktatvācca ।
। iti daharādhikaraṇam ।
nanu yuktaṃ vyomnoṃ'śato alpaukastvam, aṃśasyāpūrṇatvāt । brahmaṇi tu aṃśo api pūrṇa iti kathaṃ tasyāṃśato alpaukastvamityataḥ sūtraśeṣaṃ prakarāntareṇa vyācaṣṭe eṣa ma iti ।। ca śabdo yuktisamuccaye । sūtrakṛcchrutyuktisamuccaye vā । aguṇāḥ śrutāḥ'; iti śrutisamuccaye vā । ayasmin'; iti smṛtisamuccaye vā । anena aalpaśruteḥ'; adaharaḥ'; iti vākye sarvagate vastunyalpasthānasthitiśravaṇāt, tasyāśca viṣṇāvasambhavādanupapatterna dahare viṣṇuḥ, kintu sa jīva eveti cet na, yataḥ ataduktaṃ'; tatra nicāyyatvāditi pūrvatra tasya sarvagatasyāpi viṣṇorvyomavattadalpasthānasthitatvam, tasmādupāsanārthaṃ yuktamityuktam । na cāṃśatopi sarvagatatayā tatra tadanupapattiḥ । yatastasyāṃ aeṣa ma ātmā'; iti chandogaśrutau tena sarvajyāyastvena vṛddhatamatvena vyāptatvenaiva prakāreṇa tasya viṣṇostaddhṛdayasthatvamuktaṃ smṛtyuktaṃ cāta iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । na ca śrutismṛtyuktamapi kathametadaṅgīkārārhaṃ, yuktivirodhāditi vācyam । brahmaṇo acintyaśaktitvādupapatteḥ । aguṇāḥ śrutāḥ'; ayasminviruddhagatayaḥ'; ityādivacanācca । mama hṛdaye ya aātmā'; paramātmāsti । upalakṣaṇametat । sarvahṛdaye ca ya āste eṣaḥ hṛdayasthāṃśarūpo bhagavān ajyāyān'; vṛddhatamaḥ deśakālaguṇaiḥ pūrṇa iti śrutyarthaḥ । upaniṣaddraṣṭṛṛṣivākyametat । ('viruddhagatayo api'; anyatra bhinnāśrayā apyaṇutvamahattvādayo dharmāḥ yasmin apatanti'; vartante ca । na kālabhedenetyāha aniśamiti । muktasādhāraṇyamāśaṅkyāha vidyādaya iti ।
yasmādviṣṇoranyatrāṇutvamahatvādivividhaśaktayo dharmāḥ । vidyā āhiḥ jñaptikāraṇaṃ yeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ । jñānajñeyā iti yāvat । harau viruddhadharmasattve pramāṇamāha ānupūrvyeti । aānupūrvī śrutirvedastrayī cāmnāya ucyate'; ityabhidhānācchrutyā siddhā ityarthaḥ । yacchabdasya atadbrahmāhaṃ prapadye'; iti uttaravākyagatatacchabdenānvayaḥ) ।।
। iti daharādhikaraṇam । ।

। anukṛtyadhikaraṇam ।
adṛśyatvādayaḥ parameśvaraguṇā uktāḥ । ateṣāṃ sukhaṃ
śāśvataṃ netareṣām । tadetaditi manyante anirdeśyaṃ paramaṃ sukham'; ityādinā jñānisukhasyāpyanirdeśyatvamajñeyatvaṃ cocyata iti ।।
atrādhikaraṇe akathaṃ nu tadvijānīyām'; iti vākyoktaṃ jñānārthaṃ jñeyaprārthanāviṣayatvaṃ vā akathaṃ nu tadvijānīyāṃ kimu bhāti'; iti brahmajñānānukūlābhivyaktyākhyabhānaprārthanāviṣayatvarūpaṃ vā ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvaṃ liṅgaṃ brahmaṇi samanvīyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayan sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣaṃ darśayati adṛśyatvāditi। auktāḥ'; ānandamayādhikaraṇe udāhṛtādṛśya iti vākye iti bhāvaḥ । uktā ityanantaraṃ tatra praviṣṭamiti śeṣaḥ । prathamādipadenāniruktatvādeḥ, dvitīyena akathaṃ nu tadvijānīyāṃ kimu bhāti na bhāti vā'; iti samanvetavyaliṅgabodhakottarārdhasya ca grahaṇam । na kevalaṃ viṣṇoḥ, kintu jñānisukhasyāpītyaperarthaḥ । evārtho vāpiśabdaḥ ānumānikasūtragatāpipadavat । aajñeyatvaṃ'; sākalyenājñeyatvaṃ durjñeyatvamiti yāvat । caśabdaḥ parasparasamuccaye, ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvarūpasamanvetavyaliṅgasamuccaye vā । pūrvaśratyanusārādadṛśyatvādaya iti, etacchrutyanusārādanirdeśyatvamiti vyutkramaḥ। yadyapi atadetaditi'; etadevodāhartavyam । tathāpi pūrvapakṣe tacchabdārthapradarśanāya ateṣām'; iti pūrvavākyaikadeśopanyāsaḥ । ata eva tattvapradīpe teṣāmiti prastutiḥ pūrvapakṣotthāpiketyuktam । tathācetthaṃ yojanā pūrvamānandamayādhikaraṇe ye adṛśyatvādayo guṇāḥ parameśvarasyoktāḥ । tatra teṣu praviṣṭamanirdeśyatvamajñeyatvaṃ ca ateṣāṃ sukham'; iti prakṛtyāmnātena atadetat'; ityādinā kāṭhakavākyena pūrvapakṣirītyā samīpasthāttacchabdāt parāmṛṣṭasya ajñānisukhasyāpi'; jñānisukhasyaivocyata iti । pūrvārdhenānirdeśyatvasyottarārdhe ca akimu bhāti na bhāti'; ityanena durjñeyatvaparyavasitājñeyatvasya cārthāduktatvāditi bhāvaḥ । ṭīkāyāmadṛśyatvapadasyānirdeśyatvaparatvādanirdeśyatvamiti pāṭhābhyupagamādvā na tadvirodhaḥ । atrānirdeśyatvamajñeyatvaṃ cocyata iti phaloktiḥ, ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvasyaivātra vicāryatvāt । tattu dvitīyādiśabdopāttavākyena caśabdena vā sūcitamiti draṣṭavyam । yata evamataḥ pūrvoktamayuktamiti bhāvaḥ । anenānandamayādhikaraṇoktādṛśyatvājñeyatvarūpasyānirdeśyatvāniruktatvarūpasya ca tatrānyatra ca sattve jñānisukhe ativyāptyākṣepāt itaramātraniṣṭhatvetvasambhavākṣepātphalatastenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tathā caśabdasūcitamānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvaṃ viṣayaḥ । viṣṇoranyasya veti sandehaḥ । jñānisukhasyaiveti pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ । anirdeśyatvājñeyatve ca tasyaiveti phalaṃ, sukhaśrutiḥ, prakṛtatvādirupayuktiśca sūcitā bhavati ।

ato vakti 
sū oṃ ।
anukṛtestasya ca ।
।
atameva bhāntamanubhāti sarvam'; ityanukṛteḥ, atasya bhāsā sarvamidaṃ vibhāti'; iti vacanācca paramātmaiva
anirdeśyasukharūpaḥ ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe ata iti । aityanukṛteḥ'; ityanubhānaśruterityarthaḥ । anubhānaṃ nāma tadicchānurodhena bhānaṃ kriyāviśeṣaḥ । sūtre tasyetyasyānukṛterityanenāpi sambandhe tenaivānukaraṇapratisambandhina ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya tatkartuḥ sūryāditejasaśca lābho bhavatīti spaṣṭatvāttadubhayānuktiḥ । yadvā pūrvasūtrāttadityasya vipariṇatasyehānuvartanādubhayalābho bhavatītyāśayena tadubhayānuktiḥ । na kevalaṃ tasyetyetat samanvetavyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇatvākhyaliṅgadharmiṇaḥ, sūryāditejasaśca parāmarśakaṃ, kintu śrutipratīkarūpamapi sarvajagatprakāśakatvaparaṃ cetyāśayena taddhetvantaraparatayā vyācaṣṭe tasyeti । aiti vacanāt'; ityanena sūtre ityukteriti śeṣo darśitaḥ । yadyapi sūtrabhāṣyayoḥ aanubhāti'; itiśrutyanusārādanubhānāditi vācyam । tathāpi tāpinī pācinī caiva śoṣiṇī ca prakāśinī ।
naiva rājan raveśśaktiḥ śaktirnārāyaṇasya sā ।
iti aitareyabhāṣyodāhṛtapādmavacanātsūryādikartṛkapratapanādikamapi paramātmādhīnamiti darśayitumanukṛterityuktam । sūtre tadanusāribhāṣye ca caśabdo dvitīyasūtrasya vakṣyamāṇavyākhyānabhedena sarvajagatprakāśakatvarūpoktahetusamuccaye vā, sūryādyaprakāśyatvarūpānuktahetusamuccaye vā draṣṭavyaḥ । sūtre samanvayasūtrādanuvṛttasya vidheyaparasya tattvityasyārthamāha paramātmaiveti । na tu jñānisukhamityevaśabdārthaḥ । liṅgasamanvayena bhavatphalaṃ darśayati anirdeśyeti । anirdeśyaścāsau sukharūpaśca iti vā, anirdeśyaṃ yatsukhaṃ tadrūpa iti vā vigrahaḥ । atra rūpaśabdo bhinnakramaḥ । tathā cānirdeśyaṃ paramaṃ sukhaṃ paramātmarūpamityanvayaḥ । eka ityādau pulliṅgena prakṛtasyaitaditi napuṃsakaliṅgena grahaṇāya rūpaśabdaprayogaḥ । anugrāhyascetyapi draṣṭavyam । vastutastu vacanāccetiśabdasya sukharūpaścetyapi sambandhe tenaivānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇākhyaḥ sādhyadharmī sūcita iti dhyeyam । yadyapyanirdeśyatvamajñeyatvaṃ cetyupakramādubhayaṃ grāhyaṃ, na tvekaṃ, sukharūpamiti cādhikam । tathāpi pūrvapakṣyuktasukhaśruteḥ sukharūpe brahmaṇi sāvakāśatvajñāpanāya atadetat'; itivākyoktamanirdeśyasukharūpatvameva gṛhītam । ajñeyatvamapi draṣṭavyam । yadyapyatra bhāṣye liṅgadvayasyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya vā anirdeśyasukharūpasya vā viṣṇutve sādhye sākṣāddhetutvaṃ bhāti । ṭīkāyāṃ tu atadetat'; iti śrutisthatacchabdena samīpoktajñānisukhaparityāgena acetanaścetanānām'; iti vyavadhānena prakṛtaparamātmagrahaṇe liṅgadvayaṃ hetutvena yojitam । tathāpi hetudvayena tacchabdena jñānisukhaparityāgena paramātmana eva grahaṇasiddhau tata eva tacchabdagṛhītasya paramātmana evānirdeśyasukharūpatvaṃ paryavasyatītyāśayena bhāṣye liṅgadvayasya prakṛtasādhyahetutvenoktirityavirodhaḥ । kecittu aparamātmaivānirdeśyasukharūpaḥ'; iti bhāṣyamevānukṛtisūtre aānandamayobhyāsāt'; ityādāviva samanvetavyaśabdāderviṣṇuparatva eva heturnocye, kintvanirdeśyaṃ sukhamityatra samīpoktajñānisukhaparityāge heturucyate ityatra jñāpakaṃ, ṭīkāpi tadanusāriṇītyāhuḥ । tathā cāyaṃ siddhānte śrutyarthaḥ 
eko vaśī sarvabhūtāntarātmā ekaṃ rūpaṃ bahudhā yaḥ karoti ।
tamātmasthaṃ ye anupaśyanti dhīrāḥ ।
iti pūrvavākye aya eko'; jñānānandādyabhinnaḥ samābhyadhikaśūnyo vā yaḥ sarvamasya vaśe astīti asarvavaśī'; yaḥ asarvabhūtāntarātmā'; sarvaprāṇināmantarniyāmakaḥ aya ekaṃ'; svasvarūpaṃ bahudhā karoti niyamyānantyāt । ataṃ'; prakṛtam aātmasthaṃ'; jīvahṛdayasthitaṃ ye adhīrāḥ'; jñāninaḥ anupaśyantīti prakṛtā ye jñāninasteṣāmeva aśāśvataṃ sukhaṃ'; nityābhivyaktasaukhyaṃ netareṣām । anena brahmasāmarthyamuktaṃ bhavati । evaṃ anityo nityānām'; iti vākyamapi brahmamāhātmyaparatayā vyākhyeyam । atadetat'; ityādināpi prakṛtabhagavatsvarūpameva viśeṣataḥ pratipādyate iti । manyante ityasyottaratrānvayaḥ । tathā ca ayato vāco nivartante'; aeṣo asya parama ānandaḥ'; ityādau prasiddham anirdeśyaṃ paramaṃ sukhaṃ kathaṃ nu tadvijānīyāmiti manyante ityānukūlyena gṛhṇanti । jñānārthaṃ tadbhānaṃ vā prārthayante । akimu bhāti na bhāti vā'; iti tasya durjñeyatvaṃ ca vadanti jñāninaḥ । tat brahmaṇo rūpaṃ svarūpabhūtaṃ sukhametadekaṃ rūpaṃ bahudhā yaḥ karotītiprakṛteśvararūpābhinnamiti manyante jñānina iti । etacchabdasyeśvaraparatve api rūpaśabdasāmānādhikaraṇyāt napuṃsakaliṅgatopapattiḥ । taduktaṃ nyāyavivaraṇe ayadbrahmānirdeśyaṃ sukhamiti vadanti tadetatsvarūpamiti manyanta iti'; । kāṭhakabhāṣye tu tad aguhyaṃ brahma sanātanam'; ityupakrāntam । arūpaṃ rūpaṃ pratirūpo babhūva'; iti jīvasya pratibimbatvamuktam । rūpaśabdena prakṛtametat aekaṃ rūpam'; ityatra prakṛtaṃ ca bhagavadrūpam aanirdeśyam'; itthamiti sākalyena nirvaktumaśakyaṃ paramaṃ sukhamiti manyante jñānina iti sukharūpatvavidhiparatayā vyākhyātam । bhāṣye apyanirdeśyasukharūpa ityetāvanmātragrahaṇena śrutau sukharūpatvaṃ vidheyamiti sūcitam । tadanirdeśyaparamasukhātmakaṃ bhagavadrūpaṃ tatparasādamṛte kimu bhāti na bhāti veti samyagbhāti na bhātīti kathaṃ nvahaṃ jānīyāmiti śiṣṭavākyārthastatraivoktaḥ । vivṛtaṃ caidvyāsatīrthīye atat'; anirdeśyaparamasukhātmakaṃ bhagavadrūpaṃ tatprasādamṛte kimu samyagbhāti? na bhāti vāti? iti praśnottarabhūtam ekaṃ niścitārthaṃ akathamahaṃ vijānīyāṃ'; na kenāpi prakāreṇeti । atretiśabda ubhayānvayī । tathā ca kimu bhātīti praśnasyottarabhūtaṃ na bhātītivākyoktamekamajñeyatvarūpamarthamiti yojanā । kecittu yadevaṃ brahma tatprasādamṛte anu'; idānīṃ akathamahaṃ vijānīyām'; prārthanīyāṃ liṅ । na kathamapītyarthaḥ । jñānivākyānukaraṇametat । bhagavatprasādādapi kiṃ sākalyena tajjñānaṃ bhavatīti naciketā yamaṃ pṛcchati kimu bhātīti । uśabdaḥ samyagityarthe । tathātve samyagiti śeṣaḥ । uttaramāha yamaḥ na bhātīti । vāśabdoṣa'vadhāraṇe । na bhātyeveti vyākhyāti ।

na hi jñānisukhamanubhāti sarvaṃ, na ca tadbhāsā ।
nanu atameva bhāntam'; iti vākye sūryāditejasāṃ paramātmādhīnaprakāśakartṛtvasya atasya bhāsā'; itivākye ca sarvasya jagatastatprabhāprakāśyatvasya ca śravaṇena asiddhiparihāre kutastayorviṣṇutvasādhyenāvyabhicaritatvam, yena talliṅgadvayabalātsamīpoktajñānisukhapāmarśaparityāgaḥ syādityata āha na hīti । sarvamityubhayānvayī । bhātīti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yasmāt asarvaṃ'; sūryāditejaḥ jñānisukhamanusṛtya ana bhāti'; na prakāśate । tathā atadbhāsā'; tasya jñānisukhasya prakāśena asarvaṃ'; jagat ana bhāti'; na prakāśate cetyarthaḥ । vakṣyamāṇapramāṇavirodhāditi bhāvaḥ । caśabdaḥ samuccaye । ato na liṅgadvayamanyatrāvakāśavaditi vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

aahaṃ tattejo raśmīt'; iti nārāyaṇabhāsā hi sarvaṃ bhāti ।
astvetadubhayaṃ jñānisukhe anupapannam । tathāpyanena kutaḥ paramātmano grahaṇaṃ, asya paramātmatvasādhyasāmānādhikaraṇyāniścayādityatastatra dvitīyasūtrasthāpipadena sūcitāṃ śrutimāha ahamiti ।। ahamitītyanantaraṃ śruteriti śeṣaḥ । itiśabda ādyārthe । tena atameva bhāntamanubhāti sarvaṃ tasya bhāsā sarvamidaṃ vibhāti'; ityātharvaṇaśrutirapi gṛhyate । nārāyaṇeti । nārāyaṇādhīnabhāsetyarthaḥ । hiśabdo yata ityarthe, prasiddhau ca । asarvaṃ'; sūryāditejaḥ abhāti'; prakāśate । yadvā anārāyaṇabhāsā'; nārāyaṇīyabhāsā asarvaṃ'; jagat abhāti'; prakāśasya ityarthaḥ । aiti jñāyate'; iti śeṣaḥ । śrutau araśmīt'; ityanena sūryāditejasāṃ nārāyaṇādhīnaprakāśakartṛtvasya, atejaḥ'; ityanena sarvasya jagato nārāyaṇīyaprakāśaprakāśyatvasya coktatvāditi bhāvaḥ । aaham'; iti, śrutistvantarnaye vyākhyātā । anena taduktamityataḥ sūtre tadityanuvartate । tasyetyāvartate vipariṇamyate ca । asambhavāditi cānuvartate । tathā ca 
tadetaditi manyante anirdeśyaṃ paramaṃ sukham ।
kathaṃ nu tadvijānīyām ।
ityānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇaṃ tadetacchabdaparāmṛśyaṃ sukham anirdeśyaṃ sukhaṃ tattu viṣṇurūpameva, na samīpoktajñānisukham । kutaḥ? atasya'; sūryāditejasaḥ atasya'; ānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya sukhasya tasmin atameva bhāntam'; iti aanukṛteḥ'; anubhānaśravaṇāttasyaitadadhīnaprakāśakartṛtvaśravaṇādasyānyatejoniyantṛtvaśravaṇāditi yāvat । tathā tasya sarvasya jagatastasya tatprakāśaprakāśyatvasya atasya bhāsā'; iti śrutāvuktatvāttasya sarvajagatprakāśatvokteriti yāvat । tasya ca liṅgadvayasya aahaṃ tattejaḥ'; ityādiśrutyā smṛtyā ca tasminviṣṇāveva niścayenopapatterjñānisukhe ca aasambhavāt'; anupapatteḥ । tathā tasminnupasaṃhāre tasyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya ana tatra sūryo bhāti'; iti vākye tasya sūryādyaprakāśyatvasyacokteśceti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū oṃ ।
api smaryate ।
।
yadādityagataṃ tejo jagadbhāsayate akhilam ।
yaccandramasi yaccāgnau tattejo viddhi māmakam ।
yadetalliṅgadvayasya viṣṇuniṣṭhatvam aaham'; iti śrutyopapāditam । tatsmṛtyāpyupapādayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā tāṃ smṛtimudāharati apīti ।। iti smaryata ityanvayaḥ । ayat'; ādityādiṣu sthitaṃ tejastat amāmakaṃ'; madadhīnaṃ madīyaṃ ca, matteja evādityādiṣu prerakatvenāsti । tadevākhilaṃ jagat abhāsayate'; prakāśayatīti gītāsmṛtyarthaḥ ।

na tadbhāsayate sūryo na śaśāṅko na pāvakaḥ ।
yadgatvā na nivartante taddhāma paramaṃ mama ।
। iti anukṛtyadhikaraṇam । ।
kiṃ ca pāṭhake ana tatra sūryo bhāti na candratārakaṃ nemā vidyuto bhānti kuto ayamagniḥ'; ityādyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya sukhasya sūryādyaprakāśyatvamucyate । tacca viṣṇoreva smaryate, ato viṣṇureva atadetat'; ityatra pratipādyaḥ, na jñānisukhamiti sūtrasyārthāntaramapipadasya yuktisamuccayārthatvaṃ cābhipretya tāṃ smṛtimudāharati na taditi ।। atrāpītiśabdasya smaryata ityanvayaḥ । jñānino ayadgatvā'; yatprāpya punastasmānnanivartante, tanmama paramaṃ adhāma'; svarūpaṃ, tadetaddhāma sūryo ana bhāsayate'; na prakāśayate, evaṃ aśaśāṅkaḥ'; candraḥ । yadā caivaṃ tadā kuto ayamavamo agniriti gītāsmṛtyarthaḥ । anena pūrvavyākhyāne na kevalamanukṛtyādiḥ aahaṃ tattejaḥ'; iti śrutyantare atamevabhāntamanubhāti'; ityātharvaṇādau viṣṇudharmatvena śrūyate, kintu yadādityeti smaryatepīti śrutisamuccayārthe apiśabdaḥ । dvitīyavyākhyāne tu atameva bhāntamanubhāti'; ityuttaravākyoktānukṛtyādihetoḥ ana tatra sūryo bhāti'; iti pūrvavākyoktasūryādyaprakāśyatvahetośca samuccaye apiśabdaḥ । tathā ca na kevalaṃ atadetat'; ityatroktānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasya viṣṇutvarūpapradhānasādhye hetūkṛtamanukṛtyādikam aahaṃ tattejo raśmīt'; ityādau śrūyate, kintu yadādityeti smaryate apīti vā apiḥ । kiñca yato na kevalaṃ prathamasūtroktaliṅgadvayaṃ, kintu tato anyadapi ana tatra'; iti kāṭhakavākye tasyānukūlyena gṛhyamāṇasyoktaṃ sūryādyaprakāśyatvarūpaṃ liṅgaṃ tasya viṣṇoḥ sambandhitvenaiva ana tat'; iti smaryate । atastadetat akathaṃ nu tadvijānīyām'; ityatra viṣṇureva pratipādya iti vā sūtrasyārthadvayamuktaṃ bhavati । ana tatra'; ityāderayamarthaḥ । pūrvaṃ brahma na samyagbhātīti tasya durjñeyatvamuktaṃ, tatkuta ityataḥ idamucyate yasyaivaṃvidhaṃ sukhaṃ rūpaṃ atatra'; brahmaṇi sūryo ana bhāti'; tanna prakāśayatīti yāvat । candratārakamiti dvandvaikavadbhāvaḥ। evaṃ tat vidyuto api ana bhānti'; na bhāsayantīti । atameva bhāntam'; ityuttaravākyaṃ tu yadyapi vyāsatīrthakṛtātharvaṇaṭīkāyām aetatsamākhyārūpamātharvaṇavākyaṃ'; abhāntaṃ'; bhāsayantaṃ paramātmānamanusṛtyaiva sūryādayo abhānti'; prakāśate iti vyākhyātam । tathāpi ṭīkānusārāt asarvaṃ'; sūryāditejaḥ abhāntaṃ'; prakāśamānaṃ bhagavantamanusṛtyaiva abhāti'; prakāśate । atasya'; bhagavato abhāsā'; prakāśena aidaṃ sarvaṃ'; jagati abhāti'; prakāśyata iti vyākhyeyam । vyāsatīrthīyaṃ tu vyākhyānāntaraṃ ṭīkākṛdabhipretaṃ bhaviṣyatīti tadvirodhaḥ ।
। iti anukṛtyadhikaraṇam । ।

।
viṣṇureva jijñāsya ityuktam । tatra ūrdhvaṃ prāṇāmunnayatyapānaṃ pratyagasyati ।
madhye vāmanamāsīnaṃ viśve devā upāsate । 
iti sarvadevopāsyaḥ kaścitpratīyate ।
atrādhikaraṇer iśānanāmasamanvayaḥ kriyate । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayasaṃśayau ca sūcayati viṣṇureveti । jijñāsāsūtre viṣṇurevasarvairmumukṣubhirmokṣārthaṃ jijñāsya ityuktamityarthaḥ । na ca tatra jijñāsyatvāyogavyavaccheda eva kṛtaḥ, na tvanyayogavyavaccheda iti vācyam । anyasyāpi jijñāsyatve tasyāpi mokṣadātṛtvāpattyā ayato nārāyaṇaprasādamṛte'; ityādivivaraṇānupapatteranyayogavyavacchedasyāpi tatrābhipretatvāt । ato atraivakāra ubhayānvayitayā vyākhyeyaḥ । tataḥ kimityata āha tatreti । tatretyavyayaṃ tadityarthe api । tathā ca aathāto brahmajijñāsā'; iti yatpūrvaṃ viṣṇorjijñāsyatvamuktaṃ atatra'; jijñāsyatve atatrar'; aiśāno bhūtabhavyasya'; ityuktvā āmnāte aūrdhvam'; iti kāṭhakavākye akaścirt'; iśāno dharmitvena pratīyate । katham? yato ayaṃ asarvadevopāsyaḥ'; tairjijñāsyaḥ pratīyate ata iti vākyayojanā । na ca vāyoḥ sarvadevopāsyatve api na viṣṇossarvadevopāsyatvahāniriti vācyam । tāvatāpi sarvairmumukṣubhirviṣṇureva jijñāsya iti niyamasyāsiddheḥ । na ca śrutigataviśvedevaśabdasya gaṇaviśeṣavācitvāt sarvadevopāsya ityuktiranupapanneti vācyam । gaṇaviśeṣaparatve tasya guṇādhikyāsiddhyā sarvadevaparatvāvaśyaṃbhāvāt । anenar iśānaśabdasyānyaniṣṭhatvākṣepamukhena phalato mumukṣukartṛkajijñāsyatvasyānyaniṣṭhatvākṣepāt jijñāsādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiruktā bhavati । tatheśānākhyo viṣayaśca sūcitaḥ ।

sa ca aevamevaiṣa prāṇa itarān prāṇān pṛthakpṛthageva sannidhatte';
ayo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ'; 
akuvidaṅga'; ityādinā prāṇavyavasthāpakatvānmadhyamatvātsarvadevopāsyatvācca vāyureveti pratīyate ।
ato abravīt 
sū oṃ ।
śabdādeva pramitaḥ ।
।
vāmanaśabdādeva viṣṇuriti pramitaḥ ।
sayuktikaṃ pūrvapakṣayati sa ceti । atretthaṃ yojanā asa ca'; sarvadevopāsyaśceśāno vāyureva bhavet, na viṣṇuḥ । kutaḥ? atra prāṇavyavasthāpakatvaśravaṇāt । tathā madhyamatvokteḥ sarvadevatopāsyatvokteśca । na caiṣāṃ vāyvekaniṣṭhatvāsiddhiḥ । yato ayaṃ vāyuḥ aevamevaiṣa prāṇaḥ'; ayo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ'; akuvidaṅga'; ityādinā vākyena prāṇavyavasthāpakatvadimān pratīyate, ata iti । kāṭhake hi 
aṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣo madhya ātmani tiṣṭhatir ।
iśāno bhūtabhavyasya ।
ityanena bhagavato aṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ pūrṇaṣaḍguṇatvaṃ dehamadhyasthatvaṃ bhūtabhaviṣyadvartamāneśānatvamityādimāhātmyamabhidhāyeśānapadoktasya tasyaiva aūrdhvam'; ityādinā mahimāntaramucyate । tatra madhyaśabdaḥ siddhānte ūrdhvaṃpratyakchabdasamabhivyāhārāt deśaviśeṣavacanaḥ, natvavāntareśvaratvādirūpamadhyamatvārthakaḥ । tathā ca yaḥ prāṇākhyarūpeṇa aprāṇaṃ'; prāṇākhyavāyumūrdhvam aunnayati'; udgamayati ūrdhvagatimattayā prerayati । apānarūpī cāpānākhyaṃ vāyuṃ apratyak'; adhastādviṇmūtrādiniṣkāsanahetutayā aasyati'; nirasyati prerayatīti yāvat । taṃ adehamadhye'; hṛdaye aāsīnam'; upaviṣṭaṃ avāmanaṃ'; saundaryapradhānāḥ striyo vāmāḥ tāḥ netāraṃ viṣṇuṃ aviśve devāḥ'; sarve devāḥ aupāsate'; jijñāsanta iti siddhāntarītyā śrutyarthaḥ । pūrvapakṣī tvidaṃ vāyuparaṃ matvā madhyaśabdo ayo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ'; iti śrutyantarasamākhyānānmadhyameśvaratvavacano na deśaviśeṣavacana ityāha । aevam'; iti ṣaṭpraśnavākyaṃ ca ayathā samrāḍevādhikṛtānviniyuṅkte etāngrāmānadhitiṣṭhasveti'; iti dṛṣṭāntavākyena saha vyākhyeyam । tatprakārastu yathā asamrāṭ'; sārvabhaumaḥ aadhikṛtān niyogino adhikṛtya viniyuṅkte'; । katham? tvam aetān'; pāṭalīputrādīn grāmān aadhitiṣṭhasva'; tadādhipatyena tiṣṭhasveti । aevamevaiṣaḥ'; aātmata eṣa prāṇo jāyate'; ityātmajātatvenokto mukhyaprāṇaḥ aitarān'; bhinnān svajanyatvenopacāreṇātmapravibhāgān prāṇān vāyūn pṛthaksthāneṣu hṛdayādiṣu sthāpayatīti । ayo ayam'; ityādibṛhadāraṇyakavākyam । tatra hi pūrvaṃ vāgādīnāṃ mṛtyugrastatvamuktvā aathainameva nāpnot'; ityanena mukhyaprāṇasya tadanāttatvena tebhyaḥ śraiṣṭhyamabhidhāya ayo ayam'; ityanena prāṇaśabdavācyeṣu viṣṇuvāyutaditareṣu cetaneṣu triṣu viṣṇoruttamatvādanyeṣāmadhamatvādvāyormadhyamatvādasmānnimittādvā avāntareśvaratvādvā mukhyaprāṇasya sarvottamatvarūpakāṣṭhātvāvirodhimadhyasthatvamevocyate, na tu madhyadeśasthatvam । tathā tatraiva caturthādhyāye aayaṃ vāva śiśuḥ yo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ prāṇaḥ'; iti candrikodāhṛte vākye sthūladehākhyavistṛtapradeśagataliṅgaśarīrarūpagṛhe viṣṇurūpāyāṃ sthūṇāyām annākhyena śrīrūpeṇa dāmnā baddho govatsarūpovāyurmadhyamatvenocyate ।
kuvidaṅga namasā ye vṛdhāsaḥ purā devā anavadyāsa āsan ।
te vāyave manave bādhitāyāvāsayannuṣasaṃ sūryeṇa ।
iti ṛṅmantre aaṅga'; iti priyasambodhanam । tathā ca ye devāḥ vāyoḥ anamasā'; namaskāropalakṣitasevādinā avṛdhāsaḥ'; vṛddhā jñānādiguṇapūrṇāḥ aanavadyāsaḥ'; anavadyāḥ ajñānarāgādyavadyavidhurāśca purā sasūryā āsan । te akuvit'; kvacidrahasyasthāne sūryeṇa sākaṃ amanave'; jñānine abādhitāyā'; saṃsārakleśavadbhiḥ śaraṇaṃ prāptāya avāyave'; vāyumuddiśya auṣasam'; uṣa prakāśe, asun, buddhim aavāsayan'; tadviṣayāmakurvanniti śrutyarthaḥ ।
siddhāntayatsūtramavatārya vyācaṣṭe ata iti । avāmanaśabdāt'; vāmanaśruteḥ । evakāro vāyuliṅgasadbhāvāt vāyureveśānaḥ kiṃ na syāditi codyaparihārāya liṅgebhyaḥ śruteḥ prābalyamāha । yathoktaṃ sudhāyām evaśabdavyākhyānaṃ balavaditi aśabdādeva pramitaḥ'; iti yatheti । samanvayasūtrādanuvṛttasya tadityasyārtho viṣṇuriti । vidheyabhūtaviṣṇutvasyānvayayogyoddeśyadyotanāyetiśabdaprayogaḥ । āvartate cāyam । itiśabdātparamapi evaśabdo yojyaḥ । tenānuvṛttastu śabdo vyākhyātaḥ । tathā car aiśāno bhūtabhavyasya'; iti śrutar iśāno viṣṇureva bhavet । kutaḥ? yastatra pramito viṣṇāveva mahāyogavidvadrūḍhibhyāṃ prasiddho amadhye vāmanam'; itiśruto vāmanaśabdastasmādeveti yojanā । pramitapadaṃ śruterniravakāśatvasūcakam । anena sūtre itiśabdo adhyāhārya iti sūcitam । tathā car aiśāno bhūtabhavyasya'; itiśrutariśānaḥ atattu'; viṣṇureva bhavet । kutaḥ? yastatra viṣṇāveva pramito mahāyogavidvadrūḍhibhyāṃ prasiddho anyatra niravakāśo amadhye vāmanamāsīnam'; itiśruto liṅgātprabalo vāmanaśabdastacchrutistasmāditi sūtrārthaḥ ।

na hi śruterliṅgaṃ balavat ।
sūtre evakāraprayogena sūcitaṃ śruteḥ prābalyaṃ liṅgasya prābalyaniṣedhamukhena darśayati na hīti । hiśabdo vakṣyamāṇapramāṇavirodhāditi hetusūcakaḥ । tathā ca ahi'; yasmāt na śruterliṅgaṃ balavat, kintu durbalameva । tasmālliṅagāt prabalāt vāmanaśabdādeveśāno viṣṇurevetyarthaḥ ।

śrutirliṅgaṃ samākhyā ca vākyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ tathā ।
pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ balīyaḥ syādevamāgamanirṇayaḥ ।
kuto na śruterliṅgaṃ balavadityatastathāsati śruterliṅgātprābalyavacanavirodhāpatterityāśayena tadvākyaṃ paṭhati śrutiriti । iti skānda ityanantaraṃ vacanāditi śeṣaḥ । asya na hītyanenānvayaḥ । vācakaśabdaḥśrutiḥ । asādhāraṇadharmo vā, tadbodhakaśabdo vā liṅgam । nirṇītasyānyatra samānoktiḥ samākhyā । sā dvividhā arthataśśabdato apīti । samabhivyāhṛtapadairevākāṅkṣāpūrtau tacchāntyarthaṃ padāntaranirapekṣāṇi padāni vākyam । ekaprameyapratipādakānekavākyāni prakaraṇam । anuktasthānasamuccaye tathetiśabdaḥ । anekaprameyapratipādakamekārthatātparyayuktaṃ vacanaṃ sthānam । atra avākyaṃ prakaraṇaṃ sthānaṃ samākhyā ca tathāvidhā'; ityanuvyākhyānusāreṇa samākhyāyāḥ sthānānantaryameva grāhyaṃ, na tvatroktakramānusāreṇa vākyādyapekṣayā prāthamyam । atroktakramasyāvivakṣitatvāt । uktaṃ hi pramāṇalakṣaṇaṭīkāyāṃ samākhyāditvena grahaṇaṃ aśrutirliṅgaṃ samākhyā ca'; ityavivakṣitakramaṃ vākyamanusṛtyeti । ata eva jaiminiḥ aśrutiliṅgavākyaprakaraṇasthānasamākhyānāṃ samavāye pāradaurbalyamarthaviprakarṣāt'; iti smṛtyuktādanyathākramamāha pūrvaṃpūrvamiti । pūrvoddiṣṭamityarthaḥ । ekatra samavetaṃ viruddhamiti ca śeṣaḥ । abalīyaḥ'; atiśayena svabhāvato balavat yathātraivādhikaraṇe anantaroddiṣṭaliṅgāpekṣayā pūrvoddiṣṭā vāmanaśrutiḥ svataḥ prabalā। vākyāpekṣayā prabalaṃ liṅgam। yathā daharādhikaraṇe daharākāśasya sākṣātsarvādhāratvaprāpakāt akiṃ tadatra vidyate ubhe asmin dyāvāpṛthivī'; iti vākyātprabalaṃ viṣṇostatprāpakāpahatapāpmatvādikaṃ liṅgam । prakaraṇāpekṣayā prabalaṃ vākyam। yathā jyotirdarśanāt ityadhikaraṇe jīvasya ahṛdyantarjyotiḥ'; itivākyabodhyajyotiṣṭvasādhakājjīvaprakaraṇātprabalaṃ viṣṇorjyotiṣṭvaprāpakaṃ akatama ātmā'; iti praśnavākyam । sthānāpekṣayā prabalaṃ prakaraṇam । yathā samagropaniṣadar iśvaraparatvasādhakāt ṣaṭpraśnarūpasthānāt prabalam aātmata eṣa prāṇo jāyate'; ityetatkhaṇḍarūpaṃ mukhyaprāṇaprakaraṇam । ata evātrādhikaraṇe ṣaṭpraśnoktaprāṇavyavasthāpakatvādīnāṃ mukhyaprāṇaliṅgatvamupetya śrutyā bādha uktaḥ । samākhyāpekṣayā prabalaṃ sthānam । yathā annamayādiśabdānāṃ kośaparatvasādhakāt aannamayaprāṇamayamanomayavijñānamayānandamayā me śudhyantām'; iti nārāyaṇānuvākasamākhyāyāḥ prabalaṃ teṣāṃ viṣṇutvasādhakaṃ brahmaparānekaprakaraṇasandarbharūpaṃ sthānam । etānyeva śrutyādinār'thanirṇayasthalāni । ādyayā samākhyayā nirṇetavyaṃ yathā puruṣasūktasamākhyayā vaiśvānarasya viṣṇutvam । dvitīyayā yathā ambhraṇīsūktasamākhyayā viśvakarmasūktoktasyājasya viṣṇutvam । astvevaṃ tataḥ kimityata āha evamiti । viruddhaiteṣāṃ samavāye sati prabalena pūrveṇottarabādhe ca sati aāgamanirṇayaḥ'; āgamārthasya vipratipannasyaitaiḥ nirṇayo bhavatītyarthaḥ ।

tacca liṅgaṃ viṣṇoreva । tasyaiva prāṇatvokteḥ atadvai tvaṃ prāṇo
abhavaḥ'; iti ।
nanvastu śruteḥ svabhāvataḥ prābalyam । tathāpi bāhulyena pūrvapakṣyuktaliṅgānāmapi prābalyātsāmyenānirṇaya evetyata āha tacceti ।। liṅgamiti samudāyaikavacanam । tathā ca atat'; pūrvavādyuktaṃ liṅgajātaṃ tu viṣṇoreva yuktam, na vāyorityarthaḥ । tathā ca bāhulye api liṅgānāṃ sāvakāśatvāttebhyaḥ śruterekasyā api niravakāśāyāḥ prābalyānnānirṇaya iti bhāvaḥ । nanu na liṅgaṃ viṣṇau sāvakāśaṃ, pūrvapakṣyudāhṛtasamākhyārūpaśrutyantareṇa tasya prāṇaniṣṭhatayaivoktatvādityata āha tasyaiveti । atadvai tvam'; iti śrutau atasya'; viṣṇoḥ prāṇatvasya prāṇaśabdavācyatvasyokteruktatvādityarthaḥ । evaṃ aata eva'; ityatrādhyātmikāśeṣaśabdasya samanvayaṃ bruvatā tathā aśāstradṛṣṭyā'; ityatrāntaryāmiparatvaṃ bruvatā sūtrakāreṇetaravyāvṛttyā tasyaiva prāṇatvokteḥ sādhitatvādityapi vyākhyeyametat । tathā ca śrutyantare prāṇaniṣṭhatayā liṅgasyoktāvapi na tadvirodhaḥ । tasya prāṇasya viṣṇutvābhyupagamāditi bhāvaḥ । nanu tathāpi akuvidaṅga'; iti ṛci vāyuniṣṭhatayā liṅgoktestadvirodha ityasyāpīdamevottaram । asmin pakṣe prāṇatvamiti vāyutvamupalakṣyate । tathā cāntarnaye ādhidaivikāśeṣaśabdasamanvayaṃ bruvatā sūtrakāreṇa atasyaiva'; viṣṇoreva aprāṇatvokteḥ'; vāyuśabdavācyatvarūpavāyutsyoktatvādityarthaḥ । tathā ca na tadvirodhopīti bhāvaḥ । na ca siddhānte api sthānāpekṣayā prabalātprakaraṇāt aevamevaiṣaḥ'; itiśrutyantaragataprāṇaśabdasya, tathā ayo ayaṃ madhyamaḥ'; ityasya, tathā akuvidaṅga'; iti mantrasthavāyuśabdasya mukhyavāyuparatvaṃ, tatroktaliṅgānāmapi tatparatvamupetya teṣāṃ śrutyā bādhasyoktatvāt kathaṃ śrutyantarasthaprāṇavāyuśabdayoḥ viṣṇuparatvāṅgīkāreṇa samādhānam । ata eva candrikāyām madhyamaśabdo api aūrdhvaṃ prāṇam'; iti prāṇasya sthānāntaranirdeśāttatyāgena madhyamasthānasthabrahmaparaḥ, na tu śrutyantare madhyamaśabdoktaprāṇapara ityuktam । ataḥ aevamevaiṣaḥ'; iti vākyaṃ sthānātprakaraṇasya prābalye udāhṛtamiti vācyam । uktarītyā mukhyataḥ śrutyantaragataprāṇaśabdāderbrahmaparatvena liṅgānāṃ tattadantaryāminiṣṭhatve api samākarṣanyāyenānyaparatvasyāpyaṅgīkārāt । śrutyantaroktaliṅgānāmanyaniṣṭhatve api vā nānupapattiḥ । na caivaṃ kāṭhakoktaliṅgānāmapyanyaniṣṭhatvāpattyā anyeṣāmīśānatvādyāpattiḥ । niravakāśaśrutyā kāṭhakoktaliṅgānāṃ viṣṇuniṣṭhatānirṇayopapatteḥ । nanu tathāpi kathamīśāno viṣṇurbhavecchrutāvīśānasyāṅguṣṭhaparimitatvokteḥ । sarvagate ca harau tadayogāt । na ca vyomavatsarvagatasyāpyaṇutvaṃ yujyata iti pratipāditamiti vācyam । tathāpi aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ'; iti tanmātraparimāṇatvokterayogāt । na ca aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ'; ityatra śrutaḥ parimāṇārthako mātracpratyaya eva, na tvavadhāraṇārthako mātraśabdaḥ । adehāṅguṣṭhamito dehe jīvāṅguṣṭhamito hṛdi'; iti smṛtau mita ityanena parimāṇasyaivokteḥ । tathā ca nānupapattiriti vācyam । tathātve aṅguṣṭhamātratvābhidhātryām aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ'; iti śrutau amadhya ātmani'; ityasya smṛtau hṛdītyasya ca vaiyarthyāpātāt । tanmātraparimitatvoktyarthaṃ hi tatra hṛdayarūpasūkṣmasthānoktiḥ । tasmādavadhāraṇārthakamātraśabda evāyamaṅgīkāryaḥ uktaṃ hi candrikāyām mātraśabdasyāvadhāraṇārthakatvāditi ।

sū oṃ ।
hṛdyapekṣayā tu manuṣyādhikāratvāt ।
।
sarvagatasyāpi tasyāṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ hṛdyavakāśāpekṣayā yujyate ।
tathā ca sarvagate harāvaṅguṣṭhamātratvoktiranupapanneti nātreśāno viṣṇurityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya tadakṣarāṇi vyācaṣṭe hṛdīti । sarvagatasyāpītyanena tuśabdo yadyapitathāpītyarthatayā vyākhyātaḥ । hṛdyapekṣayetyanena sūcitahetoranvayayogyaṃ sādhyaṃ darśayati tasyeti । yojanā tu yadyapi viṣṇuḥ sarvagatastathāpi atasyāṅguṣṭhamātratvam'; aṅguṣṭhamātratvoktiryujyate । katham? yato ahṛdyavakāśopekṣayā'; hṛdi vidyamāno yo ayamavakāśo aṅguṣṭhaparimitadeśastadapekṣayā tatrābhivyaktatāvatparibhitabhagavanmūrtiviśeṣamapekṣya tasya viṣṇoraṅguṣṭhamātratvam astyata iti। yadvā ahṛdyavakāśāpekṣayā'; hṛdi vidyamānāvakāśamapekṣya tatsambandhāttasyāṅguṣṭhamātratvavacanaṃ yujyata ityāvṛttiṃ vinā yojanā । prathamapakṣe śaktyāparimite api bhagavati mūrtiviśeṣe vyaktyātmanāṅguṣṭhamātratvasya sthānini brahmaṇi tatsambandhādupacāreṇoktiriti bhedaḥ । atra ṭīkāyāṃ hṛdyavakāśāpekṣayeti bhāṣyaṃ sāvadhāraṇaṃ kṛtvā sautratuśabdo avadhāraṇatayā vyākhyātaḥ । tena viṣṇoṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ hṛdyapekṣayaiva, na tu lokavatparicchinnatvādityuktaṃ bhavati । tattatsthāneṣu vyaktamūrtiviśeṣāpekṣayā vā upacāreṇa vā tattatparimāṇatvoktyā ayastvetameva prādeśamātram'; iti chāndogye aprādeśamātraṃ puruṣam'; ityanyatra aprādeśaḥ puruṣottamaḥ'; ityaparatra ca hṛdgatasya viṣṇoḥ prādeśaparimitatvokteḥ । aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣo aṅguṣṭhaṃ ca samāśritaḥ'; iti śrutyantare aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣaḥ'; iti kaṭhavalyāṃ ca aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ puruṣaḥ'; ityaparatra cāṅguṣṭhaparimitatvokteḥ aaṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakaḥ'; iti kvacidaṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakatvoktervirodha iti codyaṃ parihṛtaṃ bhavati । dehe hṛdayākāśe prādeśaparimitarūpaviśeṣasya hṛdayagatakamalakarṇikāmūlagatākāśe aṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakarūpāntarasya karṇikāgragatākāśecāṅguṣṭhaparimitarūpāntarasya ca vyaktisambhavāt, tattatsthānadharmasya sthāninyupacaritatvasambhavācca । yathoktaṃ bṛhadāraṇyakabhāṣye 
hṛdaye sarvaśo vyāpī prādeśaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ।
jīvānāṃ sthānamuddiṣṭaḥ sarvadaivasanātanaḥ ।
hṛtkarṇikāmūlagataḥ so aṅguṣṭhāgrapramāṇakaḥ ।
mūleśa iti nāmāsmin sarve jīvāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।
aṅguṣṭhamātre puruṣe karṇikāgrasthite harau ।
prāviśanti suṣuptau tu prabudhyante tatastathā ।
asmin mūleśavyāpinormadhye aṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ ca dehe dehāṅguṣṭhamitatvaṃ jīvahṛdi jīvāṅguṣṭhamitatvamiti vivektavyam । atra aaṅguṣṭhaṃ ca samāśritaḥ'; ityanena karmendriyādhiṣṭhitatvamucyata iti prameyadīpoktamapi jñātavyam । nanu adakṣiṇākṣimukhe viśvo manasyantastu taijasaḥ'; ityādivacanājjāgradādyavasthāprerakaviśvataijasaprājñānāṃ dakṣiṇākṣyādiṣu sattvaṃ tāvatsiddham । yadi caivaṃ tadā jīvo api jāgradavasthāyāṃ dakṣiṇākṣisthaḥ svapne kaṇṭhadeśasthaḥ suptau hṛdayastho bhavati, ahṛdayasthātparājjīvo dūrastho jāgradeṣyati'; ityukteḥ । dūrastho akṣistho jāgrajjāgratvamiti tasyārthaḥ । tathā ca kathaṃ hṛdayavyāptaprādeśaparimitabhagavadrūpasya sarvadā jīvasthānatvam? kathaṃ ca hṛtkarṇikāmūlagatabhagavadrūpe sadā pratiṣṭhito jīvaḥ? suptau hṛtkarṇikāgragate harau praviśatītyuktiriti cet na, yatassarvadā hṛdi sthitameva jīvasvarūpaṃ jāgaritādāvakṣyādiṣvapi viśeṣasannihitaṃ dīpaprakāśavadityaṅgīkṛtam । yathoktamaitareyabhāṣye hṛde sthitameva tasya rūpaṃ jāgarite apyakṣyādiṣu viśeṣasannihitaṃ bhavatīti । ekasyaiva jīvasya sthāpanadhṛtyākhyapratiṣṭhāpanasuptiprāpaṇākhyaprayojanabhedādekadehe anekadhā sthitānāṃ bhagavanmūrtīnāṃ śaktyā sarvagānāmapi tatra tatra vyaktyātmanā anekālpaparimāṇavattvaṃ ca yujyata iti na kācidanupapattiḥ ।

itaraprāṇināmaṅguṣṭhābhāve api manuṣyādhikāratvānna virodhaḥ ।
। iti vāmanādhikaraṇam । ।
nanu tathāpi nāṅguṣṭhaparimāṇavattvaṃ viṣṇoryuktam । tathā hi kiṃ tattadaṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ vā yatkiñcidaṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ vā । nādyaḥ, paśvādīnāmaṅguṣṭhābhāvena tadantargatasya viṣṇoraṅguṣṭhaparimitatvāyogāt । na dvitīyaḥ, aṅguṣṭhamātratvoktestaistaistathopāsanārthatvena tasya cāṅguṣṭhavyaktiviśeṣanirdhāraṇa vināyogena yatkiñcidaṅguṣṭhamātratvoktervyarthatvāt । pipīlikādihṛdayasthe aṅguṣṭhamātratvasābhānyasyāpyasambhavāccetyāśaṅkāṃ pariharan manuṣyādhikāratvāt itisūtraśeṣaṃ tuśabdasya kākākṣinyāyena atrāpyanvayaṃ tasyāpyarthatvaṃ ca abhipretya tatsambandhipradarśanapūrvakaṃ vyācaṣṭe itareti । paśvādīnāmityarthaḥ । apirāvartate । aṅguṣṭhamātratvamityetat vipariṇāmevānuvartate । ana virodhaḥ'; iti virodhasūtrādākṛṣṭe pade । tathā ca aapi'; tattadaṅguṣṭhaparimitatvāṅgīkāre apītaraprāṇināmaṅguṣṭhābhāve api na viṣṇoraṅguṣṭhamātratvasya virodhenāṅguṣṭhamātratvokterasambhavaḥ । kutaḥ? aṅguṣṭhamātratvokteretadvidyāyā amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; manuṣyānadhikṛtya pravṛttatvāt । tadapi kutaḥ? vedavidyopāsanasya amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; manuṣyamātrādhikāratvāditi yojanā । sūtre bhāṣye ca manuṣyāṇāmadhikāro yasmin athavā adhikriyate atretyadhikāra upāsanaṃ śāstraṃ vā, manuṣyāṇāmeva adhikāro manuṣyādhikārastasya bhāvasatasmāditi vigrahaḥ । amanuṣyādhikāritvāt'; itipāṭhe manuṣyā adhikāriṇo yasmin tattathoktam । tathā ca manuṣyādhikārikatvādityarthaḥ । manuṣyapadaṃ ca vakṣyamāṇanyāyena mananādiśīlacetanaparam । tena devānāṃ jaritāryādīnāṃ vakṣyamāṇanyāyena vedavidyādhikāriṇāmetadvidyādhikārasiddhiḥ । tatra jaritāryādīnāṃ svasvāṅguṣṭhaparimitatvena bhagavadupāsanāsambhavāt, teṣāmetadvidyotpannavākyārthajñāna evādhikāro, nopāstāvapi । ata eva ṭīkāyāṃ manuṣyāṇāmeva vedavidyopāsanādhikāritveneti manuṣyatvaṃ vyāpakatvenoktam । na cānadhikāriṇāṃ paśvādīnāṃ dehasthitasya bhagavato aṅguṣṭhaparimitatvābhāve parimāṇāntarānukteradravyatvāpattiriti vācyam । paśvādidehagatasya paramātmanaḥ tattadākārayuktatvena tadanusāriparimāṇavattvāt । yathoktamaitareyabhāṣye saṅkarṣaṇaśca pradyumnastadākārau nṛṣu sthitau ।
nārāyaṇāniruddhau tu paśvākārau paśusthitau ।
anena sūtre tuśabdo apyarthevadhāraṇe ca । tatrāpyarthasyobhayatrānvayaḥ । aṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ yujyata iti śeṣaḥ । taditi pradhānasūtrādanuvṛttasyeha vipariṇāmenānvayaḥ । na virodhaḥ ityasyākarṣaḥ । atasya manuṣyādhikāritvāt'; ityāvartate । tathā ca atu'; api sarvagatasyāpi atasya viṣṇoraṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ'; taduktiryujyate । yato atra ahṛdyapekṣayā tu'; hṛdyavakāśāpekṣayaiva aṅguṣṭhamātratvamucyate, na tu paricchinnatvāt । tacca mūrtiviśeṣe tanmātratvasya sattvādupacāreṇa vā yujyate । na ca nāṅguṣṭhamātratvaṃ viṣṇoryuktaṃ, yatkiñcidaṅguṣṭhamātratvoktervyarthatvenāsambhavena ca tattadaṅguṣṭhamātratve vācye tasya ca paśvādīnāmaṅguṣṭhābhāvena tadantargataviṣṇāvayogāditi vācyam । yataḥ atu'; api itaraprāṇināmaṅguṣṭhābhāve api na viṣṇostattadaṅguṣṭhamātratvasya avirodhaḥ'; asambhavaḥ । kutaḥ? aṅguṣṭhamātratvavacanasya yadbodhakavidyāyāḥ amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; manuṣyānevādhikṛtya pravṛttatvāt । tadapi kutaḥ? atasya'; vedavidyopāsanasya amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; manuṣyamātre adhikāratvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।
। iti vāmanādhikaraṇam । ।

।
manuṣyāṇāmeva vedavidyādhikāra ityuktam ।
asminnadhikaraṇe devānāṃ brahmavidyādhikāraḥ samarthyate । prāsaṅgikatvānnādhyāyapādasaṅgatī mārgaṇīye । śrutyādisaṅgativiṣayasaṃśayatadbījāni darśayati manuṣyāṇāmiti । auktaṃ'; pūrvasūtre । tuśabdārthāvadhāraṇasya samāsapraviṣṭamanuṣyapadenāpi sambandho astīti bhāvena manuṣyāṇāmevetyanuvādaḥ । netareṣāmityevaśabdārthaḥ । avedavidyādhikāro'; vedavidyopāsanādhikāraḥ । anena devatādhikārābhāvamukhena aviśve devā upāsate'; ityādipūrvodāhṛtaśrutyupalakṣitāśeṣaśrutiprāmāṇyasyākṣepātpūrvādhikaraṇenāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ vedavidyādhikārākhyo viṣayaścokto bhavati । aaṅguṣṭhamātraḥ'; iti śrutimūlāyāḥ amanuṣyāṇāmeva'; ityukteḥ aviśve devā upāsate'; iti śruteśca koṭidvayopasthāpakatvena sandehabījatvāttaduktyaiva devānāmadhikāro asti uta nāstīti saṃśayo, nāstīti pūrvapakṣaśca sūcitaḥ ।

tiryagādyapekṣayaiva manuṣyatvaviśeṣaṇamuktaṃ, na tu devādyapekṣayetyāha 
tataḥ kimityatassaṃśayabījaṃ vighaṭayan siddhāntayituṃ sūtramavatārayati tiryagādīti । viśiṣṭabuddhyādirahitatiryagādivyāvṛttyarthamityarthaḥ । manuṣyatvaviśeṣaṇaṃ sāvadhāraṇatvenābhipretam । manuṣyapadam auktaṃ'; prayuktaṃ, tatreta śeṣaḥ । pūrvasūtra iti tadarthaḥ । svaprayuktaivakāravyāvarttyaṃ darśayati na tviti । adevādyapekṣayā'; devādivyāvṛttyartham । tuśabdo viśeṣārthaḥ । na tu devādyarthamapītyapiśabdārtho vā । aityāha'; ityabhipretya sūtrakāro devānāmadhikārabhāvamāhetyarthaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
taduparyapi bādarāyaṇaḥ sambhavāt ।
।
tadupari manuṣyāṇāṃ satāṃ devāditvaprāptyupari । sambhavati hi teṣāṃ viśiṣṭabuddhyādibhāvāt ।
tatsūtraṃ paṭhati taduparīti । atra taduparīti sādhyadharmisūcakaṃ padamanūdya teṣāṃ tasmāttasyā iti vigrahāśrayeṇa vyācaṣṭe taduparīti । vedavidyākāra ityanuṣajyate । na kevalaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ satāṃ, kintu taduparyapītyaperarthaḥ । tathā ca ateṣāṃ'; manuṣyāṇāṃ satāṃ devatāpadayogyānāṃ jīvānāṃ padaprāpteḥ pūrvaṃ manuṣyaśarīraṃ prāptānāṃ satāṃ atasmāt'; manuṣyatvāt aupari'; manuṣyaśarīrāpagamena atasyā upari'; devopadevādipadaprāpteruparitanakāle api devabhāvamāpannānāmapi vedavidyādhikāro astyeveti yojanā । kuta ityatastaddhetutayā sambhavāditi hetuṃ vyācaṣṭe । ahi'; yataḥ । avedavidyādhikāraḥ'; ityatrāpi sambadhyate । ateṣāṃ'; devānām । adhikārasambhavo api kuta ityato atrāpi sambhavādityetadevāvṛttya hetutayā yojayati viśiṣṭeti ।। teṣāmityatrāpyanvīyate । tathā ca ateṣāṃ'; yogyamanuṣyāṇāṃ vidyākarmabhyāṃ devāditvaprāptimatāṃ asambhavāt'; viśiṣṭabuddhyādibhāvādarthagrahaṇānuṣṭhānopayuktabuddhiviśeṣādisadbhāvādityarthaḥ । arthitvasāmarthye ādipadena grāhye । na cārthitvābhāvaḥ ityatrāpi teṣāṃ sambhavati hītyeva hetuḥ । vidyābhisteṣāṃ mokṣasiddhiḥ sambhavati hīti tadarthaḥ । anena sūtre tadityāvartate । manuṣyaparāmarśi cedaṃ buddhisthaparāmarśi ca। apiḥ samuccaye । adhikāra iti buddhyā vivicyātrānveti । anadhikārādhikārābhidhāyakajaiminibādarāyaṇoktirūpavipratipattisūcanāya bādarāyaṇapadam । tattvapradīparītyā tātparyajñāpanārthamadhikārādhikyajñaptidārḍhyārthaṃ ca bādarāyaṇaḥ svayameva vaktītyāha iti vā । sambhavāditi cāvartate । tathā ca yato na kevalaṃ devādipadayogyajīvānāṃ padaprāpteḥ pūrvaṃ bhūmau kiñcitkālaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ satāṃ tasyāṃ daśāyāmeva adhikāraḥ, kintu ataduparyapi'; tasmānmanuṣyatvādupari tadatyayena tābhyāṃ vidyākarmabhyāṃ tasyāḥ devāditvaprāpteruparitanakāle api devabhāvamāpannānāmapi vedavidyāyāmadhikāro astyeva । na ca tatkāraṇābhāvaḥ । asambhavāt'; adhikāropayogino viśiṣṭabuddhyādesteṣu sambhavāt । na ca devādīnāṃ viśiṣṭabuddhisāmarthyasadbhāve apyarthitvābhāvādadhikārābhāva iti vācyam । kutaḥ? asambhavāt'; vidyāsādhyajñānamokṣayorarthitvasambhavāditi bhagavān bādarāyaṇo manyata iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

tiryagādīnāṃ tadabhāvādabhāvaḥ । teṣāmapi yatra viśṣṭabuddhyādibhāvastatrāvirodhaḥ ।
nanu na devā vedavidyādhikāriṇaḥ, tathā sati sūtre amanuṣyamātravyāvartakamanuṣyapadaprayogena tiryagādivadamanuṣyatvānna devā vedavidyādhikāriṇa ityanumānasūcanāttadvirodhāpatterityata āha tiryagādīnāmiti । ādipadena sthāvarāṇi mūḍhamanuṣyā vā gṛhyante । atadabhāvāt'; viśiṣṭabuddhyāderabhāvāt aabhāvaḥ'; tasya vedavidyādhikārasya । anenādhikārābhāve viśiṣṭabuddhyādirāhityasya prayojakatvoktyā paroktāmanuṣyatvahetoḥ sopādhikatvaṃ sādhyavyatirekasādhakopādhivyatirekākhyapratipakṣagrastatvaṃ coktaṃ bhavati । sautramanuṣyapadaṃ ca mananādiśīlaparaṃ sat viśiṣṭabuddhyādirahitameva cetanaṃ vyāvartayati, na tu martyabhinnamātramiti na tadvirodha iti bhāvaḥ । nanu viśiṣṭabuddhyādirāhityamupādhiḥ । tiryakṣu adhikārābhāvarūpasādhyāvyāpakatvāt । ata eva na tadabhāvo api sādhyavyatirekaheturityata āha teṣāmapīti । apirubhayatrānveti । tatrādyassamuccaye । adhikāra iti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca na kevalaṃ devānāṃ, kintu ateṣāṃ'; tiraścāmapyadhikāre api na virodhaḥ nanu kathamavirodhastiryakṣu sarvatra vedādhikāre mānavirodhāpātādityata āha teṣāmapīti ।। tiraścāṃ madhye apītyarthaḥ । ayatra'; yeṣu viśiṣṭabuddhyarthitvākhyarāgādibhāvaḥ tatsattvaṃ tatraivādhikāre aavirodho'; mānāvirodhaḥ । bādho na sarvatretyarthaḥ । anenāpinā sautro apiśabdo jaritāryādisamuccāyakaśceti sūcitam । yadāha tattvapradīpikākāraḥ ateṣāmapītyādirapipadavyākhyā'; iti । ānandamālākāro api atiryañco api kecidapiśabdagṛhītāḥ'; ityāha । tathā ca manuṣyabhinneṣvapi tiryakṣvadhikārasadbhāvādvyabhicārādadhikārābhāve nāmanuṣyatvaṃ hetuḥ, kintu viśiṣṭabuddhyādirāhityamevāvyabhicārāt । ato bhavatyeva sa upādhiḥ । ata eva sautramanuṣyapadasya vyāvarttyasaṅkoco api yukta iti bhāvaḥ ।

niṣedhābhāvāt । dṛśyante hi jaritāryādayaḥ ।।
nanu kathaṃ tiraścāmapyadhikāre apyavirodhaḥ । teṣāmadhikāraniṣedhasya taddarśanasya vā virodhitvādityāśaṅkya nādya ityāha niṣedheti ।। teṣāmityatrāpi sambadhyate । adhikāre ityādau saṃyojyam । tena niṣedharāhitye sati viśiṣṭabuddhyādimattvamevādhikāre prayojakam, na kevalaṃ yena śūdrādau vyabhicāraḥ syāditi sūcitam । na dvitīya ityāha dṛśyante hīti । vedādhikāritayeti śeṣaḥ । hiśabdo bhāratādiprasiddhisūcakaḥ । ata eva bhārate 
evamukto bhrātṛbhistu jaritārirvibhāvasum ।
tuṣṭāva prāñjalirbhūtvā yattacchṛṇu narādhipa ।
ityādinā jaritārisārisṛkkastambamitradroṇākhyeṣu pakṣiṣu madhye jaritāriragrajaḥ svabhrātṛbhirasmānmocayeti prārthitaḥ aayamagne jaritā'; ityāgneyasūktenāgniṃ stutvā khāṇḍavavanadahane svabhrātṝnagnidāhādamocayaditi pratipāditam । yata ityarthe vā hiśabdaḥ । atra jaritāryādaya ityeva pāṭho yuktaḥ, na tu jaritaryādaya iti hrasvayuktapāṭhaḥ, bhāratavirodhāt, tattvapradīpavirodhācceti dhyeyam । dṛśyante hītyanena devā vedavidyādhikāriṇaḥ niṣedharāhitye sati viśiṣṭabuddhyādimattvāt tādṛśamartyavaditi siddhāntyabhimatānumāne manuṣyatvopādhirnirasto bhavati । jaritārau ādiśabdagṛhītasārisṛkkādau ca sādhyāvyāpaktavāt ।

sū oṃ ।
virodhaḥ karmaṇīti cennānekapratipatterdarśanāt ।
।
manuṣyā eva devādayo bhavantīti taduparītyuktam । tatra yadi manuṣyāḥ santo devādayo bhavanti tatpūrvaṃ devatābhāvāddevatoddiṣṭakarmaṇi virodha iti cet 
devānāṃ vedavidyādhikārasiddhyarthaṃ taduparītyanenoktaṃ sāditvamākṣipya samādadhatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā'kṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe virodha iti । devādipadayogyā jīvāḥ pūrvaṃ bhūmau kiñcitkālaṃ manuṣyāḥ santa eva atha devādayo bhavantītyarthaḥ । na tu manuṣyabhāvaṃ vinetyevaśabdārthaḥ । ityuktamiti ।। atroktamityanantaraṃ tadayuktamiti śeṣaḥ । kuta ityatastatpakṣe bādhakoktiparaṃ virodha ityaṃśaṃ sahetukaṃ vyācaṣṭe tatrayadīti । yadītyārabhya bhavantītyantaṃ pūrvavākyārthānuvādastasyāpādakatvapradarśanārthaḥ । tatretyavyayaṃ tarhītyarthakaṃ bhavantītyataḥ paraṃ yojyam । yadvā manuṣyā eva devādayo bhavantītyantaṃ pūrvavākyārthānuvādastasyāpādakatvapradarśanārthaḥ । tatretyavyayaṃ tarhītyarthakaṃ bhavantītyataḥ paraṃ yojyam । yadvā manuṣyā eva devādayo bhavantītyuktyā prāptābhedaśaṅkāṃ vārayituṃ manuṣyā evetyādisvapadāni varṇayati tatreti । yadvā tatra devatoddiṣṭakarmaṇīti sāmānādhikaraṇyam । atra pakṣe yadīti śravaṇāttarhīti labhyate । bhavantītyanantaramityuktamityasti । ubhayatrādipadenopadevādayo gṛhyante । karmapadaṃ śabdasyāpyupalakṣakam । tathā ca yadi pūrvaṃ manuṣyāḥ santo apyatha devādayo bhavantītyuktamityucyate, tarhi atatpūrvaṃ'; tebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ teṣāṃ devādipadaprāpteḥ pūrvaṃ sādhakatvāvasthāyāṃ adevatābhāvāt'; devatāyā asattvāt yena karmaṇā devāditvaṃ sādhyamityuktam, atatra'; tasminneva adevatoddiṣṭakarmaṇi'; pūrvakalpe devatoddeśena pravṛttakarmaṇi devatāvācakaśabde ca avirodhaḥ'; tayorvaiyarthyamiti yojanā । uddeśyābhāvādvācyābhāvācceti bhāvaḥ ।

na, anekeṣāṃ devatāpadapratipatterdarśanāt । ate ha nākaṃ mahimānassacante । yatra pūrve sādhyāssanti devāḥ'; iti ।
parihārāṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe neti । yojanā tu na karmaṇi virodha, kutaḥ? yato na pūrvaṃ devatābhāva iti । teṣāṃ pravāhato anāditvenaitaddevānāṃ pūrvamabhāve api devatāntarasadbhāvāditi bhāvaḥ । na ca tatra pramāṇābhāva ityataḥ prāptamaneketyaṃśaṃ pratipattiśabdasya jñānārthatvabhramaṃ vārayan tatsambandhipradarśanapūrvakaṃ vyācaṣṭe anekeṣāmiti ।। atehanākam'; iti śrutau aanekeṣām'; ekaikagaṇaśo anantānāṃ devatvādiyogyamanuṣyāṇāṃ vidyākarmabhyāṃ pūrvapūrvadevatāpadaprāpterdarśanādityarthaḥ ।
anenataduparītyatroktaṃ devānāṃ sāditvamayuktaṃ, tathā sati yena karmaṇā devāditvaṃ sādhyamityuktam, tatra karmaṇi śabde ca virodhastasya vaiyarthyaṃ syāt tatpūrvaṃ devatābhāvāditi cet na, yato na pūrvaṃ devatābhāvaḥ । tatkatham? etaddevānāṃ pūrvamabhāve api devāntarasadbhāvāt । na ca tatra mānābhāvaḥ । aanekapratipatterdarśanāt'; anekeṣāṃ yogyamanuṣyāṇāṃ pūrvapūrvapadaprāpteḥ ateha nākam'; ityatroktatvāditi sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । śrutau ayajñena yajñamayajanta devāḥ । tāni dharmāṇi prathamānyāsan'; iti pūrvavākye prakṛtāḥ devāstacchabdena gṛhyante । haśabdaḥ punararthe prasiddhau vā । tathā ca ye adevāḥ'; devatvayogyāḥ manuṣyā jñānakarmātmakena ayajñena'; ayajñaṃ'; viṣṇum aayajanta'; apūjayan । tatastena jñānapūrvakakarmaṇā devapadaṃ prāpya aprathamāni'; prathamāḥ mukhyāḥ adharmāṇi'; dharmāḥ lokadhārakā āsan । amahimānaḥ'; mahātmānaḥ mahimaguṇātmakā vā । ate'; devāḥ aha'; punaḥ anantaraṃ svādhikārāvasāne anākaṃ'; kaṃ sukhaṃ tadanyat duḥkhamakaṃ, tanneti nākaṃ, nañdvayena pūrṇasukhātmakamiti labhyate । evaṃbhūtaṃ mokṣaṃ asacante'; āpnuvan । laṅarthe laṭ । laṅvā, etvāḍabhāvau chāndasau । ayatra'; mokṣe apūrve'; pūrvakalpe muktāḥ asādhyāḥ'; bahuvacanamādyarthe ।
ṛjavo brahmamukhyā hi suparṇaśśeṣa eva ca ।
sarasvatī suparṇī ca vāruṇī sādhyanāmakāḥ ।
ityuktāḥ sādhyādayo devāḥ santīti śrutyarthaḥ । na ca vasurudrādityamarutsādhyeṣu vasūnāmāditvāt ṭīkāyāṃ vasvādidevā iti vaktavyam, na tu sādhyādīti । ata eva tattvapradīpe apūrve sādhyāḥ vasvādayo devāḥ pūrvasiddhā muktā vā'; ityuktamiti vācyam । sādhyaśabditānāṃ prādhānyena kramollaṅghanāt । chandogaśrutikramānusāreṇa tattvapradīpapravṛtteḥ। na caivaṃ vyākhyāne puruṣārthādhikaraṇe asyāḥ prāptapadevatāparatvenodāharaṇānupapattiriti vācyam । ye padaṃ prāpya jagaddhārakā abhūvan te devā yajñena yajñamayajanta te ha nākaṃ mokṣagatātiśayaṃ sacante iti śruterarthāntaravivakṣayā tadupapattestadanusāreṇa taṭṭīkāyāṃ vyākaraṇasyāpyupapatteśca ।

sū oṃ ।
śabda iti cennātaḥ prabhavātpratyakṣānumānābhyām ।
।
avācā virūpa nityayā'; ityādiśruterāptyaniścayānnityatvāpekṣatvācca mūlapramāṇasya ।
yaddevānāmadhikārasiddhyartham ādyantavattvamuktaṃ taduparyaneketyābhyāṃ, tadākṣipya samādadhatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā'kṣepāṃśaṃ tāvadvyācaṣṭe śabda iti । anekapratipatterdarśanānna virodha ityādyanuṣajyate । yaditarhyerapyanuṣaṅgaḥ । tathā cetthaṃ yojanā yadyanekeṣāṃ pūrvapūrvamuktyā devatāpadaprāpterdarśanānna karmaṇi virodha iti ucyate, tarhi tatraiva śabde darśanapadokte vede aprāmāṇyākhyo virodhaḥ syāt । kutaḥ? devānāmanityatvāt । aneketyādinā devānāmanityatvasyāntavattvasyoktatvāt । nanu devānāmanityatve api vedānāmaprāmāṇyaṃ kuta ityataḥ taduditānāmityāha । hetugarbhaviśeṣaṇametat । anenānityadevavācakatvāditi hetuḥ sūcitaḥ । nanu devānāmanityatve api na tadvācakavedasya vācyahīnatvarūpāprāmāṇyaṃ prasajyate, devavadvācakavedasyāpyanityatvena kadāpi vācyahīnatvābhāvādityata uktaṃ vedasya nityatvāditi । vedasya nityatvameva kuta ityata uktaṃ vāceti । śruterityasya vedasya natyatvādityanenānvayaḥ । jñānopalakṣakaṃ caitat । ādiśabdena anityayānityayā'; anityā vāva śrutiḥ'; ityādikaṃ gṛhyate । nanu na nityo vedaḥ । na ca śrutivirodhaḥ, śruterbahukālīnatvarūpanityatvārthakatvenopacaritārthatvādityato apyāha । tathā sati vedasyānityatvādaprāmāṇyākhyavirodhaḥ syāditi । nanu vedasyānityatve apyāptimūlatvena prāmāṇyaṃ sambhavatītyata āha āptyaniścayāditi । vedakarturiti śeṣaḥ । tathā ca kartuḥ sārvajñādau mānābhāvena vedakartuḥ sārvajñādirūpāptyaniścayādityarthaḥ । yadvā astu vā kartaryāptiniścayaḥ, tathāpi na vede tanmūlatvaniścaya ityāha āptyaniścayāditi । tathā ca vedasyāptapraṇītatvarūpāptimūlatvāniścayādityarthaḥ । tasmānmānābhāvenāptitanmūlatvāniścayādvedānityatve tatprāmāṇyābhāvāpatteḥ na nityatvaśruterupacaritārthatvaṃ vācyamiti bhāvaḥ । na kevalaṃ śrutervedanityatvasiddhiḥ, kintu pariśeṣānumānādapītyāha nityatveti ।। mūlapramāṇasya nityatvāpekṣatvādvedasya nityatvāvagamādityanvayaḥ । ayaṃ bhāvaḥ prāmāṇyasiddhyarthaṃ vedasyāptapraṇītatve mūlapramāṇena bhāvyaṃ, pauruṣeyasya mūlapramāṇasāpekṣatvaniyamāt । anyathānāśvāsādyajñādeḥ puṇyasādhanatādibodhakaṃ vedamūlaṃ ca bhavatpratyakṣānumānayorasambhavātpariśeṣādvākyameveti vācyaṃ, tasya cānityatāmupetya mūlānveṣaṇe anavasthāpattyā nityatvameva vācyaṃ, tato varaṃ vedasyaiva nityatvāṅgīkaraṇaṃ, śrutisiddhatvāditi ।

svataḥ prāmāṇyaprasiddheśca nityatvādvedasya taduditānāṃ
devānāmanityatvāt ।
nanu yathā vedānityatve āptyaniścayātprāmāṇyābhāvāpattirbādhikā, tathā tasya nityatve apyāptoktatvarūpaguṇajanyatvābhāvena prāmāṇyābhāvāpattiriti samaṃ bādhakamityata āha svata iti । vedasyetyanuvartate । tathā ca avedasya'; vedajanyajñānagatayāthārthyarūpaprāmāṇyasya asvata eva'; jñānasāmānyakāraṇādeva aprasiddheḥ'; upapatteḥ pramitatvādityarthaḥ । yadvā vedagatayathārthajñānakaraṇatvarūpakaraṇaprāmāṇyasya asvata eva'; jñānakaraṇatvasahajaśaktyabhinnayathārthajñānajanakatvaśaktirūpatvenaiva pramitatvādityarthaḥ । asyāpi vedasya nityatvasambhavādityanenānvayaḥ । tathā ca vedasya nityatvasya siddhatvāttadvācyadevānāmanityatve vācyahīnatvarūpāprāmāṇyāpattiriti bhāvaḥ ।

punaranyabhāvaniyamābhāvācca śabde virodha iti cet 
nanvatītakalpe ekadevatābhāve devatāntarasadbhāvādyathā karmaṇyuddeśyābhāvanimitto virodho nāsti, tathātrāpyekadevatānāśe api punaranyadevatotpattisambhavānna vācyahīnatvākhyo virodha ityata āha punaranyabhāvaniyamābhāvācceti। pūrvakalpīyanāśānantaramityānantaryārthe punaśśabdaḥ । uttarakalpa ityarthe vā । anyabhāvaḥ anyotpattiḥ । tasya niyame pramāṇābhāvādityarthaḥ । atītadevatāpravāhe tu pramāṇamastīti vaiṣamyamiti bhāvaḥ । anenottarakāle devatābhāvavirodhaḥ karmaṇyapi samāna iti sautraśabdaśabdena karmāpyupalakṣaṇīyamityuktaṃ bhavati । na caivamatrāpi virodhapadākarṣaṇamiti ṭīkavirodhaḥ । atadupari'; itisūtrādaperanukarṣokteḥ tasya ca na kevalaṃ śabde uttarakāle devatābhāvavirodhaḥ, karmaṇyapītyetadarthakatvāditi vācyam । ākarṣaṇaśabdasyānvayārthatvamāśritya na kevalaṃ pūrvasūtre virodhapadānvayaḥ, kintvetatsūtre apīti ṭīkārthāṅgīkāreṇa apivirodhapadayorākarṣaṇamityarthānabhyupagamāt । astu vā dvandvaḥ, tathāpi nānupapattiḥ, apeḥ svarūpanityatvābhāve apītyarthābhyupagamena karmasamuccayārthatvānabhyupagamāt । ata eva ṭīkāyāṃ devānāṃ svarūpanityatvābhāve apītyuktiḥ । atra nityatvasādhakayoḥ śrutyanumānayoḥ samuccaye ekaścaśabdaḥ । anityatvabādhakasya nityatve tadabhāvasya ca samuccaye anyaḥ । anityatvānyabhāvaniyamābhāvayoḥ samuccaye apara iti vivekaḥ ।
atasmai nūnamabhidyave vācā virūpa nityayā ।
vṛṣṇe codasva suṣṭutim'; 
iti ṛgyajurmantrārthastu na vilakṣaṇatvādhikaraṇaṭīkāyāmuktaḥ । tatra yadyapi virūpeti svātmānaṃ prati sambodhanamityukteḥ viṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāyāṃ virūpākhyaṛṇessambodhanamityukteśca virodho bhāti । tathāpi virūparṣikartṛkaṃ svāntaryāmisambodhanamiti tadarthābhyupagamānna virodhaḥ । uktaṃ hi tattvapradīpe prerayeti prārthanaṃ virūpasya ṛṣerantaryāmiviṣayamiti । virūpakartṛkaṃ taduddeśyakaṃ sambodhanamiti pakṣe api svātmaśabditasvajīvaṃ pratisambodhanamiti ṭīkārthābhyupagamānna virodhaḥ । asmin pakṣe tattvapradīpoktaṃ vyākhyānāntaraṃ bhaviṣyati । na ca padmanābhatīrthakṛtaviṣṇutattvanirṇayaṭīkāyāṃ nyāyaratnāvalyāṃ dharmeṇa virūparṣiṃ pratyetaducyata ityuktatvāttadvirodha iti vācyam । prathamaṃ yamadṛṣṭasya mantrasyānantaraṃ virūpeṇāpi dṛṣṭatvasambhavena tadā svasambodhanasambhavenāvirodhāt । tathā ca he virūpa abhito dyauḥ prakāśo yasyāsāvabhidyuḥ, tasmai avṛṣṇe'; varṣiṇe atisamarthāyeti vā । tattvapradīparītyā vṛṣā śreṣṭhastasya caturthī vṛṣṇe iti vā । tasmai bhagavate enamuddiśya anūnaṃ'; niścitaṃ anityayā'; anādinidhanayā vedalakṣaṇavācā asuṣṭutiṃ'; śobhanāṃ stutiṃ acodasva'; preraya kurvityarthaḥ ।

na, asūryācandramasau dhātā yathāpūrvamakalpayat'; 
yathaiva niyamaḥ kāle surādiniyamastathā ।
tasmānnānīdṛśaṃ kvāpi viśvametadbhaviṣyati ।
ityādeḥ, ata eva śabdātteṣāṃ prabhavaniyamāt mahatāṃ pratyakṣāt ।
parihārāṃśaṃ vyākhyāti neti । tathā ca vedasya vācyahīnatvaprayuktāprāmāṇyākhyavirodho netyarthaḥ । kuta ityataḥ prāptaṃ prabhavāditi hetuṃ tatsambandhipradarśanapūrvakaṃ pravāhataḥprabhavaniyamaparatayā ca vyācaṣṭe teṣāṃ prabhavaniyamāditi । ateṣāṃ'; vedavācyadevānāṃ aprabhavasya'; pravāhatautpatteḥ aniyamāt'; pratikalpaṃ niyamenotpatteriti yāvat । tathā ca devānāṃ svarūpeṇa nityatvābhāve api pravāharūpeṇa nityatvānna tadvācakavedāprāmāṇyamiti bhāvaḥ । nanu pramāṇābhāvādasiddho heturityataḥ prāptamataḥśabdamanūdya sāvadhāraṇatvena vyācaṣṭe ata eva śabdāditi । ko asau śabda ityato yasminvirodhaḥ śaṅkitastasmādeva, nānyasmādaprakṛtādityāśayena tadudāharati sūryetyādinā । śruto asmin kalpe apīti śeṣaḥ । nanūtpādakābhāva ityato apyāha ata eveti । akāravācyāt śrutyuktāddhāturviṣṇoreva, nānyasmādityarthaḥ । asmin pakṣe ataśśabdāditi vyākhyānāntaram । nanvakalpayaditi laṅyogādiyaṃ śrutiratītaviṣayaiva, ato na devaprabhavaniyamaṃ pramāpayatītyato apyāha ata eveti । tathā ca dhātā yathā pūrvakalpe sūryācandramasāvakalpayat tathāsminkalpe apīti pratikalpaṃ śrutyā kathane devānāṃ sarvakalpeṣu prajananākhyasadbhāvasiddheradhyāhāraṃ vinā ataevaśabdāt buddhisthāt yathaiveti spaṣṭaśrutyantarācca teṣāṃ sarvakalpeṣu prabhavasiddhernoktacodyāvakāśa iti bhāvaḥ । nanu śrutāvupacāreṇāpyuktiḥ sambhavatīti na tayā devaprabhavaniyamaniścaya ityataḥ prāptaṃ pratyakṣetyaṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe mahatāmiti । atītānāgatavidāmityarthaḥ । asyāpi teṣāṃ prabhavaniyamādityanenānvayaḥ । nanu parapratyakṣasyāpratyakṣatvāttadaniścaya ityatopyāha mahatāṃ pratyakṣāditi ।
yathartuṣvṛtuliṅgāni nānārūpāṇi paryaye ।
dṛśyante tāni tānyeva tathā bhāvā yugādiṣu ।
ityādirūpāt amahatāṃ'; bhāratācāryāṇāṃ apratyakṣāt'; pratyakṣavacanādityarthaḥ । asmin pakṣe apratyakṣāt'; niścitātpratyakṣādityanvayaḥ ।

yathedānīṃ tathoparyapi devā bhaviṣyantītītareṣāmumānācca ।
nanvayogināṃ śrutipratyakṣayoraviśvāsena teṣāṃ devaprabhavaniścayābhāva ityataḥ prāptamanumānetyaṃśaṃ vyācaṣṭe yatheti । idānīntanakāle yathā devāssanti tathoparibhāvikāle api devā bhaviṣyantītītareṣāṃ mahadbhyo anyevāmayogināmanumānādityarthaḥ । asyāpi prabhavaniyamādityanenānvayaḥ । caśabdaḥ prabhavaniyame, śabdapratyakṣānumānākhyapramāṇatrayasamuccaye vakṣyamāṇayuktyantarasamuccaye ca । anumānākārastu uparitanakālo devavān apralayakālatvāt idānīntanakālavaditi । anena devānāmadhikārasiddhyarthaṃ yadyādyantavattvamabhyupagamyate, tarhi pūrvasūtre yadbalātpūrvapūrvadevatāpravāhasyānāditvamuktaṃ, tasmin aśabde'; avācā virūpa nityayā'; ityādiśrutau nityatayā siddhe vede karmaṇi cottarakalpe vācyoddeśyahīnatvarūpāprāmāṇyākhyo virodhaḥ syāditi cet na, kutaḥ? aprabhavāt'; devānāṃ sarvakalpeṣu prabhavaniyamānnityamenopapatteḥ । teṣāṃ pravāhato nityatvāditi yāvat । na cotpādakābhāvaḥ । aato'; viṣṇoreva prabhavāt । aato'; adhātā yathāpūrvam'; itiprakṛtācchabdācchruteḥ ayathā'; iti spaṣṭaśruteśca । tathā mahatāmatītānāgatakālavidāṃ yogināṃ apratyakṣāt'; ayatharturṣu'; iti pratyakṣavacanāt jñāpitāt mahatāmatītānāgatakālayordevaprabhavaniyamagrāhipratyakṣāt । tathā mahadbhyaḥ itareṣāmayogināmanumānācca tatsiddheriti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । ayathaiva'; iti śrutyarthastu yathā pūrvayugātyaye kalpātyaye vā punaryugakalpāntarotpattiriti kāle prabhavaniyamaḥ, tathā surāderdevopadevādeḥ pūrvapūrvakalpātyaye punaranyabhāvaniyamo asti । yathoktam 
sa hi viśvasṛjo vibhuśambhupurandarasūryamukhānaparānaparān ।
sṛjatīḍyatamo avati hanti nijaṃ padamāpayati praṇatānsudhiyā ।
iti । pratikalpamiti śeṣaḥ । tasmātpūrvakalpa ivottarakalpe api pūrvakalpasadṛśasarvotpattiniyamādeva atasmāt'; viṣṇossakāśādetadviśvaṃ akvāpi'; kadāpi aanīdṛśaṃ'; pūrvapūrvavisadṛśaṃ devatāprabhavaśūnyaṃ na bhaviṣyati, kintu tatsadbhāvopetameva bhaviṣyatīti । yadvā aetat'; cetanācetanātmakaṃ viśvamanīdṛśaṃ na bhaviṣyati, kintu nāmarūpābhyāmīdṛśameva bhaviṣyatītyarthaḥ । tattvapradīpe tviyaṃ śrutiḥ ayathaiva kālaniyamaḥ'; iti vyatyāsena paṭhitā ।

sū oṃ ।
ata eva ca nityatvam ।
।
ata eva śabdasya nityatvādeva ca devapravāhanityatvaṃ yuktam ।
yuktyantareṇa devapravāhasya nityatāṃ sādhayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe ataeveti । tasya vyākhyānaṃ aśabdasya'; vedasya nityatvādeveti । evakāreṇa na devapravāhanityatve yuktyantaraṃ gaveṣaṇīyaṃ, kintu yatpūrvapakṣiṇā vedanityatvaṃ sapramāṇakamuktaṃ, tata eva tadanyathānupapattyaitatsidhyatīti sūcayati । nityatvādevetyupalakṣaṇaṃ, pramāṇasya sādhitatvenāprāmāṇyābhāvādevetyapi ataḥśabdavyākhyānaṃ draṣṭavyam । anyathā pūrvapakṣī aprāmāṇyenānyathopapattiṃ brūyāt devapravāhasya । yuktamiti ca sūtraśeṣoktiḥ । ayuktaṃ'; vedanityatvānyathānupapattyākhyayuktisiddham । caśabdastu samuccetavyayuktīnāṃ śabdātpratyakṣādanumānādityanena darśitatvāttatsamuccayārthakatayār'thādvyākhyātaḥ । ataeva pūrvasūtrabhāṣye caśabdaḥ saṃyojitaḥ । atrāpi bhāṣye caśabdena ca tadvācyadevatāsvarūpasyaiva nityatvena anyathopapattiḥ । ataeva asūryācandramasau'; ayathaiva'; ityādyudāhṛtaśrutereva ayamapyeti bhuvanaṃ sāmparāye'; ayatprayantyabhisaṃviśanti'; ityādi bahulaṃ pralayaśruteśca sūryādidevānāmutpattināśāvagamāt, ataeva svarūpanityatvāyogena pravāharūpeṇaiva teṣāṃ nityatvāvaśyaṃbhāvādityādiṭīkoktārthaḥ sarvo api saṅgṛhītaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
samānanāmarūpatvāccāvṛttāvapyavirodho darśanātsmṛteśca ।
।
atītānāgatānāṃ devānāṃ samānanāmarūpatvātparāptapadānāṃ
muktyā'vṛttāvapyavirodhaḥ ।
nanu na devānāṃ pravāhanityatvenāpi vedaprāmāṇyopapattiḥ । tathā hi kiṃ pūrvakalpe muktā eva devā uttarakalpe punarāvartante, tadanye vā । nādyaḥ । mukterapunarāvṛttitvāt । na dvitīyaḥ । tathātve dharmibhūtadevānityatvahetukavirodhābhāve api nāmarūpādidharmavaicitryakṛtavirodhaprāpteḥ, vācakavedasya pratikalpaṃ pāṭhabhedābhāvenaikavidhatvāt, anyathā nityatvavyāghātāt । vācyadevānāṃ ca nānāvidhanāmarūpavattvādityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtramupanyasya vyācaṣṭe samāneti । atrātītapadaṃ prācīnaparam । anāgatapadaṃ ca tadanyabhaviṣyadvartamānaparam । dharmipratiyogyubhayasamarpakametat । nāma indrādi, rūpam ākṛtiḥ । sūtrānusārādatrāpi caśabdaḥ saṃyojyaḥ । samānadharmakarmavattvācceti tadarthaḥ ।
svapadeṣvati śeṣaḥ । muktyā'vṛttāvapītyuktiḥ pūrvapakṣyāśaṅkitavirodhe hetusūcanārthā । yadyapitathāpītyarthe apiśabdaḥ āvartate । tathā cetthaṃ yojanā aprāptapadānāṃ'; prācīnānāṃ devānāṃ amuktyā'; prāptamuktitvena kāraṇena punasteṣāmeva svapadeṣu aavṛttāvapi'; asattve api tadanyeṣāṃ tatra satve api ca aavirodhaḥ'; ma tadvācake ekavidhe api śabde vede aprāmāṇyākhyo virodhaḥ । kutaḥ? vācyānāmapyatītānāgatānāṃ devānāṃ parasparaṃ asamānanāmarūpatvāt'; samāne ekavidhe nāmarūpe yeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ, teṣāṃ bhāvastattvaṃ tasmāditi । candrikāyāṃ tu sūtre bhāṣye ca tattvapradīpānusārādāvṛttāviti vicchedaṃ bhāṣye muktyāvṛttāvityasyaikapadyaṃ cāśritya ekasya padaprāptāvanyasya muktiḥ, punastasya muktau punaranyasya padaprāptiriti krameṇa mukterāvṛttāvapīti vā, svasvapadasyāvṛttāvapīti veti ṭīkānuktaprakāradvayenāpyāvṛttāvityaṃśo vyākhyātaḥ ।

ayathāpūrvam'; iti darśanāt ।
nanu sarvadevānāṃ samānanāmarūpatve pramāṇābhāvādasiddho heturityataḥ prāptaṃ darśanādityaṃśaṃ vyākhyāti yatheti । adhātā yathāpūrvam'; iti śruterityarthaḥ ।

anādinidhanā nityā vāgutsṛṣṭā svayambhuvā ।
ṛṣīṇāṃ nāmadheyāni yāśca vedeṣu dṛṣṭayaḥ ।
vedaśabdebhya evādau nirmame sa maheśvaraḥ । ।
nanvetacchrutestattatsvarūpakalpanāniyamaparatvamapi sambhavatīti nānayā samānanāmarūpatvaniścayo bhavati। kiṃ ca devapravāhasya nityatve teṣāṃ samānanāmarūpatve vā na tadvācitvena nityavedaprāmāṇyopaptiḥ, tadvācitvasyaivāsambhavāt । na hyapauruṣeyasya vedasyaitāvatkālamayaṃ devo mayoktaḥ, ataḥ paramenaṃ vakṣyāmīti vimṛśya vṛttiḥ sambhavatītyataḥ prāptaḥ smṛterityaṃśa ityāśayena tāṃ darśayati anādīti । nityatvokterupacaritatvavāraṇāya anādinidhanetyuktam । ato na paunaruktyam । ata eva tattvapradīpe anādinidhanatvena nityā, na tvanidhanatvamātreṇetyuktam । bahukālīnatvena vetspi draṣṭavyam । vedeṣvityanantaramuktā iti śeṣaḥ । nirmame ityasyāvṛttiḥ । tenāpyevaśabdasyānvayaḥ । tathā ca aādau'; sṛṣṭikāle asvayambhuvā'; svatantreṇa maheśvareṇa viṣṇunā aanādinidhanā nityā'; ādyantaśūnyatayaiva nityā, na tūpacāreṇa bahukālīnatāmātreṇānidhanatvamātreṇa nityā । yā avāk'; vedarūpā autsṛṣṭā'; uccāritā । atadvedaśabdebhyaḥ'; vedagatebhyaḥ tebhyaḥ śabdebhya eva, nānyebhyaḥ, asaḥ'; maheśvaro viṣṇuḥ aṛṣīṇāṃ'; brahmādivibudhānāṃ anāmadheyāni nirmame'; tāneva śabdān teṣu saṅketitavān pratikalpamayaṃ śabdo atra śakta iti jñāpitavān । ayāśca'; ṛṣīṇāṃ devānāṃ vedeṣūktāḥ dṛśyante iti dṛṣṭayo rūpāṇi, tāśca tāni ca tathaiva pūrvakalpīyarūpasādṛśyenaiva nirmame iti smṛtyarthaḥ । darśanātsmṛterityanayoḥ samānarūpatvādityanenānvayaḥ । āgamopalakṣakaṃ caitat । tathā ca nāsiddhiriti bhāvaḥ । anena prācīnānāṃ devānāṃ muktyā punaḥ svapadeṣvavṛttāvapi tadanyeṣāṃ tatra vṛttāvapi na tadvācake ekavidhe api śabde aprāmāṇyākhyo virodhaḥ । kutaḥ? prācīnānāṃ tadanyeṣāṃ cānyonyaṃ asamānanāmarūpatvāt'; tadyogyakarmadharmavattvācca । na ca hetvasiddhiḥ । adarśanāt'; ayathā pūrvam'; iti śruteḥ aanādinidhanā'; iti smṛteśceti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati । atra tattvapradīpe pralaye kasyāpi devasyābhāvena tadā vedasya vācyahīnatvarūpāprāmāṇyamāśaṅkya bhagavanmātraviṣayatvena tadupapattiriti samādhānamabhipretya aśabde'; kadāpi vācyahīnatvakṛto virodhaḥ aprāmāṇyam । kutaḥ? mukhyavācyasya viṣṇoḥ sarvadā vidyamānatvāt । kuta etat? aata eva'; śabdātteṣāṃ devānāṃ prabhavaniyamādikarturapīśasya sadā sattvāvagamāt। pratyakṣaścāsau mahatām। kutaḥ? aataeva'; apuruṣamīhate'; akavayo vayanti'; ityādiśrutereva itareṣāmanumānācca । yathā yena prakāreṇedānīṃ devā bhavanti tathānyadāpītyanumānācca tadavagamaḥ । evam aataeva'; śabdanityatvādeva pravoḍhurnityatvam । tathā viṣṇossamānanāmarūpatvādanyeṣāṃ tadabhāvācca aavirodhaḥ'; na tasya sarvaśabdavācyatvavirodhaḥ । samānāni sadṛśāni nāmāni yeṣāṃ rūpāṇāṃ tāni tathoktāni, tādṛśāni rūpāṇi yasya sa tathoktaḥ tasya bhāvastasmāt । na hi viṣṇvanyarūpāṇāṃ sadṛśanāmarūpatvaṃ, śabdapravṛttihetuvaikalyāt । na cātra mānābhāvaḥ, ayathāpūrvam'; iti darśanāt । yathā pūrvaṃ pūrṇajñānaḥ sarvasvatantraḥ sarvanāmarūpasthitastathaiva sa dhātā sūryādīnakalpayaditi śruteḥ । ataḥ sūryādikḷpteḥ prāgapi pralaye śabdaprāmāṇyāvirodha iti siddhamiti । idamevābhipretya ṭīkāyāṃ ana ca'; ityādinā śaṅkottare darśite । aatītaviṣayatvasya ca'; iti parihārottaraṃ cābhihitam ।

sū oṃ ।
madhvādiṣvasaṃbhavādanadhikāraṃ jaiminiḥ ।
।
avasūnāmevaiko bhūtvā'; ityādinā prāpyaphalatvātprāptapadānāṃ devānāṃ madhvādividyāsvanadhikāraṃ jaiminirmanyate ।
nanu na devānāṃ vedavidyādhikāro yuktaḥ । tathā hi dvividhā vedavidyāḥ muktiphalārthāstaditaraphalārthā iti । mokṣetaraphalā api dvividhāḥ । brahmakarmavidyābhedāt । tatrādyā yathā madhuvidyā । dvitīyā yathā agniṣṭomavidyā । tatra na tāvaddevānāṃ mokṣetaraphalakadvividhavidyāsvadhikāro yujyate, tatsādhyānāṃ mokṣetaraphalānāṃ madhye keṣāñcidyogyānāṃ prāptatvena ayogyānāṃ ca prāptumaśakyatvena arthitvābhāvāditi jaiminimatāvalambenākṣipatsūtramunyasya vyācaṣṭe madhvādiṣviti । prathamādipadena śiṣṭavākyaṃ, tathā adevo bhūtvā devānapyeti'; iti vājasaneyavākyaṃ, tathā asa ūrjamupagacchati'; iti śrutyantaravākyaṃ, dvitīyamadhuvidyāntgataṃ arudrāṇāmevaiko bhūtvā'; ityādikaṃ ca gṛhyate । prāpyaphalatvāt aprāpyaphalatvādityubhayathā vicchedaḥ । asyobhayatrānvayaḥ । vasvādipadānāmiti śeṣaḥ । tatrādipadena devarudrādipadānāṃ grahaṇam । yadvā prāptapadānāmityatratyaṃ padānāmityetadbuddhyā vivicyātra dharmitvena sambadhyate । prāptapadānāmiti bahuvrīhiḥ, karmadhārayaśca । tatrādyo hetugarbhaviśeṣaṇarūpaḥ । dvitīyasyobhayatrānvayaḥ । devānāmiti sūtre adhyāhṛtaṃ padaṃ, prakaraṇalabdhaṃ vā । madhuśabdo amadhu'; ityupakramyāmnātaprathamadvitīyādyamṛtavidyāparaḥ । atrādiśabdena vasvādipadaphalakakarmavidyā vājasaneyoktavāgādividyāśca gṛhyante । asambhavāditi sautro heturatrāpi saṃyojyaḥ । tadupapādakoktyaiva taduktirbhavatīti tasya sākṣādanuktiḥ । yadvā prāptapadānāmaprāpyaphalatvādityuktyaiva tasyoktatvādasambhavāditi na saṃyojyam । tathā cetthaṃ bhāṣyayojanā madhvādividyāsu aasau vā ādityo devamadhu'; iti prastutyāmnātena asa etadevāmṛtaṃ veda vasūnāmevaiko bhūtvā agninaiva mukhenaitadevāmṛtaṃ dṛṣṭvā tṛpyati'; ityādivākye apadānāṃ'; vasvādipadānāṃ aprāpyaphalatvāt'; madhvādividyāsūktopāsanāprāpyaphalatvaśravaṇāt aprāptapadānāṃ ca'; vasvādidevānāṃ prāptasvasvapadatvena aasambhavāt'; tadarthitvāsambhavāt adevānāṃ'; devaiḥ prāptapadānāṃ punastaiḥ aaprāpyaphalatvāt'; aprārthyaphalatvāditi vā । dvitīyavidyādyamṛtavidyāphalānāṃ rudrādipadānāṃ ca vasvādidevānām aaprāpyaphalatvāt'; prāptumayogyaphalatvāt tatrāpyarthitvāsambhavātteṣāṃ madhvādividyāsu aanadhikāram anadhikārābhāvaṃ jaiminirmanyata'; iti । jaiminigrahaṇena āptatamena jaimininaivaṃ matatvācca na teṣāmadhikāra iti yuktyantaraṃ sūcyate । anena amadhvādiṣu'; aasau vā ādityo devamadhu'; ityādimadhuvidyāsu devānām aanadhikāram'; anadhikārābhāvaṃ jaiminirmanyate tasmāddhetoḥ aasambhavāt'; taistadvidyāsūktaphalānāṃ madhye keṣāñcidyogyānāṃ prāptatvena keṣāñcitprāptumayogyatvena teṣāṃ tatrārthitvāsambhavāditi āptatamo jaiminirmanyata iti sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।
chāndogye hi aasau vā ādityaḥ'; ityanena ādityasya viṣṇoḥ paramānandatvena madhutvamuktvā asa etat'; ityādinā madhuśabditasya bhagavata ādityamaṇḍalasya pūrvadakṣiṇapaścimottarordhvaraśmiṣu sthitānāṃ prathamāmṛtādiśabdapañcakavācyavāsudevasaṅkarṣaṇapradyumnāniruddhanārāyaṇākhyapañcarūpāṇāṃ madhye prācyāditattaddiksthataiḥ tattatpadayogyairvasurudrādityamarutsādhyapadoktaṛjurūpapañcagaṇasthairdevaiḥ krameṇa agnivāyvindrasomaviriñcapradhānakaiḥ agnyādimukhenaikaikopāstau kṛtāyāṃ tadaparokṣajñānajanitatatprasādadvārā vasvādipadaprāptistattadgaṇasthānāṃ bhavatītyucyate । tathā ca ayaḥ'; adhikārī aetat amṛtaṃ'; vāsudevākhyaṃ rūpam aevam'; uktaprakāreṇa aveda'; asa ca vasūnāmapyeko bhūtvā'; vasubhogyadeśakālādhipo bhūtvā aagninā mukhena'; tatprādhānyena tadupadeśeneti yāvat । aetadevāmṛtaṃ'; vāsudevākhyaṃ adṛṣṭvā'; sākṣātkṛtya atṛpyati'; mukto bhavatītyarthaḥ । evaṃ ayo'; devatvayogyo adhikārī vākprāṇacakṣuḥśrotramanohṛdayanāmakaṃ brahmopāste sa devatvamapyeti tato adevo bhūtvā'; svottamadeveṣu sāyujyaṃ prāpya devān śvetadvīpagatabhagavadrūpaviśeṣān caturmukhabrahmaṇā sahāpyeti । so adhikārī aūrjam'; annam aupagacchati'; yatheṣṭaṃ prāpnoti iti śrutyantarārthaḥ ।

sū oṃ ।
jyotiṣi bhāvācca ।
।
jyotiṣi sarvajñatve bhāvācca । ādityaprakāśe antarbhāvavattajjñāne
sarvavastūnāmantarbhāvāt । nityasiddhatvācca vidyānām ।।
nanu māstu mokṣetaraphalavidyāsu adhikāro devānāṃ, tathāpi asatyaṃ jñānamanantaṃ brahma'; ityādimokṣārthavidyāsvadhikāro bhaviṣyati, tatrārthitvasambhavāt ityāśaṅkāṃ pariharatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe jyotiṣīti । jyotiṣīti sūtrapadānuvādaḥ । tasya vyākhyānaṃ sarvajñatva iti । yadyapi jñāne iti vyākhyeyaṃ, tathāpi viṣayāviśeṣitajñānasyānirūpyatvāt, yatkiñcidviṣayake jñāne viṣayatayā sarvabhāvasyāsiddhatvāt tajjñāpanāya sarvajñatva iti vyākhyātam । tena sūtre vastūnāmityantarbhāvasambandhijñāpakaṃ padamadhyāhāryamiti sūcitaṃ bhavati । asya hetorasambhavādityanuvṛttahetudvārā madhvādiṣu anadhikāraṃ manyata iti pūrveṇānvayaḥ । anena madhvādiṣvityādiśabdena mokṣārthavidyā api grāhyāḥ । jyotiśśabdaśca āvartanīyaḥ jyotiṣīva jyotiṣīti । saptamī ca caitrarathasya buddhau śāstrārtha itivat yujyate iti sūcitam । kathaṃ vastūnāṃ jñāne antarbhāva ityataḥ sarvajñatve bhāvāditi svapade varṇayati āditya iti । sarvavastūnāmādityaprakāśe antarbhāvavat tadgṛhītatvavat tajjñāne taduparīti prastutadevatākartṛkajñāne sarvavastūnām aantarbhāvāt'; viṣayībhūtatvādityarthaḥ । abhiprāyaṃ vyanakti nityeti । devānāṃ sārvajñena avidyānāṃ'; sarvabrahmakarmavidyāsādhyajñānānāṃ anityasiddhatvāt'; niyamena prāptatvādityarthaḥ । yadvā avidyānāṃ'; jñānasādhanavidyānāṃ nityaṃ niyamena asiddhatvāt'; upalabdhatvādityarthaḥ । devānāṃ vedadraṣṭṛtvāditi bhāvaḥ । yadvā avidyānāṃ'; mokṣataditaraphalasādhanajñānasādhanavidyoktārthānāṃ anityasiddhatvāt'; niyamena tairjñātatvādityarthaḥ । tathā ca na devānāmubhayavidyāsādhyajñāne arthitā sambhavatīti bhāvaḥ । anayorapi pañcamyantayoḥ pūrvavadanvayaḥ । na cāsya hetoḥ pūrvasūtroktāsambhavahetūpapādakatvāt kathamatra caśabda iti vācyam । pūrvaṃ phalamukhena atra ca sādhanamukhena arthitvāsambhavasya abhipretatvena asya hetordvitīyāsambhavopapādakatve api asambhavasāmānye upapādakatvena caśabdopapatteḥ । yadyapi bhāṣye ajyotiṣi'; iti sūtraṃ kiṃ devānāṃ mokṣetaraphalārthāyām? uta mokṣaphalārthāyāṃ vidyāyāmadhikāra iti pakṣadvaye api sādhānamukhena doṣoktiparatayā pratīyate । ṭīkāyāṃ tu mokṣārthavidyāyāmapi na devānāmadhikāraḥ, tatra phale arthitāsattve api tatsādhanavidyopāsanātmakajñāne arthitvābhāvāt, vidyāyāśca jñānārthatvāt, jñānasya ca prāptatvāditi dvitīyapakṣamātradoṣoktiparatayā vyākhyātam । tathā ca visaṃvādo bhavati । tathāpi mokṣetaraphalakavidyāsvanadhikāra iti prācīnapakṣe na kevalaṃ madhuvidyāphale vasutvādau prāptatvāt devānāmarthitvābhāvāt tadvidyāyāmadhikārābhāvo doṣaḥ । kintu vasutvādiphalasādhanajñāne apyarthitvābhāvāt adhikārābhāva ityasambhavadoṣe upapādakāntaramuktaṃ bhavatīti ṭīkāyāmuktatvānna visaṃvādaḥ । ata eva na caśabdānupapattiḥ । prācīnapakṣavivakṣayā tadupapatteḥ । hetvantareṇa etatsādhayatīti sattarkadīpāvalī ca ādyapakṣavivakṣayā pravṛttā । dvividhavidyāsamuccaye vā caśabdaḥ । anena na kevalaṃ mokṣetaraphalārthaṃ madhvādiṣvanadhikāraṃ manyate jaiminiḥ । kintu ādiśabdena vā āvṛttajyotiśśabdena vā gṛhītāyāṃ asatyaṃ jñānam'; iti mokṣārthavidyāyāmapi । kutaḥ? ajyotiṣīva'; ādityaprakāśe iva ajyotiṣi'; sarvaviṣayakadevatājñāne sarvavastūnāṃ viṣayatayā abhāvāt'; mokṣasādhanajñānasya siddhatvāt । ata eva na mokṣe, tasyāpi siddhaprāyatvādarthitvāsambhavāt । na kevalaṃ vasvādidevānāṃ phale arthitvābhāvāt madhvādiṣvanadhikāraṃ jaiminirmanyate, kintu ajyotiṣi'; vasutvādiphalasādhanajñāne apyarthitvāsambhavāt । so api kutaḥ? ajyotiṣi'; devānāṃ jñāne abhāvāt'; sarveṣāṃ vastūnāṃ viṣayatayā antarbhāvātphalasādhanajñānasya siddhatvāditi yāvaditi vā sūtrārtha ukto bhavati ।

sū oṃ ।
bhāvaṃ tu bādarāyaṇo asti hi ।
।
phalaviśeṣabhāvātprāptapadānāmapi devānāṃ madhvādiṣvapyadhikāraṃ bādarāyaṇo manyante । asti hi prakāśaviśeṣaḥ ।
evaṃ devairmokṣetarayogyaphalānāṃ prāptatvāt ayogyānāṃ prāptumaśakyatvāt mokṣasyāpi brahmajñānitvena arthato labdhatvādarthitvābhāvena teṣāṃ kāsvapi vidyāsu adhikārābhāve jaiminimatāvalambinā samarthite punaradhikāraṃ samarthayatsūtraṃ paṭhitvā vyācaṣṭe bhāvamiti । phalaviśeṣabhāvādityanena sūtre pūrvasmādbhāvādityasya anuvṛttiḥ sūcitā । prāptapadānāmiti । padyata iti padaṃ prāpyaphalamātram । apītyanena viśeṣārtho api । apiśca yadyapi tathāpītyarthe ityuktaṃ bhavati । devānāmiti sūtre śeṣoktiḥ । madhvādiṣvityanuvṛttapadānuvādaḥ । atra ādiśabdena mokṣataditaraphalārthāśeṣabrahmakarmavidyā gṛhyante । aadhikāram'; adhikārabhāvamiti । anena abhāvam'; ityasyārtha uktaḥ । manyata iti śeṣoktiḥ । astītyasya kartṛsāpekṣatvāt taṃ darśayati prakāśaviśeṣa iti । jñānātiśaya ityarthaḥ । hiśabdo yata ityarthe । tathā cetthaṃ yojanā bādarāyaṇastu bhagavān devānāṃ madhvādyaśeṣavidyāsu adhikārabhāvaṃ manyate । na ca prāptaphalatvāttatra arthitvābhāvo doṣaḥ । yadyapi devāḥ prāptapadāḥ brahmajñānitvātsiddhamokṣataditaraphalāḥ prāptumaśakyāyogyaphalāśca । tathāpi prāptapadānāmapi devānāṃ madhvādividyāsūktopāsanākarmakaraṇābhyāṃ phalaviśeṣabhāvātsvasvayogyasya jñānamātreṇa asādhyasya mokṣaphale atiśayasya bhāvāt siddherarthitvasambhavāt । na ca phale atiśayasya siddhatvena tatrārthitvasambhave api tatsādhanavidyānāṃ nityasiddhatvāt vidyāvicārasya jñānārthatvāt tatrārthitvāsambhava iti vācyam । ahi'; yato bhagavaditareṣāṃ nirupacaritasārvajñābhāvāt vidyāvicāreṇa aprakāśaviśeṣaḥ'; jñānaviśeṣaḥ aasti'; sambhavatīti । anena sūtravṛttirdarśitā । atra bādarāyaṇapadaṃ pūjārtham ।

yāvatsevā pare tattve tāvatsukhaviśeṣatā ।
sambhavācca prakāśasya paramekamṛte harim ।
teṣāṃ sāmarthyayogācca devānāmapyupāsanām ।
sarvaṃ vidhīyate nityaṃ sarvayajñādikarma ca ।
nanu tattadvidyoktopāsanakarmakaraṇābhyāṃ tattadvidyoktaphalādanyadapi phalaṃ prakāśaviśeṣaśca devānāṃ bhavatītyetat kuto jñāyate ityāśaṅkāṃ parihartumuktārthe hiśabdasūcitāṃ smṛtiṃ darśayati yāvaditi । svārthe tal । bhāvabhavitrorabhedavivakṣayā vā । siddhyatyasyeti śeṣaḥ । yadvā ādyaścaḥ prakāśasya ceti sambadhyate । phalasamuccāyakaścāyam, asambhavasamuccaye ca । sambhavādityāvartate । tathā ca apare tattve'; paramātmasvarūpe aasau vā ādityaḥ'; ityādinokte tadviṣaye adevānāṃ'; devairvasvādibhiḥ ayāvat'; yāvadadhikaṃ asevā'; aeṣā sevā'; ityuktā śravaṇādirūpopāsanā kriyate atāvat'; tāvadadhikaṃ teṣāṃ asukhaviśeṣatā'; svargāpavargādisukhe atiśayaḥ svasvayogyo jñānamātreṇa sādhyaḥ siddhyati । yato ataḥ aparaṃ'; svatantraṃ harimekamṛte anyeṣāṃ aprakāśasyāsambhavāt'; nirupacaritasārvajñyābhāvāt । ata eva vidyāvicāreṇa sādhyasya prakāśasya jñānaviśeṣasya sambhavāt, ata evārthitvasya sambhavātteṣāṃ devānāṃ asāmarthyayogāt'; sāmarthyasambhavācca vidvattāsambhavāccāpi prāptapadānāmapi adevānāṃ'; devaiḥ asarvamupāsanaṃ'; sarvavidyoktopāsanaṃ sarvayajñādikarma ca anityaṃ'; niyamena avidhīyate'; śrutiṣu kartavyatvena bodhyata iti yojanā । caḥ samuccaye । aprakāśasyeti pāṭhe nirupacaritasārvajñyābhāvasyetyarthaḥ । tadā prakāśasya caśabdena grahaṇam । sambhavādityasya siddhatvāt sattvādityarthadvayam । pāṭhadvaye apyanyeṣāmiti śeṣaḥ । ekaśabdo avadhāraṇārtho viriñcasyāpi varjyatvanivārakaḥ skānde uktamiti śeṣaḥ । ataḥ phalaviśeṣabhāvādasti hi prakāśaviśeṣa ityanayornāsiddhiriti vākyaśeṣaḥ ।

uktaphalānadhikāramātraṃ jaiminimatamato na tanmatavirodhaḥ ।
nanvastvevamasambhavādityuktayuktiparābhavaḥ । tathāpi devānāmadhikārābhyupagatāvāptatamajaiminimatavirodha ityata āha ukteti ।। uktaṃ ca tat phalaṃ ca uktaṃ phalaṃ yasyeti ca vigrahaḥ । tathā ca tattadvidyoktaphalārthaṃ tatphalakaprāgāptajñānārthaṃ ca yo ayamadhikārastadabhāvamātraṃ ajaiminimatam'; jaiminyabhimatamityarthaḥ । mātraśabdena phalāntarārthādhikārābhāvo vyāvartyate । kimato yadyevamityata āha ata iti jaiminyuktasya sūtrakāreṇāpyaṅgīkṛtatvāt, sūtrakṛduktasya ca jaimininā anirastatvānna tayorvirodhaḥ ityarthaḥ ।

sarvajñasyaiva kṛṣṇasya tvekadeśavicintitam ।
svīkṛtya munayo brūyustanmataṃ na virudhyate ।
iti brāhme ।
। iti devatādhikaraṇam । ।
nanu kimanayormatayorviṣayavailakṣaṇyakalpanena virodha eva kiṃ na syādityata āha sarvajñasyeti । tuśabdo viśeṣārthaḥ । evakāro bhinnakramaḥ । tathā ca yasmāt amunayo'; jaiminyādyāḥ nirupacaritasarvajñasya akṛṣṇasya'; dvaipāyanasya aekadeśavicintitaṃ'; vicintitārthaikadeśaṃ tanmataikadeśameva svīkṛtya tadeva brūyuḥ, nānyat । tasmāt atanmataṃ'; teṣāṃ kṛṣṇamunīnāṃ mataṃ parasparaṃ na viruddhyata ityarthaḥ । brāhma ityanantaraṃ uktamiti śeṣaḥ । ato viṣayavailakṣaṇyameva kalpyaṃna matavirodha iti bhāvaḥ ।।
। iti devatādhikaraṇam ।

। apaśūdrādhikaraṇam ।
manuṣyādhikāratvādityukte aviśeṣācchūdrasyāpi aahaṃ hāretvā śūdra'; iti pautrāyaṇokteradhikāra iti ।
atrādhikaraṇe trivarṇetarasya śūdrasya vedoktabrahmavidyādhikāro nirākriyate । prāsaṅgikatvāt nādhyāyādisaṅgatiranveṣaṇīyā । śrutyādisaṅgatiṃ viṣayādikaṃ ca sūcayati manuṣyeti । adhikāropayogitayokte manuṣyatve aviśeṣāditi vā । na kevalaṃ dvijātīnāṃ, kintu śūdrasyāpītyaperthaḥ । tathā ca śūdrasyāpi vedavidyādhikāraḥ prāpnoti । kutaḥ? amanuṣyādhikāratvāt'; ityanena manuṣyāṇāmadhikārasyoktatvāt । adhikāropayogitayokte manuṣyatve ca śūdrasya dvijātibhyaḥ aaviśeṣāt'; viśeṣābhāvāt । nanu na manuṣyatvaṃ vedavidyādhikāropayogi, kintu viśiṣṭabudhyādimattvamevetyato apyāha aviśeṣāditi । śūdrasya viśiṣṭabuddhyādimattve api anyebhyaḥ aaviśeṣāt'; viśeṣābhāvādityarthaḥ । evamaviśeṣākhyayuktimabhidhāya śūdrasya vedavidyādhikārādarśanāt, anadhikāra ityato liṅgadarśanamāha pautrāyaṇokteriti । chāndogye pautrāyaṇasya vaidikasaṃvargavidyādhyayanokterdarśanādityarthaḥ । nanu pautrāyaṇākhyapuruṣasya śūdratvameva kuta ityataḥ tajjñāpakamāha aha hāretvā śūdreti । pautrāyaṇokteriti ।
pautrāyaṇaṃ prati raikkoktestatkartṛkasambodhanādevetyarthaḥ । nanvadhikārābhāve api pautrāyaṇo vedavidyāṃ vicārayāmāseti kiṃ na syādityatopyāha pautrāyaṇokteriti । pautrāyaṇaṃ prati raikkeṇa nispṛheṇa muninā saṃvargavidyopadeśādityarthaḥ । anadhikāriṇaṃ prati munerupadeśāsambhavāt । pautrāyaṇasya arthācchrutāvadhikārokteśceti vā yojanā । adhikāra ityanantaramato virodha ityanukṛṣyate । tasyokta ityanenānvayaḥ । anenoktanyāyena uktārthe śrutyādipramāṇavirodhākṣepāt pūrveṇāsyākṣepikī saṅgatiḥ, vedavidyādhikārākhyo viṣayaḥ, sayuktikapūrvapakṣaśca darśito bhavati ।
